Version 7.3 Release Notes 7.3.498.097

Click 7.3 Recent Updates and Enhancements for a brief synopsis of recent changes to this version (see page 107 of the printed notes, or jump to page 121 in the Adobe .pdf reader).

1 System

Important Installation Note: The zip file for this release includes a file containing all bitmap definitions in the image (master~pushbuttons.obj) and an executable image (v.exe) stripped of all bitmaps. The bitmaps will be loaded when a user logs on from the master~pushbuttons.obj file and the SKIN1 directory (if bitmap skinning is in effect). Running this release requires the presence of the change.log, recover.log and master~pushbuttons.obj files in the same directory as the image (v.exe) file. This configuration should allow XP users to run without ‘non-continuable protection fault errors’.

1.1 Updated/New Reports

This release corrects a System Primitive Failure error that occurred with saving some reports as .CSV files.

This release corrects a recent problem with drilldown reports which used hidden fields to pass values to component reports; the hidden field information was not being passed correctly. This fix is in SAM Pro, not the individual Drill Down reports.

1.1.1     Service Invoice Report (SERVICEINVOICEv73b032.rpt)

A Note on Report Naming:
The version and build number of the first Version/Build a report is valid for will now be appended to the filename of the user reports generated and update by our Data-Basics report writers. Note that is NOT necessary to change the filename before imported the report into a database: SAM Pro will use the internal Report Id and Name when updating / adding the report.

07/12/2010

An option to show Service Invoice detail info by Equipment is now available.

A recent tax change in Canada has resulted in some users having to change the Tax Authority in the WO Sales Tax tab. In the version of the Service Invoice Report dated July 12, 2010, this has been corrected so that the Service Invoice used the tax authority information on the WO tax tab to display the tax information correctly on the invoice.

08/06/2010
Enhancement to auto-saving service invoices:

The system now writes the Invoice # and date to the document Description.
PM Invoices now reference the PM Invoice Workorder in the Document record.
Auto-saved Service Invoices now also attach to the Client Site.

10/05/2010

Fix needed for Batch Service Compute of COD work orders.

11/30/2010

If the Billing Address Id is completed in the Work Order, the billing address for the Service Invoice and Worksheet come from this field. If the Override Client Id (see user note 11.1.10) is completed, but the Billing Address Id is not, the billing address for the Service Invoice and Worksheet come from the Override Client record.

Updated reports are required to support this functionality:

SERVICEWORKSHEETv73b032.rpt

SERVICEINVOICEv73b032.rpt

08/29/2011

Supports expanded Material, Other and Sub quantity fields of up to 99.999.99; previously, quantities were limited to 9,999.99.

2/13/2012

Certain custom formats specify that the work requested is suppressed. Previously, if work orders using these formats were included in a batch service compute run with (for example) FORMAT_11 formats, the work requested suppression was not turned off for the FORMAT_11 work orders, resulting in the Work Requested not printing when it should. The service invoice (serviceinvoicev73b032.rpt) dated 2/13/2011 or later corrects this problem at both the work order and equipment levels.

 

1.1.2 Service Worksheet Report (SERVICEWORKSHEET.rpt)

New validation ensures that template-type clients are only billed when the net invoice amount is exactly ZERO DOLLARS. The Service Billing Worksheet report has been modified to display a very noticeable warning for each WO/Job invoice that would result in a template-type client being billed for any amount other than zero. The Service Worksheet report SERVICEWORKSHEETv73b032.rpt dated 11/22/2011must be imported to support this functionality.

This release also corrects a problem with auto-saving service worksheets. The registry entry sys-report-serviceworksheet must include the following registry option:

Key Setting: AutoSaveWhenPrinted Key Value: true

This registry must also include the applicable autosavefilename, autosavedirectory, and autosavebysection entries.

1.1.3 Service Invoice Post Report (SERVICEINVOICEPOST.rpt)

The Service Invoice Post Report was updated on August 19, 2010 to support multiple payment lines for COD invoices.

1.1.4 Sales Summary by Sales Rep (rslssmmryslsrp.rpt)

This report lists Sales and Quota information for your Sales Reps for the selected month (current and previous year), as well as year to date figures for the current and previous sales year. See user note 5.3 for details. This report must be installed in your database.

1.1.5 Updated Construction Invoices

(Requires rininv4.rpt and rininv3.rpt dated 08/04/2010)
When auto-saving invoices, the system now writes the Invoice # and date to the document Description.

1.1.6 Report PR 941 Quarterly Summary (RPR941S.rpt)

The Report PR 941 Quarterly Summary (RPR941S.rpt) was updated on August 13, 2010 to provide a better input document for the Federal form and on January 5, 2011 to support the change in employee/employer social security taxes.

Changes to the Report Range Screen:

In the earlier report, the report range screen provided input fields for Prior Quarters Federal Tax Adjustment and Total Deposits for Quarter. In the updated report, these fields have been lumped together in the input field (11) Total Deposits, including Prior Quarter Overpayments.

FICA Sick Pay Adjustment has been relabeled as (7b) FICA Sick Pay Adjustment.

FICA Other Pay Adjustment has been relabeled as (7c) FICA Other Pay Adjustment.

Advanced EIC Payments has been relabeled as (9) Advanced EIC Payments.

Additions to the Report Range Screen:

(5b) Social Security Tips
SAM Pro does not track Social Security Tips. This data entry field may be completed by the user if Social Security Tips should be reported.

(6a) Number of Qualified Employees First Paid Exempt Wages this Quarter
(6b) Number of Qualified Employees Paid Exempt Wages this Quarter
(6c) Exempt wages/tips paid to qualified employees this Quarter
SAM Pro does not track this information. These data fields should be completed by the user if exempt wages were paid to qualified employees this quarter / first paid this quarter.

(12a) COBRA Premium Assistance Payments:
(12b) Number of Individuals Provided COBRA:
SAM Pro does not track this information. These data fields should be completed by the user if COBRA assistance was provided this quarter.

1.1.7 Drill Down Job Unbilled Cost Summary (DJBUBCS.rpt)

New Option: Include Closed Jobs?
The report DJBUBCS (Job Unbilled Cost Summary) excludes closed jobs.  However, Job EOM processing does not exclude these jobs.  The option to include closed jobs and mirror more closely what will happen in the Job EOM posting has been added to the report DJBUBCS.rpt as of 8/17/2010. This report works with SAM Pro Version 7.0 and up.

1.1.8 Report AIA Construction Inventory Report (RAIA.rpt)

This report was updated on August 4, 2010 to support sectionkeyvalue for naming the saved report and document archiving (attaching the various versions of the report to the Client, Client Site, Job and Invoice Master records). This report may be used in Version 7.0 and up. Note that the appropriate registry options (see below) must be implemented, as well as the updated report being installed.

Id: sys-report-raia_owner (also needed for architect and cm)

Setting Key: autosavebysection  Setting Value: true

Setting Key: autosavefilename  Setting Value: name,^sectionkeyvalue^

You may use some or all of the parameters in this option. If more than one is used, parameters should be separated by commas. name should be replaced a short description of the report (Invoice or AIAInvoice).

The system will replace ^sectionkeyvalue^ with the invoice number. Note that if you use this parameter you must also specify the autosavebysection=true option.

Other Recommended options:

Setting Key: bitmap   Setting Value: \\sharepath\standard_construction_owner.bmp

Setting Key: sectionbackerbitmap  Setting Value:\\sharepath\standard_construction_continuation.bmp

Setting Key: autosavewhenprinted  Setting Value: true

Setting Key: autosaveoverwrite  Setting Value: true

Setting Key: autosavedirectory  Setting Value: path (to appropriate directory)

1.1.9 Report Inventory Audit Report (RINVNTRYADT.rpt)

This report was updated to compensate for PO’s received to jobs/work orders on September 1, 2010.

1.1.10 Report AR Drill Down Detail (CARAGE1.rpt)

This report was updated on September 16, 2010 so that tax is no longer included in the total line’s profit amount and profit percentage. The Total line is now labeled to indicate that it does not include taxes.

1.1.11 Drill Down AP Aging Report

Enhanced Reports with Date Received (DAVAGE.rpt, CAPVAGE1.rpt and CAPVAGE2.rpt)

These reports are version 7.30, and must be dated 11/18/2010 or higher.

The Drill Down AP Aging report has been enhanced so that it may be aged by the Vendor’s Invoice Date (its current behavior), or the new Date Received field in the AP Journal. Note that if the Date Received field is blank, the date will be understood as 1900-01-01 and the amounts will appear in the 90+ Days aging column.

Revised Report: Aging by Vendor (DAPVAGEv73b033.rpt):

This release / report enhancement adds new temp table logic to resolve out of memory errors that some users experienced when working with large databases. Note that this version of the report (dated 2/28/2011) should only be used with 7.3.493.033 and up.

The updated report (DAPVAGEv73b033.rpt dated 2/28/2012) corrects a problem that only occurred if you ran this report with the Invoice Detail option set to Yes. Previously, this resulted in the associated drill-down displaying the incorrect Vendor Name; this has been corrected.

1.1.12 Updated Report: Report PR Certified Payroll Report (RPRCRPR.rpt)

Report Dated 11/12/2010

New Report Field: Classification

If this line was entered for a Prevailing Wages Job, this field will default from the new Certified PR Report Label field on the Job Prevailing Wages tab. If the Certified PR Report Label field on the Job Prevailing Wages tab is blank, or this line is not for a Prevailing Wages job, the field defaults from the Labor Rate Description.

1.1.13 Client Profitability Report – Version 7.0 and Up

This report (DCPFTR.rpt) now skips entries with Client Rn = 0. Note that its component reports (CCPFTR1.rpt, CCPFTR2.rpt & CCPFTR3.rpt) should be updated for Version 7.0 (these reports are dated 10/8/2009) or an error may occur with certain settings.

The Service Account Manager from the Client Site has been added to the Drilldown Client Profitability report as a range field. Both the DCPRTR.rpt (dated 6/10/2011) and the CCPRTR1.rpt (dated 6/13/2011) must be installed to support this functionality.

1.1.14 Unvouchered AP Summary Report (12/3/2010) – Version 7.0 and Up

This version of the Unvouchered AP Summary Report (RUNVCHRDAP3.rpt) corrects a typo in the GL Entity field.

1.1.15 Reports for US Payroll Tax Reporting

Payroll Employee Tax Table Report (12/28/2010)

This report (RPREMTX.rpt) enables the user to print the contents of the Employee Record Tax tab; it is useful to confirm data entry, and may also be run to verify that the both the FICA SS and FICA SSER tables are correctly specified in all applicable Employee records. We recommend that you filter on the Tax Tables beginning with FICA (FICA%) or FICA SS (FICA SS%) to make the report easier to review.

The Employee Date Termination Range can be set to the blank date (1900-01-01) to display only those employees who have not been terminated. To include employees who have not been terminated, or will be terminated after 2010, the Employee Date Terminated Range may be set as follows: sql=(emplye_dte_trmntd='1900-01-01' or emplye_dte_trmntd>='2011-01-01’)

Report PR Federal Fax Report (RPRTAXF.rpt) (01/05/2011)

Report PR 941 Quarterly Summary (RPR941S.rpt) (01/05/2011)

Report W2 Electronic File (RW2EF.rpt) (02/21/2012)

These reports should be installed to support Payroll Tax Reporting in 2011 (with the different employee / employer tax for Social Security.

In this version, a registry entry is now required to set Position 174 on the RE line as the default has been changed to blank to accommodate special processing for the state of Maryland. The following option is now required for federal processing with this report.

Id: sys-w2-ef

Setting Key: reEmployerKind    Setting Value: N

This entry is REQUIRED for federal processing; the value will default to blank if no entry is made.

Most companies will use a Setting Value of N; if your organization is tax exempt or a government agency, see the following for other options:

F – Federal Government

S- State and Local Government

T – Tax exempt Employer

Y – State and Local Tax Exempt Employer

N – None Apply

The Audit Report option of Report W2 Electronic File (report RW2EF.rpt dated 2/21/2012) has been modified so that the totals row is offset so that larger payroll amounts do not overlap. This change impacts the Audit option only. This report is suitable for version 7.2 and up.

1.1.16 Revised Report AR Aging (DARAGE.rpt)

This drill-down report has been revised as of 3/9/2011 to better handle unapplied cash receipts.

1.1.17 Revised Report PR Local Tax Report – RPRTAXL.rpt (3/4/2011) – version 7.0 and up

Corrects a ‘Table #lcltx not found’ error’ when run for a tax authority with no activity for the given time period. In the 3/4/2011 revision, if no activity is found, the report is displayed with the header only and no data.

1.1.18 Revised Report Quote (RQTEFRM.rpt)

3/29/2011

Includes a new checkbox, Omit Declined Options. When flagged, Declined scope options will not appear in the printed Quote and Quote total. A registry may be used to flag the Omit Declined Options box (default is for the box to be clear to preserve current behavior); see user note 2.25 for details.

4/22/2011

Expands the Extended Price fields to support options of up to $9,999,999.99. Note that the Quote Total also supports this value.

6/20/2011

The quantity fields which show on the quote have been changed to only display 2 decimal places to be consistent with the labor detail lines.

8/29/2011

The Estimated Tax for Fixed Price Scopes will be displayed when the Print Estimated Tax box is flagged.

This report adds the ability to expand the printing of Scope Of Services by adding Notes attached to the Quote record via the sidebar Notes button. To enable this feature, The Notes Summary field must contain the Option Code. If the system locates the appropriate Notes records, their text will be printed following the Scope of Services text for that option. Up to 60 lines of 80 characters each are supported. If the Notes text is longer than 80 characters, the system will automatically wrap the text to the next lines when it is printed on the quote. If the Notes text exceeds the report limit, it will be truncated. Note that this field will not be split between pages.

1.1.19 Quote Recap (RQTERCP.rpt)

The revision dated 4/22/2011 expands the Extended Price fields to support options of up to $9,999,999.99. Note that the Quote Total also supports this value.

1.1.20 Report Service PM Agreement Summary Report (RPMAGRMNT.rpt)

New Option: Use Job Open Date?
The revision dated 8/22/2011 includes this new option. Checking this box will restrict the report to only include history that is greater than or equal to the Job’s Date Open. Default is unchecked (the original way the report ran); all history would be included.

Report Description:

The report is sorted by Asset Id. The following information is listed for each Asset if the Job Details box is flagged – it the box is not flagged, the Job Detail will not be displayed:

Asset Id: Asset Name:

Earned Revenue
Other Rate Id Date WO Id Job Id Cost Code Cost Cat Revenue Dollars Quantity Billed

Overhead Costs

Date Vendor/Employee Inv#/Labor Jrnl Cost Code Cost Cat Cost

Asset Profitability:

Asset Cost/Hour:

Total Profitability:

Report Range Screen:

Beginning Date: Ending Date:
These fields specify the time frame used to compute the profitability. At least the Ending Date must be completed. Only Assets with Revenue and or Costing history within this date range will be listed on the report.

Show Job Details?
If you flag this box, the Job and Cost Code will be shown on the Earned Revenue portion of the report.

Asset Id:
Asset Type:
These range fields may be used to limit the Assets displayed on the report. If these ranges are empty, all Assets with activity in the period defined by the Beginning and Ending Dates will appear on the report.
