1.1.23 Report Customer Statement (RCUSTSTMNT.rpt)

This report now supports auto-emailing in the Customer Statements report (RCUSTSTMNT.rpt) dated 8/30/2011 or later. If an e-mail address exists in the Client Collections Email Address field, a copy of their section of the report will be emailed to that address. In addition to installing the updated report, the following registry options must be added to the sys-report-rcuststmnt registry to enable this behavior.

Setting Key: emailbysection Setting Value: true

Setting Key: autoemail Setting Value: true

 

1.2 Viewers (General)

This release eliminates a sporadic problem where the Change Record message displayed twice when leaving a record without saving your changes.

This release corrects a problem where the wrong sidebar appeared when the Refresh button was clicked in the Client Site Equipment and Job Billing Item viewers

This release extends the ability to successfully create a named range to history viewers opened at the filter screen.

In previous releases, the mouse over box drawn around bitmaps was not always removed when the mouse was quickly run over a series of buttons. This problem has been corrected so that these “leftover” boxes no longer appear when the mouse has moved off of the button.

More efficient/quicker right-click open of viewers implemented.

When typing in a multiple line text box with only one line showing, pressing Enter once again adds a carriage return instead of moving the cursor to the next field.

This release corrects a Field Size error that only occurred if the user saved a record while a push button on one of the child lines in the record was in mouse over mode.

This release corrects a spurious invalid id error that occurred when an Id of the maximum field size is typed in and the user presses the Enter key to advance to the next field.

This release corrects a display issue that occurred if Windows Clear Text is enabled: field labels would display bolder when the screen was repainted after selecting an Id. In this version, SAM Pro handles Clear Text so that labels will be displayed correctly.

This release corrects a display problem that occurred if you used Ctrl+Z (or the View menu option) to Zoom while in Single View, and then clicked the Lines View button. Note that the user is not permitted to access Single View (with the Magnify button) while in Zoomed mode.

This release corrects the horizontal placement of bitmaps in the top button bar.

The user will now be notified if an attempt to create a duplicate entry fails. For example, if the database is structured properly, there is a UNIQUE CONSTRAINT such that a technician cannot be scheduled on the same date and work order more than once. Previously, the duplicate line would not be added, but the user would not be notified. In this release, the error is reported to the user.

This release corrects sporadic problems where the screen would erroneously autoscroll when you clicked into a field (e.g., in the AP Journal, the upper pane would auto-scroll when you tabbed into the Account Period field under some screen resolutions).

When the Refresh button was clicked, certain fields (such as the Work Order’s AR Term Code on the COD tab) were not reloaded from current data. All fields are now reloaded when Refresh is clicked.

The system now prevents unnecessary 'Change Record?' prompts associated with starter-type functions such as Start Create PM Work Orders.

Validation in Phone / Fax Number Fields
The software now validates that phone numbers only contain numeric digits when the user attempts to exit the field; this addresses the problem of users inadvertently pasting letters into phone numbers.

In some instances, the switch from the lines view to the single/detail view generated an error that appeared to be data related but was really a timing problem. This has been corrected.

1.2.1 Child Tab Detail / Single View Enhancements:

This release adds functionality to the Single (detail) View of child tab lines that are accessed via the Magnify button.

The Magnify button (used to zoom in on the Single/Detail view of lines) has been updated to help users distinguish between zooming in on a particular line, and searching for an Id (in the case of Id Search (discuss below). In addition, the Magnify button now responds to a single click – in previous release, it was necessary to double-click it.

New Buttons:

This release adds graphical buttons to the Single (detail) View of child tab lines that are accessed via the Magnify button. The following buttons enable the user to scroll though the lines in this child tab:

First – Previous – Next – Last line in the tab

In addition, Add, Insert and Delete lines buttons have been added to enable this functionality in the Single (detail) view line screens.

Clicking the Lines View button will return the tab to its initial, multiple line view.

Child Lines – Odd / Even Color:

Child tab lines are now displayed using the Odd / Even color scheme selected by the user with the Set Color button. The selected line will be displayed in the Background color selected by the user with the Set Color button.

1.2.2 Top Button Bar

Some buttons have been re-arranged so that the Exit button is always the right-most button. The Alarm Board button has been moved the second row of the top button bar.

1.2.3 New Windows Pulldown Menu

A new pulldown menu labeled ‘Windows’ has been added to SAM Pro windows.  It can be used as an additional tool to navigate within SAMPRO to currently open SAM Pro windows (for records, starter functions, and reports) by simply selecting an entry on the Windows list.

1.2.4 Status Pane

This release includes updates to the text that is displayed in the status pane at the very bottom of the SAM Pro window when the user places the mouse cursor over a button. A registry entry is also available to adjust the status line’s height, foreground color, background color and font. You may use the security option of this entry to help remind multiple security users how they are logged in. See user note 2.27 for details.

1.2.5 Id Search Buttons

This enhancement enables the addition of the Id Lookup button to the right-hand side of Id fields. This enhancement lets the user easily see which fields are Id fields, and also select the field AND bring up the list in a single click of the button. See user note 2.8.9 for details on enabling this option.

This functionality has been expanded to support disabled fields. If a field is disabled, the grayed out version of the Id Search button will be displayed, and the user will not be able to access the field by clicking on the button.

1.2.6 Side Button Bar

The Delete Record button no longer appears on the Side Button bar. To delete a record, the user may 1) Access the menu bar to select Record>>Delete Record or 2) Use the keyboard equivalent Ctrl+d to delete the record.

This release corrects a problem where the Add record button was not grayed out when a new record was added.

1.2.7 Calendar and Clock

Updated buttons that are easier to read on high-resolution monitors have been added to the following screens:

Clock: Increment/Decrement Minutes/Hours -

Calendar: Previous/Next Month -

1.2.8 Record Validation

WO Inventory (and other journals): This release implements enhanced journal validation logic to prevent sporadic posting reversals with inappropriate Transaction Ids. If this situation is about to occur, the erroneous reversal is suppressed AND an error is written to the error log noting the reversal suppression.

Additional validations have been added to alert a user when they are in danger of exiting a record without saving it.

When you access another record by entering its ID directly into the field at the top of the viewer, the system will now display the following message if any unsaved changes are detected in the original record:

Warning: the changes made to record ‘original record id’ were not saved.

Do you wish to return to ‘original record id’ to save your changes?

If you click Yes, the original record id will be restored. At this point, you should save the record before accessing a different record or cloning a new one.

If you click No, your changes to the original record will be discarded, and the record whose id you entered will be displayed.

This release also adds validation when precisely one field (not the record’s Id field) is changed without tabbing out of it. The system now displays the Change Record message in this circumstance when you do one of the following:

Click the List button and select another record

Click the Close (X) button

Click the Record Up or Down button

1.2.9 List Highlight Colors

In previous versions, the highlight color for lists (including new call and the dispatch board) was a bright blue. In Version 7.3, the highlight was changed to a dark gray for better readability. In response to user comments, this highlight color has been changed back to blue.

1.2.10 Bitmap ‘Skinning’

Version 7.3 supports a new and brighter look for SAM Pro via bitmap ‘skinning’ of the top and side button bars. These newer bitmaps are also designed to display more clearly on today’s high-resolution monitors. To implement this look requires a few simple registry settings and the set of SKIN1 bitmaps from Data-Basics. If you have been using SAM Pro for many years, this may feel like a big change, but once you start using the new bitmaps you will be surprised by how quickly you adapt to and enjoy using them. See user note 2.32 for details on configuring your system to run with these new skins. A PowerPoint entitled Graphical User Enhancements provides additional details on installing and using this enhancement; contact your support representative for details.

1.2.11 Notes

If a user (who was not a notes administrator) accessed a private note created by someone else, and then attempted to change it, the message “you cannot change the record because the change button is disabled” would appear and the user would be unable to exit SAM Pro correctly. In this release, the message appears, but the user is allowed to leave the notes viewer.

1.2.12 New Help Menu Option - SQL History:

There may be times when your support representative needs to see the SQL generated by certain actions: the SQL History option has been added to the Help menu to enable this.

To capture SQL History:

Select Help > SQL History. This menu provides three options: Capture SQL History, View SQLHistory and Clear SQL History. If a check mark does not yet appear next to Capture SQL History select this option to turn this feature on. Next, perform the steps that your support representation tells you.

To View SQL History:

Use the menu option Help>SQL History>View SQL History

A workspace window will appear with the SQL history that has been logged. In the workspace with, select File > Save As. A browser window will appear: browse to a location you will be able to retrieve the file from, and save it using a appropriate name.

To Clear SQL History:

The Help>Clear SQL History option may be used to clear SQL history before making another test.

To Turn Off SQL History:

It a check mark appears next to the Capture SQL History menu option, is it toggled on. To toggle Capture SQL History off, select Help>SQL History> Capture SQL History. Note that even if you do not explicitly turn this feature off, it will be disabled when you log off.

1.2.13 Type-Ahead/Autosearch Enhancement

The 'Type-Ahead' feature allows the user to position the caret to a specific row of a list just by typing the first few characters of the desired row. In previous versions, this only worked only on first column of the list. This release extends this functionality so that it works on whatever the column the cursor is positioned in IF the target column has been pre-sorted in ascending order by clicking the column header of the desired column.

For example:

  1) the user sorts column three in ascending order
  2) the user positions the cursor at the first character in column three
  3) the user types the characters b, o, and b.
  4) the cursor will automatically positioned on the forth character of the first line having column three beginning with 'bob'.

 

1.3 Viewer Filtering

1.3.1 Additional Filters Added to the AP Journal, Bank Transfer, and Checklist Viewers

Bank Transfer: GL Bank Account

AP Journal: EFT/Credit Trx: Id and Payment Type (Check, EFT or Credit) filters

Check Viewer: EFT/Credit Trx: Id and Payment Type (Check, EFT or Credit) filters

1.3.2 Special Filtering for Encapsulated GL Accounts

Special Filtering for encapsulated GL Accounts has been added to the AP Journal, AR Cash Receipts Journal, AR Sales Journal, Bank Deposit and Bank Reconciliation Journals. Since multiple GL accounts are present in the ‘parent’ tables of the several of the Journals, simple range filters (where you simply enter the GL Account Id) do not work for these "encapsulated" fields. To enable the user to filter on a specific parent GL Account, special filter ranges with the necessary SQL to filter on a specific GL Account have been added to following Journals:

AP Journal: GL AP Control Account and GL Bank Account filters 

AR Cash Receipts Journal: GL Bank Account filter

AR Sales Journal: GL AR Control Account and GL Bank Account (for COD Cash Receipts) filters

Bank Deposit: GL Bank Account and GL Sweep Account Filters

Bank Reconciliation Journal: GL Bank Account, GL Fees Account and GL Interest Account filters

Example on Using Filters for Encapsulated Fields: Bank Reconciliation Journal

Range filters for the GL Bank Account Id:, GL Fees Account Id: and GL Interest Account Id: have been added to the range filter screen. When the range filter is initially displayed, the GL Bank Account range appears as follows:

GL Bank Account Id:
sql= gl_bnk_glaccnt_rn in (select glaccnt_rn from glaccnt where glaccnt_id like '%')

Suppose that your firm uses more than one Bank Account. To filter on Bank Reconciliation Entries for a specific GL Bank Account, simply replace the % in the SQL statement with the GL Bank Account Id you wish to filter on. For example, to filter on the GL Bank Account Id 1005, simply change the SQL statement in the range to:

sql= gl_bnk_glaccnt_rn in (select glaccnt_rn from glaccnt where glaccnt_id like '1005')

Tip: Saving Ranges

Rather than adjust the SQL statement each time you use the filter, you may save your settings as a range. To do so:

1. Complete all range fields as desired.

2. Select a Filter Key (in the upper left-hand portion of the range screen) to control the sort order of the records that you are filtering on.

3. Click the Save Range button.

A box will appear requesting that you enter the name of the range to save. Type in a descriptive range name – begin the name with an asterisk it you want all users to be able to select the range. In our Bank Reconciliation example, this might be *Bank Account 1005

4. Click the OK button. Your custom range will be listed in the Filter Ranges pane. When you access this range viewer in the future, you can select a saved range by clicking on it in the Filter Ranges pane.

1.4 Login

The size of the user login window has been made slightly larger to accommodate small screens with high resolutions.

1.5 Document Management / Archiving

Updated buttons (easier to read on high-resolution monitors) have been added to the Document Viewer:

The Archive File Location and Type fields in the Document Record are now successfully completed during the scanning process.

SAM Pro no longer assumes that the user included a file extension in the original file name. This corrects a problem encountered during the TechAnywhere post.

The View Documents filter now includes ranges for Table Name, Reference Id and Reference Name.

A sort option has been added to the Document viewer (as accessed from View Document, not a record’s attachments). The new option is DocumentByReferenceId, with the columns:

 Reference Id-Reference Name-Category-Description-Date Logged-Document Id

This release also corrects a system primitive error that occurred in View Documents if you changed the sort order in the KeyNames pane and then clicked the Create .PDF button. The Create PDF button now supports use with archived documents tagged as ‘Read Only’.

1.5.1 Automatic Attachments to additional tables

This enhancement allows the user to specify attachments to other tables in the record when attaching or scanning a new document from the viewer (functionality that Quick Attach already provides). See user note 2.26 for the registry option to do so.

1.6 Saving Report Files as .csv

This release corrects an issue that only occurred if the user’s Windows folder settings were set to hide extensions for known file types; the file was not assigned a file extension. In this release, the filename extension is now correctly set to .csv.

1.7 Menu Option to Specify Windows to be Opened when User Logs In

A new option has been added to the File menu: Save Viewer Attributes. This menu option may be used with or without the registry option that sets the default window size and position (see user note 1.7.1 below).

When you select this option from a viewer, the Select Viewer Attributes to Save box will appear. It has two check boxes:

Save Size/Position?

If you check this box, the next time this viewer is opened, will be displayed as it is now. For example, if you have a very wide monitor, you might like to have your Folders viewer on the left side of the screen, and your Labor Journal on the right. To do so, you would position these viewers as desired, select File=>Save Viewer Attributes, and check the Save Size/Position box, and then click OK. In this example, you would repeat this process twice – once for the Folders Viewer and again for the Labor Journal. If you are doing so for the Notes viewer, you must log off and on again to see the results.

Open during login?

If this box is checked, this viewer will be open during the login process. It is recommended that you only check this box for viewers you have open every day.

Tip: Undoing Viewer Attributes
To undo Viewer Attributes, select File=>Set Viewer Attributes, clear the check boxes, and click OK.

Tip: Resetting Viewer Attributes
To reset Viewer Attributes, first select File=>Set Viewer Attributes, clear the check boxes, and click OK. Next, reset them by selecting File=>Set Viewer Attributes, and checking the appropriate boxes.

1.7.1 Registry to Control Initial Home Position and Size of Open Windows

This functionality applies to record Viewers, most initial Starter screens, and Report ranges. The size and position settings in this registry will be overridden is the user has individually set the size and positions via the File menu: Save Viewer Attributes functionality.

Id: sys-screen

Note that this setting may be customized by user with the sys-screen-branchid-userid or sys-screen- - userid formats.

Setting Key: nomaximize Setting Value: true

(default is false: all record viewers are maximized when initially opened)

Setting Key: topleftratio Setting Value: x@y

‘at’ allows you to specify the initial location of the top left corner of the SAM Pro window (as a percentage of the screen) of the upper left corner of the image. For example, the setting value 10@5 moves set the initial open location to the right by 10% of the screen width, and down by 5% of the screen height.

Setting Key: sizeratio Setting Value: x@y

‘at’ allows you to specify the initial size of the SAM Pro window (as a percentage of the screen). For example, the setting value 40@60 sets the initial open size to forty percent of the screen’s width and 60% of its height. This might be an appropriate setting if you have a very large monitor (e.g., 1900 x 1080, for example).

1.8 Document viewer

Filter Screen: if the user double-clicks on the Reference Id range, the system will alert the user that the Reference Id must be entered manually instead of displaying an error message.

Document References Tab: if the user double-clicks on the Reference Id field without first entering a valid Table Name, the system will alert the user that the Table Name field must be completed first.

1.9 Zip Code Lookup

Back in Version 6.2, the ability to set related fields from the Zipcode table was implemented via registry (sys-zipcode-lookup was required). At some point, the software stopped recognizing the registry, and always defaulted from the zipcode table. This was a problem because you could not turn the functionality off – for example, to prevent the Branch Id from defaulting when a new Vendor record was created.

In this release, the registry functionality has been restored. What this means, however, is that if the registry is not in place, defaulting from the zipcode table will no longer work. Check that your database includes the appropriate registry if you wish the zipcode table fields to default; see user note 2.14 for details.

1.10 Preview Reports

This release corrects a spurious error in recent releases that occurred when moving the mouse over a report preview screen.

This release corrects problems that occurred if the user clicked on the Preview Report option of the report range viewer and selected HTML or Text: selecting the Text option resulted in an error, selecting the HTML option did not generate an error but did not open the IE browser.

Important Note:

For the HTLM option to work correctly, the system must be aware of the path to the IE Browser. Right click your Internet Explorer Icon select properties. The target line has the Directory Path of Internet Explorer.

Add/Change the line in registry sys-ffv-global-settings

Setting Key: iebrowserpath  Setting Value: path

Note: make sure to use the Directory Path Only.

Example:

Setting Key: iebrowserpath Setting Value: C:\Program Files\Internet Explorer

Correction to Documentation:

The documentation for the browserpath was incorrect in previous versions of Help. It was incorrectly specified as registry id iebrowserpath and path=... as an option instead of the sys-ffv-global-setting noted above.

1.11 Custom Index (new record)

Purpose:

Based on their analysis, database administrators may identify and implement custom indexes (in addition to those maintained by SAM Pro) which enhance a particular system’s performance. Until this release, these custom indexes had to be re-implemented after each database conversion. This enhancement enables the DBAs or system administrators to store custom indexes within their data. The next time the database conversion is triggered (when updating to a new version), the SAM Pro software will automatically install all active Custom Indexes (not flagged as Obsolete).

Usage:

It is the responsibility of the user to configure the SQL correctly for their particular database. It is recommended that this viewer only be available to DBA/System level personnel.

Important Buttons:

Click this button to create this Custom Index within your database. Note that this record must be saved first.

Click this button to drop this Custom Index.

Important Fields:

Custom Index Id:
This field must uniquely identify this record.

Index Name:
This field should have some relationship to its function. It SHOULD NOT include blanks as it will be referenced in the SQL Create String field. If its function is not obvious, consider using the Notes or Attachment features to add additional documentation.

Table Name:
Double-click on this field to select the table the index should be applied to.

SQL Create String:
This field must reference the exact Index Name noted in this record. The table referenced in the Create String must reference the internal database name, NOT the one selected in the Table Name field.

Sybase Example:

Custom Index Id: GLH01

Index Name: GLHistoryByDateEffective

Table Name: GLHistory

SQL Create String: Create Index GLHistoryByDateEffective on glhstry (glhstry_dte_effctve)

SQL Server Example:

Custom Index Id: GLH01

Index Name: GLHistoryByGLAccountRn

Table Name: GLHistory

SQL Create String: CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX GLHistoryByGLAccountRn

on glhstry (glaccnt_rn)

INCLUDE (glentty_rn, glhstry_amnt_dbt, glhstry_amnt_crdt)

 

1.12 Message Table Purge/Archive

A new Starter function, Start Message Table Purge, has been added to the system to clean up the Message table (used by TechAnywhere, SaqeQuest, FMMS, etc.) and improve the performance of the Work Order TechAnywhere tab. By default, this function will purge / archive all Posted messages that are 60+ days old. Unless disabled via registry, these messages will be archived to the new mssgearcve table.

When this function is selected, it runs without further user input. The intention is that this purge/archive can be run unattended (like the other purge/archive functions) as a Scheduled Event.

1.12.1 Registry Entry to Control Purge Message Table

Id: sys-start-sprgemssgetble

Setting Key: DaysToKeep Setting Value: Number of days   Default 60

Setting Key: DisableArchive Setting Value: true          Default false

This registry option allows you to disable archiving of purged messages to the mssgearcve table. If these options are enabled, the purged messages will be deleted, and will no longer be available for inspection in your database.

1.13 Accounting Period

New Field: Work Order Other to GL:
In previous releases, the GL was never impacted from Work Order Other tab entries. In this release, the Work Order Other tab will write to GL if this field is flagged.

Note: the sys-viewer-vwrkordr registry option RestrictWOOthercost should NOT be set to true if this option is enabled.

See user note 19.6 for additional information on using this feature in conjunction with the expensing of company assets.

See user note 2.15 for a registry option to control the use of this new option.

1.14 Start Report Import - Report Import Checklist

New Fields:

CaseNo:
This field displays the internal Case Number (if completed) from the report that is being imported.

First Version No:
This field displays the First Version Number (if completed) from the report that is being imported. This is the first SAM Pro version number the report should be used with.

Install Version:
This field displays the First Version Number (if completed) of the report that is currently installed in the system. This field will display as ‘Not Installed’ if this report is not already in the database, or Unknown if the First Version Number is not completed in the installed report.

Custom For:
This field displays the Custom For field (if completed) from the report that is being imported.

Changed Field:
Do:

The system will consider the contents of the First Version No:. Install Version:, and the version of SAM Pro itself when determining whether or not to flag a report for import. A report will be flagged for import if its First Version Number is the highest allowable for the SAM Pro version running.

The import will not check the Do box for any reports with Unknown status for the first or installed version number.

1.15 Database Conversion

This release corrects an error encountered when logging out after a database conversion.

This release implements incremental commits when creating Foreign Keys and Indexes during SQL server conversions.

1.16 Printer List

Users with a very large number of printers may have found some missing from SAM Pro’s list of printers because the allowable number of characters for all the printers’ names was exceeded. The allowable number of characters has been expanded from 6000 to 10,000 characters to correct this problem.

1.17 SAM Pro Services

Previously, if an error occurred during startup of a Sampro service, the image was left running in the background using up RAM. The image is now successfully closed preventing this memory leak.

1.18 Wheel Mouse Users

This release prevents “Key is missing” errors and other undesirable results if the user scrolls their Wheel Mouse while waiting for the Service Invoice (and other reports) to display.

1.19 End Key

The End Key now positions the cursor correctly (at the end for the text) in Id-type fields when the Id Search/Lookup buttons are turned on. In multi-line textbox fields with word wrap, Ctrl-End now also works correctly if the text includes an embedded blank line, positioning the cursor at the end of all the lines of text.

1.20 User Viewer – Registry Tab

This release implements the use of the Registry tab in the User Viewer to add / override sys-ffv-global-settings for this User. Since these settings are loaded when the user logs on, he or she must log on after User Registry changes are made to see them in effect.

1.21 Email (SMTP)

This release adds a 'Date:' header line to email messages to support email servers that require it. An updated version of the XmlToPdf.jar file is included in the zip file for this release that also supports the Date header line for emails with .PDF attachments sent from SAM Pro.

The system now correctly handles the case of a message containing a line consisting solely of a period.

1.22 Startme.exe

This release includes a new startme.exe file. When the first user (of a particular OS) accesses a new image, the underscore version of the v.exe runtime will be generated with the user’s OS designation. For example, if you have XP and Windows 7 users, you would expect to see two runtime images:

V_2011_9_16_12_13__18_[Microsoft_Windows_XP].exe and

V_2011_9_16_12_13__18_[Microsoft_Windows_7_Professional].exe

XP users will be directed to the XP runtime, and Windows 7 Professional users will be access the Windows 7 runtime.

1.23 History Table Viewers

In this release, History record viewers will start at the Range screen to avoid the unnecessary load time need to display the entire list of entries. In previous releases, the registry entry sys-startscreen-filter was required to implement this functionality.

1.24 VM Memory

SAM Pro’s Smalltalk virtual memory has been expanded to 250MB from 150MB. This should better support the running of extremely long reports and the unfiltered display of large record viewers without encountering out of memory errors.

 

2. Registry Entries

2.0 Registry Viewer

When a Registry record containing an option that is flagged as Multiple Settings (e.g., some sys-printer-W2 records) is loaded into the viewer, the option will be ‘exploded’ so that each setting now as its own Setting Key/Setting Value line. Disabled lines are excluded from this enhancement.

2.1 Job (sys-viewer-vjb)

2.1.1 Registry Option to Set Effective Date of Budget Tab Entries to the Job Open Date

By default the effective date of Budget Entries posted to Job History via the Budget tab is set to blank (1900-01-01). This could cause issues when compiling a WIP summary report.  For example, suppose the user runs a WIP summary report for say 03/31/2010, and then places new jobs in service in April.  If the user must re-run the report for the end of March (03/31/2010) the totals will change (using the budgets from Job Viewer) whereas, using the Job Journal or if the budgets had a date they would have remained consistent. 

The following registry option causes entries from the Job’s and the Project Manager Workbench’s Budget tab to use the Date Opened from the Job record for both forwarding and reversing entries:

Setting Key: BudgetEffectiveDate Setting Value: DateOpened

Note on Existing Data: when implementing this registry, you may wish to update the Job History Budget entries generated by the Job Budget tab to correspond to the Job’s Date Opened. An SQL script for this purpose may be run to update your data: contact your support representative for details.

2.2 AP Checks (sys-report-rapchck)

2.2.1 MICR Support for multiple bank accounts

With this enhancement, the AP Check Entry Fields GL Account and GL Entity are used to look up the registry. If none found the default is used (sys-report-rapchck). In this way you can assign different MICR values to each GL Account/Entity group.

Id:  sys-report-rapchck-GLACCTID-GLENTTYID

sys-report-rapchck-GLACCTID

2.3 Quote Viewer (sys-viewer-vqte)

This release corrects a display issue encountered when clicking the filter button.

2.3.1 Registry Option to ‘Pop’ Site Notes without Prompting the User

When you begin to add a Quote in Quote Master, the system will now ask if you wish to view the Notes associated with the Site you selected (either directly or by choosing a source Work Order). The following registry options may be used to alter this behavior:

Id: sys-viewer-vqte

Setting Key: SiteNotesNoPrompt Setting Value: true

This entry changes the default behavior of Quote Master – which is to prompt the user to view any notes that are associated with the selected Client Site when a new Quote is being created. If you implement this option, Quote Master will automatically display the list of notes with a Client Site is selected (either directly or by choosing a source Work Order).

2.3.2 Registry Option to Suppress Site Notes when Creating a Quote

Id: sys-viewer-vqte

Setting Key: nonotes Setting Value: true

This entry changes the default behavior of Quote Master and suppresses the display of Site Notes when a Quote is being created. This restores the behavior present in version 7.2 and earlier.

2.3.3 Flat Rate Import Tax Rules

By default, the Flat Rate Import code forces each line's Tax Type Id to 'n/a' instead of applying normal SAMPRO tax rules. The following registry setting may be used to use the Job’s tax rules when setting the Tax Type.

Registry Id: sys-viewer-vqte

Setting Key: ApplyTaxRulesOnFlatRateImport Setting Value: true

2.3.4 Allow Changes to Accepted Options

In an earlier release, validation was added to disallow changes to any scope lines if the status is set Printed, Accepted, Approved or Declined, forcing the user to first change the status to Open to make changes. Changes to Labor, Inventory, Material, Other and Subcontractor lines were only allowed if the associated Scope Option was set to Open.

The validation associated with Accepted options has resulted in procedural issues for some of our customers. For this reason, the following registry setting may be implemented to allow changes to Accepted options on the Scope tab, and also to Labor, Inventory, Material, Other and Subcontractor lines associated with Accepted Scope Options.

Note: this registry option should be used with caution if CRMAnywhere is enabled; options that a customer has accepted should not be altered.

Setting Key: IgnoreAcceptedValidation Setting Value: true (default is false)

 

2.4 Work Order Viewer (sys-viewer-vwrkordr)

2.4.1 Disable Remote Tech Warning

By default, the software displays a warning message if the work order has at least one open assignment to a Remote Tech.  The following registry setting disables the warning.

Setting Key: DisableRemoteTechWarning Setting Value: true

2.4.2 Credit PO Handling

One of the major differences between regular and credit POs is the posting of the Quantity Ordered and Quantity Received values.  On a credit PO, the Quantity Received is ignored and the Quantity Ordered is used in its place.  For example, on a regular PO the Quantity Received is posted to IMH as Quantity On-hand and to JCH as Actual Quantity.  For credit POs, the on-hand and actual quantities are derived from the Quantity Ordered.

Some customers may wish to use Quantity Received as an indicator that the vendor has actually credited them for the returned items rather than whether the Credit PO is vouchered.  By their definition, an open credit PO is one where the Quantity Received is less than the Quantity Ordered on one or more lines.  The following registry entry changes the definition for open Credit PO’s to be those where the Quantity Received is less then Quantity Ordered:

Setting Key: CreditPOsMustBeReceived Setting Value: true

The default value is false so as to preserve existing behavior. 

2.4.3 Default Quantity and Date if Inventory Item Entered first

When this option is implemented, and a new WO-INV line is started and the Inventory Item Id is entered before the Date and Quantity fields, default the Actual Quantity to 1; default the Bill Quantity to 1; and default the Date to the current system date.

Setting Key: EnableCase3571  Setting Value: true

This option should NOT be used with the DefaultLineDateFromDateWorkCompleted=true option. If both options are set, the WO Date Work Completed is set, when you enter the Inventory Id first, the Effective Date is set to the Date Work Completed, but the quantity is not defaulted to 1.

2.4.4 Disable Posting of Budget Cost and Revenue of PM Work Orders

This registry option, when implemented, will disable the posting of job history of budget cost and budget revenue for Preventive Maintenance work orders where the work order lines are marked QU and the work order is set to Ready to Invoice. This option would be enabled if a customer wishes to enter manual budgets for PM work. Note that this option only impacts the processing of Work Order Type PreventiveMaint

Setting Key: PostQuotesToJCHBudgets Setting Value: false

2.4.5 Other Rate Filtering

Implementing this registry option filters the Other Rates displayed on the list view to those referenced in the Job’s Rate Schedule when the user double-clicks the Other Rate Id on the Work Order’s Other tab.

Setting Key: FilterOtherRatesByJobRateSchedule Setting Value: true

2.4.6 Allow Changes to Revenue Adjustments on PM Invoice Work Orders

When the work order's Work Type is 'PM Invoice', changes are no longer allowed by default on the Revenue Adjustments tab.  This includes line inserts and deletes.

The previous behavior (to allow changes) can be restored with the following registry setting:

Setting Key: PreventRevenueAdjustmentAccessOnPMInvoices Setting Value: false (default true)

2.4.7 WO Inventory / IM History Alert:

This entry validates that the total cost and quantity entered directly on the tab matches the total cost and quantity what have already been or will be posted to Inventory history when the Work Order is saved. If a discrepancy is found, a TabHistoryMismatch alert box will appear, and the work order will not be saved. The tab mismatch information is written to the error log. This alert should only appear if erroneous reversal history was previously written to Inventory History – a sporadic issue in previous images. It is only recommended for users who are concerned with tightening up inventory, and are willing to have support correct issues before work orders can be edited/invoiced. To implement this option:

Setting Key: TabMismatchINV-IMH Setting Value: enabled

If this option is not implemented this alert will not be raised.

 

2.5 Sagequest (sys-mapping-sagequest)

Id: sys-mapping-sagequest   

2.5.1 Treat Listed Technicians as Unassigned

Sometimes users create "fictitious" techs to use as place holders for unassigned work orders. For example, users put a tech called PM on their D-Boards and park the PM Work Orders there for later assignment. Since the tech "PM" isn't a valid SageQuest driver the work order wouldn't show on the SageQuest map. This registry setting will cause any tech listed to be handled just like the work order had no tech assigned to it. Since SageQuest displays unassigned work orders, these work orders would show up with a blank tech id.

This registry option will allow a user to specify a list of tech id's that SageQuest will treat the same as it treats un-assigned work orders.

Setting Key: TreatAsUnassignedTech  Setting Value: list of techs

Example:

Setting Key: TreatAsUnassignedTech Setting Value: PM

2.5A Specify Initial Starter Function Registry Settings (sys-start-sfunctionid)

The software now supports general functionality to allow the user to specify the initial value for Starter function inputs.

Setting Key: InitialValueFor~fieldId Setting Value: fieldvalue

Note that ”fieldId” is displayed on the start input screen when you lay your cursor over it. For boolean fields (check boxes), the field value of true is for checked, and false is for blank. Note that ^today^ is supported as a token initial value.

Example: Start Material Requisitioning – set the Date as Of field to today, and the Work Order Type field to exclude Preventive Maintenance work orders.

Id: sys-start-smtrlrqstnng

Setting Key: initialValueFor~dte-as-if   Setting Value: ^today^

Setting Key: initialValueFor~wrkordr.type Setting Value: !PreventiveMaint

2.6 Reporting – general registry entry (sys-report-functionid)

2.6.1 Specify Initial Default Report Settings

The software now supports general functionality for registry entries for reports which will allow for the default setting for Settings and Range type fields to be specified.

Setting Key: InitialValueFor~fieldId Setting Value: fieldvalue

Note that ”fieldId” is display on the report screen when you lay your cursor over it. For boolean fields (check boxes), the field value of true is for checked, and false is for blank.

Example: enable the Estimated Sales Tax box on the updated Quote Form report

Id: sys-report-rqtefrm

Setting Key: initialValueFor~p_shw_estmtd_tx  Setting Value: true

2.6.2 Auto-emailing: Do Not Email User Running Report if Report Section lacks a Recipient Email Address

By default, if the User's email is completed in the User's Contact Record AND the appropriate Email To address is blank (for example, the Email Invoice Address (or Billing Address Id) in the Job is blank for service invoices), the invoice is sent to the User's Email Address in the Contact record. This may be undesirable. The following registry setting applies to auto-emailing in general and may be implemented on a report by report basis to disable the emailing of a report section when the section does NOT have a recipient email address available.

Setting Key: SkipEmailNoAddress Setting Value: Y (default is N)

2.6.3 Option to prevent Zero Dollar Service Invoice

This option applies specifically to Service Invoicing and can be used to prevent the emailing of zero-dollar invoices.

Id: sys-report-serviceinvoice 

Setting Key: SkipEmailZeroInvoice Setting Value: Y (default is N)

2.6.4 Validate that Report is Printed before E-mail is Allowed / Disallow Email

Two new registry entries can be implemented for reports that have a ‘did this report print successfully’ confirmation box, such as the Purchase Order and Service Invoice.

Id: sys-report-functionid

Setting Key: OkToEmail Setting Value=false (default is true)

This setting will permanently disable the SendEmail button.

Setting Key: OkToEmailWithoutPrint Setting Value: false (default is true) 

If this option is set to false, the Email button will be disabled (grayed-out) when the report is first displayed. The button will be enabled only when the report has been printed.

Example: Purchase Order Control

If a Purchase Order is not linked to a Quote, the Vendor may be changed if items have not been received AND the PO had not been printed. Some users were completing a Purchase Order, emailing it to the Vendor, and then changing the Vendor on it. Implementing the following registry forces the Purchase Order to be printed before it can be e-mailed. Since the Vendor cannot be changed on a Printed Purchase Order, this entry effectively stops the undesirable practice of ‘reusing’ Purchase Orders.

Id: sys-report-rpofrm

Setting Key: OkToEmailWithoutPrint Setting Value: false 

2.7 Dispatch Board Registry Options (sys-viewer-vdsptchbrd)

Id: sys-viewer-vdsptchbrd

2.7.1 Dispatch Board Available Hours Tab

This option may be implemented to allow the user-definable setting for Available Hours. By default, Available Hours are set to 8.

Setting Key: availableHoursPerDay Setting Value: ##.## (enter a decimal number with 2 places)

Example:

Setting Key: availableHoursPerDay Setting Value: 10.50

2.8 Global Settings Registry Entries (sys-ffv-global-settings)

Important Note - User Viewer: Registry Tab
This release implements the use of the Registry tab in the User Viewer to add / override sys-ffv-global-settings for an individual User. Since these settings are loaded when the user logs on, he or she must log on after User Registry changes are made to see them in effect.

Id: sys-ffv-global-settings

2.8.1 Price Code Handling Option– always default Price Code Level 1 Price

This registry entry impacts the Work Order, Quote, Client Order, and CSRAnywhere (Quote Management). Note that the Inventory Item allows for 10 levels of Material Pricing, but Price Codes only allow for 5.

Setting Key: DefaultExceptionPriceCodeLevel1  Setting Value: true

When this option is enabled, and the system defaults inventory unit pricing and there is a Price Code in play, the system ignores the Price Level found in the Client Site or Job and assumes price level 1 of the Price Code. This setting impacts the Work Order, Quote, Client Order, and CSRAnywhere (Quote Management).

The default (if this option is NOT implemented) and Price Codes are in effect, and the default price level from the Client Site or Job is greater than 5, the system now defaults price level 1 from the Price Code. If the default Price Level (in the Site or Job) is 5 or less, the corresponding Price Code Price will be used.

2.8.2 Journals – Do not Default in Equipment Id if Work Order Id is selected – (restore default behavior)

The Equipment Id field now appears after the Work Order Id in the AP, Job, Labor and Purchase Order detail tabs. When the user enters a Work Order Id in any of these tabs, the new default behavior is for the Equipment on the first line of the Work Order’s Equipment tab to default in The following registry option may be used to disable this behavior so that the Equipment Id does NOT default in.

Id: sys-ffv-global-settings

Setting Key: DefaultEquipmentFromWorkOrder

Setting Value: false

The default is True.  When not True, don't default in the Equipment Id. 

Note: If the sys-ffv-global setting 'DefaultEquipmentFromWorkorder' is set to false, the user is now allowed to set the Equipment Id back to blank in the Labor, PO and AP Journals. If this registry option is not present or set to true, the Equipment Id must be completed if a Work Order Id is referenced.

2.8.3 Required Resources – registry entry to enable Vendor defaulting

Currently, the default Vendor (in the inventory item record) does not default when you enter a Required Resource line manually or as a result of generating a PM Work Order with flagged parts - the idea being that aggregation will be used. Customers that wish to generate individual po's for the work orders required resources (using the mat req button in the work order) must individually set the Vendor Id in each line.

The following registry entry changes this behavior so that the system will default in the Vendor Id from the Inventory record (if set) on manual Work Order Required Resource entries and on Create PM Workorders.

Setting Key: DefaultRequiredResourceVendorFromInventory Setting Value: true (default is false)

2.8.4 Specify Maximum Wait Time when Create PDF Button is Clicked

This release corrects the File Creation error sporadically experienced when using the Create PDF button in the Documents viewer or the View Files button in the Start AP Payment Approved List function waiting up to 30 seconding before the time out error is generated.

The user may also make a new entry in sys-ffv-global-settings to increase the maximum wait time if the default 30 seconds is not enough.

Setting Key: MakePDFTimeOut

Setting Value: (an integer value represented in milliseconds 60000=60 secs)

2.8.5 Internet Explorer Browser Path

This release corrects problems that occurred if the user clicked on the Preview Report option of the report range viewer and selected HTML or Text: selecting the Text option resulted in an error, selecting the HTML option did not generate an error but did not open the IE browser.

Important Note:

For the HTLM option to work correctly, the system must be aware of the path to the IE Browser. Right click your Internet Explorer Icon select properties. The target line has the Directory Path of Internet Explorer.

Add/Change the line in registry sys-ffv-global-settings

Setting Key: iebrowserpath  Setting Value: path

Note: make sure to use the Directory Path Only.

Example:

Setting Key: iebrowserpath Setting Value: C:\Program Files\Internet Explorer

Correction to Documentation:

The documentation for the browserpath was incorrect in previous versions of Help. It was incorrectly specified as registry id iebrowserpath and path=... as an option instead of the sys-ffv-global-setting noted above.

2.8.6 Inventory Average Cost Calculation

By default, if an Inventory Item is flagged as using Average Cost, the system will make the following attempts to determine the cost if the first option (average cost of that inventory on-hand at the specified location) is not available:

1. Average from Inventory History (constrained by Where)

2. Average from Inventory History (not constrained by Where)

3. Standard from Inventory Item [unless the RevenueFromStandardCost registry option is enabled]

4. Last from Inventory History (constrained by Where)

5. Last from the Inventory Item

This calculation may be quite time-consuming, and may not be the preferred methodology for all installation. The following registry entry allows the user to only make the first calculation. If there is no stock on-hand for the specified location / serial number, the cost will be zero.

Setting Key: InventoryItemAverageCostByLocationOnly Setting Value: true

This registry impacts certain reports and the following screens:

Work Order Inventory Tab

Start Work Order Entry

Inventory Item: parent tab, Locations and BOM Tabs

Purchase Order Inventory Tab

Inventory Receipts Journal Receipts Tab

Accounts Payable Journal Inventory Tab

Shop Order” Main and BOM Tab

Job Journal Expenses tab

2.8.7 Specify Standard Annual Hours for Salaried Employees

By default, the system uses the value of 2080 for the annual standard hours (for salaried employees) used for various payroll reporting calculations (such as Report PR Verification) run before (or in lieu of) Compute Payroll. This enhancement allows the user to control the Standard Annual Hours via registry or in the Employee viewer so that the pay rate written to job history will use the ‘correct’ rate (Salary / Standard Hours) without having to run Compute Payroll to have the pay rate updated to the correct effective rate (= Salary / Pay Periods / Hours Entered).

Setting Key: StandardAnnualHours  Setting Value: NNNN

Where NNNN is replaced by the number of Standard Annual Hours that your firm wishes to use. This value will be used for all employee payroll calculations unless overridden by the Annual Hours field in the Employee viewer.

Tip: if all employees are to use the same standard annual hours (either the default 2080, or as set by global registry) you may wish to disable this field so that it is not erroneously completed. Contact your support representative for details.

2.8.8 Deny Change / Delete to Notes Unless User is a Notes Administrator

This enhancement Implements a global registry setting that prevents non-administrator users from changing or deleting Notes records.  When this setting is ON, only a Notes Administrator account can change and delete public or private notes.

Setting Key: NoteChangeDeleteRequiresAdministrator Setting Value: true

Rules for Note Record change and delete actions are as follows ...

A Notes Administrator can change/delete all but 'secure' notes. Only a support representative can delete or change secure notes.

If the original author is not a Notes administrator, they can change/delete their own private and all public notes except when the new registry setting is in place.

2.8.9 Enable Id Search Buttons

This enhancement enables the addition of the Id Lookup button to the right-hand side of Id fields. This enhancement lets the user easily see which fields are Id fields, and also select the field AND bring up the list in a single click of the button.

The Magnify button (used to zoom in on the Single/Detail view of lines) has been updated to help users distinguish between zooming in on a particular line, and searching for an Id (in the case of Id Search.

Setting Key: UseIdSearchButtons Setting Value: true

When this registry option is implemented, the Id Search button is automatically added to the right-hand side of most Id-type fields. Certain Id fields (especially very short ones) are excepted from this behavior.

When the Id Search button is pushed, the system:

Changes the focus to the associated Id input field.
Emulates the left mouse-button double-click logic to display the list of Id’s for this field

2.8.10 Registry Entry for Job Costing Fringe Burden

Using this option brings the Job History computation in line with the computation used in the GL History. This is important if your firm is not using Data-Basics Payroll module, but still desires to job cost estimated fringes and also accrue these to the general ledger.

Setting Key: LaborJobCostRateMethod Setting Value: BurdenOnWagesOnly

Background:

An Earnings ID for a burden (type marked N/A) is setup. This Earnings record is marked Accrue (Yes) and JobCost Labor Entry (Yes).

There can be 2 different types of burden Fixed (hourly) and Flexible (percent of wages).

When this registry is set the percentage is only taken on Earnings flagged as “Wages”. The default was adding “Wages” and Fixed Burden and then calculating the percentage on these.

WARNING ON USING THIS PROCESS:

Regardless of whether this registry option is enabled, GL will post on Labor Entry:

 DR COGS LABOR Wages

  CR Accrued wages payable

Also

 DR COGS Fringes

  CR Applied Fringes

Job Cost will post on Labor Entry:

The Total Amount as one number STORING a single COST CATEGORY (selected on labor line).

The problem arises at month-end during the WIP process if these costs are unbilled. The month-end process will:

 DR WIP

  CR COGS LABOR Wages

COGS LABOR Wages will be understated and COGS fringes will be overstated.

2.8.11 Global Registry Entry to Default PM Billing GL Accounts

Setting Key: DefaultGLAccountPMIncome Setting Value: GL Account Id

Setting Key: DefaultGLAccountPMBilledInAdvance Setting Value: GL Account Id

This option provides default GL Accounts for the system to use if the corresponding fields on the Client Site PM Billing tab are blank (or are not specified in Master Contract) when Start Create PM Billing is run. One or both should be completed as follows:

If Amortizing the Amount Earned on a Billing Schedule

The Setting Value for the DefaultGLAccountPMIncome option should specify the Income (sales or revenue) account where the Amount Earned will post. This Account will be credited with the Amount Earned when the Start Create PM Invoice function is run.

The Setting Value for the DefaultGLAccountPMBilledInAdvance should specify the Liability (unearned income) account where the Amount Billed will post. This Account will be credited with the Amount Billed when PM invoices are generated, printed, and posted.

If Not Amortizing the Amount Earned on a billing schedule

The Setting Value for the DefaultGLAccountPMIncome option should specify the Income (sales or revenue) account where the Amount Billed will post. This Account will be credited with the Amount Billed when PM invoices are generated, printed, and posted. The second GL Account field should not be completed.

2.8.12 Option to Define Statuses to Release to Tech

Setting Key: TechReleaseFromStatuses Setting Value: list of from statuses (default is Pending)

By default, clicking the Release to Tech button changes the status of the selected Technician line from ‘Pending’ to the application status for the Technician (most likely Unacknowledged). This enhancement allows the customization of the release to tech button located on the dispatch board and the workorder technician line to specify the "from" status (statuses) so that they no longer are forced to used just the status of "Pending". The "to" status will continue to follow the same rules as it always has.

Example: Setting Key: TechReleaseFromStatuses Setting Value: pending, waitcustapprvl

2.8.13 Update Work Order Escalation Status in absence of Escalation Profile

In the past, the WO Escalation status was only updated if an Escalation Profile existed in the system. For a variety of reasons (including invoicing and credit hold processing), the WO Escalation status/Status Category should be updated for all systems. The following registry option results in the work order escalation status always being updated, regardless of whether or not an Escalation Profile exists.

Setting Key: EscalationManager Setting Value: always

 

2.9 TechAnywhere Registry Options

Id: sys-techanywhere

2.9.1 Do Not Post COD Work Orders to AR Sales / Cash Receipts

A new registry Item has been added to allow COD-type work orders to be invoiced from SAM Pro instead of occurring as part of the TechAnywhere post. This allows the back office staff to review the Tech Anywhere COD Invoices before posting to AR.

Setting Key: AutoPostCOD Setting Value: false or true

The default is true. If the option is absent or set to true, the current default is retained: the post will create an Invoice, AR Sales Journal, and Cash Receipt.

When the Setting Value is false, the behavior is completely changed. An invoice master record is still created, but now left at the status of New, and no AR Sales Journal or Cash Receipt is created. All imported lines come in without an AR invoice reference ID so that they can be billed normally via Service Compute. AR entries can then be created through SAMPro.

2.9.2 Adjust Default Date or Accounting Period

Inventory from TechAnywhere can be posted to the default accounting period, even if the effective date is outside of the period range. However, a problem occurs when the user attempts to bill the WO and encounters an error indicating that the effective date was out of period range. A registry entry is now available to adjust either the date or accounting period to keep them in sync. 

When the defaulted Date and Accounting Period are NOT out-of-sync, NO adjustments are made to the defaulted values.  The rules noted below are used only when an adjustment is necessary.

Setting Key: AdjustDefaultDateOrPeriod Setting Value: period or date

If period is selected, the Accounting Period table is queried for eligible Accounting Periods.  To qualify, the period must be Active and its date range must include the defaulted Effective Date.  When multiple periods are eligible, the one with the smallest Period Id is chosen to become the new Accounting Period for the current transaction.  If no eligible period is found, nothing is changed.

If date is selected, the Effective Date is adjusted to be either the Start Date or the End Date of the defaulted Accounting Period.  The Start Date is chosen when the current date is less than the Start Date.  The End Date is chosen when the current date is greater than the End Date.

NOTE: the current TechAnywhere post behavior does not change unless the new registry setting is turned on. 

 

2.10 New Call Registry Options (sys-newcall)

Id: sys-newcall

Setting Key: PromptPrintNewWO    Setting Value: true or false
Setting Key: PromptViewNewWO   Setting Value: true or false
Setting Key: PromptViewNewWOWorkCodes  Setting Value: list of work codes to view

PromptPrintNewWO defaults to True to retain the existing behavior.  If set to False, it eliminates the 'Print Work Order?' prompt that currently pops up after creating a new work order.

PromptViewNewWO defaults to False.  When set to True, a new prompt appears after creating a new work order giving the user the opportunity to launch the Work Order viewer with the new work order already loaded.

PromptViewNewWOWorkCodes lets you specify the new work orders to view by work code; overrides PromptViewNewWO.

2.11 Create PM WOs (sys-start-scrtepmwo)

Id: sys-start-scrtepmwo

2.11.1 Set the Cost Category for Required Resources:

In addition to these options, Required Resource processing must be enabled via a customization file or a registry setting (in sys-ffv-global-settings).

Setting Key: RequiredResourceInventoryCostCategory Setting Value: CostCategoryIdInventory
Setting Key: RequiredResourceOtherCostCategory Setting Value: CostCategoryIdOther

In the first option, specify a Cost Category Id to be used with the Inventory Items on the PM Parts list.

In the second option, specify a Cost Category Id to be used with the Other Items on the PM Parts list.

Also, if PM WO’s are being generated that HAVE required resources, the work order status will be Waiting Parts. This will override any entries made in the sys-web-access registry entries.

2.11.2 Do Not Write Required Resources to PM Work Orders

If your firm uses required resources, the following new registry may be used to prevent the writing of PM parts to the Required Resources tab for non-subcontractor technician (Required Resource lines are never written if the PM is created for a subcontractor technician):

Id: sys-start-scrtepmwo

Setting Key: DisableReqPMParts  Setting Value: true (default is false)

This registry entry only controls the writing of flagged service parts to the Required Resources tab. The TechServiceParts option is used to determine whether flagged parts will also be written to

The Inventory,/Other tabs as quoted lines (TechServiceParts=Yes or if the option is absent)

The Work Order Equipment Work Requested (TechServiceParts=Sub)

No additional lines written (TechServiceParts=No)

The above options control the behavior of flagged service parts if the technician is not a subcontractor or if a technician is not assigned. Flagged service parts are always written to the Work Order Equipment Work Requested for subcontractor techs.

2.11.3 Allow Multiple Work Codes Per Work Order

In version 7.2.476.071, we corrected a bug so that, if the Work Code Id is different on two lines of the Client Site Equipment PM Schedule for the same day and technician, the system forces a separate work order to be created. Since some users prefer to have PM lines with multiple work codes appear on the same work order, the following registry entry is now available:

Id: sys-start-scrtepmwo

Setting Key: IgnoreCase3242 Setting Value: true

2.12 AP Journal (sys-viewer-vapjrnl)

Disable Account Type Validations on GEN lines

In version 7.2.476.098, validations were added to the AP Journal to prohibit the entry of AR Control, AP Control & Bank accounts on GEN lines. Some users find that these validations conflict with their processing procedures: the following registry entry may be implemented turn the default error behavior (that does not allow the account to be selected) into a warning.

WARNING: disabling this validation is NOT recommended. In particular, entering a bank account on AP General lines will result in Bank Reconciliation issues.

Id: sys-viewer-vapjrnl

Setting Key: IgnoreCase3193  Setting Value: true

2.13 AR Sales Journal (sys-viewer-varslslst)

Disable Account Type Validations on Price lines

In version 7.2.476.098, validations were added to the AR Sales Journal to prohibit the entry of AP Control accounts on Prices lines. Some users find that these validations conflict with their processing procedures: the following registry entry may be implemented turn the default error behavior into a warning.

WARNING: disabling these validations is NOT recommended.

Setting Key: IgnoreCase3193  Setting Value: true

Allow Entry Type to be Changed

Validation has been added to prevent the user from changing the Entry Type on an existing entry. By default, the Entry Type may only be changed in the Sale Journal is in ‘add’ mode.

The following registry entry overrides the above validation, effectively restoring the previous behavior. Implementing this option is not recommended.

Setting Key: OkToChangeEntryType Setting Value: true (default is false)

2.14 Zip Code Lookup (sys-zipcode-lookup)

The ability to set related fields from the Zipcode table was originally implemented via registry. In recent releases, the software ignored the registry, and always defaulted from the zipcode table. This was a problem because you could not turn the functionality off. In this release, if the registry is not in place, defaulting from the zipcode table will no longer work. If your firm uses the zipcode table for defaulting, the registry option sys-zipcode-lookup must be in place.

Id: sys-zipcode-lookup

Set Default Behavior

Setting Key: default  Setting Value: true or false

This option controls the default behavior for the defaulting of the blank City and State fields, Branch Id’s. and Service Zones when a zip code (from the zip code table) is entered. Exceptions to this setting may be specified by record.

Set Exceptions to Default by Viewer

Setting Key: afunction  Setting Value: true or false

This option enables you to specify exceptions to the default behavior.

Example: Default Zipcode fields except in the Vendor Record

Setting Key: default Setting Value: true

Setting Value: vvndr Setting Value: false

2.15 Accounting Period

Option to Control WO Other to GL Box (sys-viewer-vaccntngprd)

In version 7.3, we implemented the optional interface of WO Other to GL which is controlled by a check box in the Accounting Period record. The following registry option is designed to help manage the setting of this new field:

Id: sys-viewer-vaccntngprd
Setting Key: OtherToGL Setting Value: true or false

This option should be set to true if the WO Other To GL box should be checked on all (or most) Accounting Periods.  If the user then creates an Accounting Period without checking the WO Other To GL box, he or she will be warned that this option has not been selected. 

This option should be set to false if the WO Other to GL box should never be checked.  The user will be unable to save the record with the Inventory to GL box checked.

If this option is not implemented, the system will not alert the user regardless of the status of the WO Other To GL box.

Note: the system also recognizes the Setting Key WOOtherToGL with the same functionality.

2.16 PR Check Printing

2.16.1 MICR Support for Multiple Bank Accounts / Entities

This release extends MICR check printing to handle multiple bank accounts / entities. The UseMICR option has been extended to PR check registry entries of the following forms:

sys-report-rprchck-GLACCTID-GLENTTYID

sys-report-rprchck-GLACCTID

Now the PR Check Entry Fields GL Account and GL Entity are used to look up the registry; if not found the default (sys-report-rprchck) is used. In this way you can assign different MICR values to each GL Account/Entity combination.

2.16.2 Suppress PTO Section on Check Stubs

Id: sys-report-rprchck

This registry setting will disable the display of PTO information on the PR check stubs. The default is for the PTO section to be displayed on the stubs.

2.17 Compute Payroll

Id: sys-compute-payroll

Setting Value: true

2.18 Registry to Set the Child Tab Label Fonts

This setting may be used to adjust the fonts used for the child tab labels in SAM Pro viewers. This was implemented for use with the Work Order (and other viewers with MANY tabs) for systems with lower resolution screens. By selecting a ‘skinnier’ font or lower point size, these tabs will now be available for users with lower-resolution screens. Previously, the only way of handling this was to suppress tabs or shorten their names via registry. This was not desirable since, if a new tab was added to SAM Pro, it would not appear unless the existing registry was altered.

Id: sys-font-TabControlChild

Setting Key: Facename Setting Value: aFaceName

where aFaceName is replaced by a valid font name (e.g., Arial, Tahoma). This font must be installed on the users’ computer or it will not be used. Hint: Arial is the ‘skinniest’ font that is available on the vast majority of PC’s.

Setting Key: Bold  Setting Value: Yes or No

Specify yes to use the bold version of the font, or no to use the normal version. Hint: the regular versions of variable width fonts such as Arial are ‘skinnier’ than the bold version.

Setting Key: Points:  Setting Value: aPointSize

Where aPointSize: specifies the size in points. Point sizes ranging from 8-10 are recommended.

Example:

Id: sys-font-TabControlChild

Setting Key: Facename  Setting Value: Arial

Setting Key: Bold  Setting Value: No

Setting Key: Points  Setting Value: 9

2.19 Registry to Set the Parent Tab Label Font

This setting may be used to adjust the Fonts used for the Parent tab labels in our SAM Pro viewers. This was implemented to use with the Job and other viewers with MANY tabs for users with lower resolution screens. Although the user may scroll the top tab bar, this registry may provide a more desirable solution.

Id: sys-font-TabControlParent

Setting Key: Facename Setting Value: aFaceName

where aFaceName is replaced by a valid font name (e.g., Arial, Tahoma). This font must be installed on the users’ computer or it will not be used. Hint: Arial is the ‘skinniest’ font that is available on the vast majority of PC’s.

Setting Key: Bold  Setting Value: Yes or No

Specify yes to use the bold version of the font, or no to use the normal version. Hint: the regular versions of variable width fonts such as Arial are ‘skinnier’ than the bold version.

Setting Key: Points:  Setting Value: aPointSize

Where aPointSize: specifies the size in points. Point sizes ranging from 8-10 are recommended.

Example:

Setting Key: Facename  Setting Value: Arial

Setting Key: Bold  Setting Value: Yes

Setting Key: Points  Setting Value: 9

2.20 Registry to Set Title Font

In previous releases, the registry entry (sys-font-title) used to specify the font for labeling titles and lists was restricted to a 10 point fixed width font. Changes to the way in which the titles are constructed means the registry is no longer limited to fixed-width fonts or a 10 point font size.

Example:

2.21 Inventory Restock (sys-viewer-vrstck)

In previous releases, the system deleted closed (completed) Inventory Restock transactions. This resulted in a lack of an appropriate audit trial for this function. The default in this release is to not delete restock records when they are closed.

To set the software to re-enable deletion for closed entries, set the following registry entry:

Id: sys-viewer-vrstck
Setting Key: DeleteClosedTransactions Setting Value: true

A Status filter range has been added to the Inventory Restock List and Inventory Restock Pick List Entry viewers. By default, this range is set to Open. To view both Open and Closed entries, click the All filter button. To view only Closed entries, click the Closed filter button.  

2.22 Tech Finder – Registry Options to Set Colors / Hour Levels

By default, cells in the Scheduled Hours grid are colors as follows:

Green: 2 hours or less currently scheduled

Yellow: 2.01 - 4 hours currently scheduled

Red: More than 4 hours currently scheduled

Gray: weekend day

This enhancement enables the user to set up to 5 work order hour cut offs and associated colors for use in the Tech Finder assigned hours section.

Note: When entering a color in registry If no registry entries are added the original colors for hours will be used.

Id: sys-tech-finder

Setting Key: Level#Limit Setting Value: hourlimit

Where # is replaced by the level number (1-5) and hourlimit is replaced by the number upper limit of hours displayed in the Level#Color option. Up to five levels may be specified.

Setting Key: Level1Color  
Setting Value: double-click left to bring up the color palette and select a color.

Registry Option to Set Color of Empty Cells

This sets the empty cells to the color set by the user.

Setting Key: emptyHoursColor
Setting Value: double-click left to bring up the color palette and select a color.

Example:

Setting Key: Level1Limit  Setting Value: 2
Setting Key: Level1Color  Setting Value: 8454016:Custom
Setting Key: Level2Limit  Setting Value: 5
Setting Key: Level2Color  Setting Value: 8454143:Custom

Note: when actually entering these options, set the colors by double-clicking in the Setting Value – this will display the Color Palette from which you will select a color.

2.22.1 Font and Alignment Options

Background:
Inconsistencies in the way Windows renders various fonts resulted in the right and left-hand upper panes in TechFinder not aligning perfectly. This was particularly obvious if many techs were listed. By default, the upper left-hand pane will now display in Courier New 10 point, and the upper right-hand will display in Arial 9 point. These defaults appear to work correctly if the user’s display is set to 100% font size.

The following registry setting may be used to override these defaults:

Id: sys-tech-finder-branchid-userid

Id: sys-tech-finder- - userid

Id: sys-tech-finder

Setting Key: font-WO-field  Setting Value: font:point:Bold

Setting Key: font-WO-title  Setting Value: font:point:Bold

Setting Key: font-Tech-field  Setting Value: fixedfont:point:Bold

Setting Key: font-Tech-title  Setting Value: fixedfont:point:Bold

Where

font is replaced by a replaced by a font facename (e.g., Arial, Tahoma, etc.). The font must be installed on users’ computers in order for it to be used.

fixedfont is replaced by a replaced by a fixed width font facename (e.g., Courier New, Lucida Console, etc.). The font must be installed on users’ computers in order for it to be used.

Point is replaced by an integer point size (typically 9 or 10).

:Bold is optional

Settings for Users Running at 125% Display

If the user is running in 125% (as set in Control Panel\All Control Panel Items\Display in Windows 7), the default setting may result in the left and right panes not aligning properly. In this case, the following settings may resolve the problem:

Setting Key: font-WO-field Setting Value: Arial:10:Bold

Setting Key: font-WO-title Setting Value: Arial:10:Bold

Setting Key: font-Tech-field Setting Value: Courier New:10

Setting Key: font-Tech-title Setting Value: Courier New:10:Bold

A registry setting is now available that, when implanted, adds a new method which will check for Pending events which have tokens which have not been replaced. This new method will do token replacements and update record change log for scheduled events. Please consult your support representative before implementing this option.

Id: sys-start-sschdldevntmngr

2.24 Start Reverse Job Invoice

Allow PM Invoices to be Reversed

The default behavior is now to deny PM Invoice reversal. The following registry setting may be implemented to allow PM Invoices to be reversed with a warning instead of an error. This registry option is deprecated, and should only be implemented after discussion with your support representative.

Id: sys-start-sjbinvcervrse

Setting Key: ReversePMInvoice Setting Value: warning (default is error)

Note: The PM Billing Schedule should now be used as the one-and-only source for PM Billing adjustments.  If a PM Invoice is issued in error, or needs to be reversed, the preferred method is to add a new line (with the appropriate negative value(s)), run Compute PM billing, and that print the negative dollar invoice (it will use the Client Site PM Billing line as the ‘source journal’).
