2.27 Registry Entry to Set Status Pane Color, Height and Text

This release includes updates to the text that is displayed at the very bottom of the SAM Pro window when the user places the mouse cursor over a button.

Now that the button definitions are being improved, it may be appropriate to make the status line itself more prominent. The following registry entry may be used to adjust the status line’s height, foreground color, background color and font.

Id:

sys-statuspane-branchid-userid

sys-statuspane--userid

sys-statuspane-branchid

sys-statuspane-securityid

sys-statuspane-usergroupid

sys-statuspane

Hint: you may use the security option of this entry to help remind multiple security users how they are logged in.

Specify Font Parameters

Setting Key: Facename Setting Value: aFaceName

where aFaceName is replaced by a font name (e.g., Arial, Tahoma). Note that font must be installed on the user’s computer to be displayed.

Setting Key: bold Setting Value: yes or no

Specify yes to use the bold version of the font, or no to use the normal version.

Setting Key: points Setting Value: aPointSize

This option specifies the size in points. Point sizes ranging from 10 -12 are recommended

Specify Height of Status Bar

Setting Key: height Setting Value: #ofpixels

This option specifies the height of the status pane in pixels. As a general rule of thumb, the height in pixels should be at least double the point size. For example, if your font is set to 11 points, the height should be set to 23.

2.28 Dispatch Board (sys-viewer-vdsptchbrd)

2.28.1 Identify Unavailable Techs

The Dispatch board and other viewers in the system are now able to indicate that a Technician is unavailable. The following registry entry is required to turn this functionality on. The Unavailable Days are set in the Unavailable Tab in the Technician record:

On the Classic board, unavailability is indicated with a red background on the column or row header displaying the Technician’s information for those days that he or she is unavailable. On the Power board, a currently unavailable Technician’s line in the Technician Summary (upper portion of the board) will be displayed in red.

In New Call, if the Technician and Date scheduled are both entered, a Warning will appear saying the Tech is Unavailable when the New Call is saved.

In TechFinder, the word ‘OFF’ will appear on the Technician hours pane if the technician is Unavailable. A Warning will appear saying the Tech is Unavailable if you select an Unavailable date.

In the Work Order Technician Tab, when the Tech Id or Date Scheduled is added or changed, the user will be warned if the Technician is Unavailable.

To implement this functionality, the following registry option must be enabled:

Setting Key: IdentifyUnavailableTechs Setting Value: true

2.29 Service Channel – (sys-fmms-vendor-servicechannel)

Specify Invoice UserId and Password

Invoices are uploaded to ServiceChannel by sending them an email with an attached spreadsheet. For each work order, the spreadsheet includes a User Id and a password. The User Id and password are derived from the Sampro Registry sys-fmms-vendor-servicechannel.

Setting Key: InvoiceUID  Setting Value: User Id provided by Service Channel

Setting Key: InvoicePWD  Setting Value: User Password provided by Service Channel

 

2.30 Service Channel - New Registry Entries for Multi-Company Use

Purpose:

Invoices are uploaded to ServiceChannel by sending them an email with an attached spreadsheet. For each work order, the spreadsheet includes a User Id and a password. Previously, the User Id and password were derived from the Sampro Registry sys-fmms-vendor-servicechannel, supporting only a single User Id and password contained in the registry entry. This results in the sending of the same User Id/Password pair for every work order regardless of the Sampro 'company'.

This procedure has been enhanced so that User Id/Password used is dependent on the corresponding work order. This release provides a mechanism for implementing multiple User Id/Password pairs when uploading invoices to ServiceChannel. The technique used is to provide for PIN based overrides in the Sampro ‘sys-fmms-vendor-servicechannel’ registry entry.

It work likes this:
•    The entire registry entry is retrieved from the Sampro Registry for the ‘sys-fmms-vendor-servicechannel’ key as usual.
•    The entire registry entry is retrieved from the Sampro Registry for the ‘sys-fmms-vendor-servicechannel-pin-XXXX’ key (where ‘XXXX’ is the pin identified by the work order).
•    The two entries are merged. Where there are duplicate entries, the second pin based registry takes precedence.

To implement the correct User Id/Password uploading for multi-company users, you must create a ‘sys-fmms-vendor-servicechannel-pin-XXXX’ for each company’s pin. The only lines needed are the InvoiceUID and InvoicePWD lines. For single company users, the invoiceUID and InvoicePWD lines can remain in the normal 'sys-fmms-vendor-servicechannel' registry entry.

Important Fields:

Id: sys-fmms-vendor-servicechannel-pin-XXXX

Where XXXX is replaced by the PIN provided by Service Channel. Note that individual registry entries must be created for all applicable PIN’s.

Required Settings for Multi-Company Use:

Setting Key: InvoiceUID  Setting Value: User Id provided by Service Channel

Setting Key: InvoicePWD  Setting Value: User Password provided by Service Channel

Make sure to specify the User Id and Password appropriate to the PIN specified in this registry entry.

2.31 Registry Option to Restrict Inactive Quotes

All quotes for an active lead work order are displayed in/ accessible from CSRAnywhere - including those that have a status category of Inactive. This Registry option may be overridden or implemented in the Web User registry tab.

Registry Id: web-settings-csr

Setting Key: RestrictInactiveQuotes Setting Value: true, false

The default is false - Quotes with an Inactive Status Category will NOT be restricted from the CSR Manage Quotes page to retain current default behavior. If this option is set to true, quotes with a status category of Inactive will not appear on the Quotes page. Note that the Web Server must be restarted for this option to take effect.

2.32 Registry Options for Bitmap ‘skins’

Version 7.3 supports a new and brighter look for SAM Pro via bitmap ‘skinning’ of the top and side button bars. These newer bitmaps are also designed to display more clearly on today’s high-resolution monitors. To implement this look requires a few simple registry settings and the set of SKIN1 bitmaps from Data-Basics. If you have been using SAM Pro for many years, this may feel like a big change, but once you start using the new bitmaps you will be surprised by how quickly you adapt to and enjoy using them.

Important Note on Colors: In order to fully support Bitmap Skinning, users’ computer display settings must be set to 24 or 32 bit color. If the Color Quality is set to 16 bit (Medium in XP, or High Color in Windows 7), the new bitmaps will appear with their standard, pale gray background, but the registry settable background and mouse over color changes will not appear. Setting the Color Quality to 24 or 32 bit should provide the full bitmap skinning functionality.

‘Not enough storage error’: The error ‘Not enough storage is available to process this command. ( OS error 16r8 )’ occurred to some users if their systems did not support the bitmap cloning associated with the new skins. In this release, bitmap cloning is disabled when the 'sys-gui' registry not available, a Skin Id is not specified, or when logging in as the support user. Note that this allows the skinning/cloning to be turned off (or on) by user via the User record Registry tab.

2.32.1 Global Settings Entry to Enable Bitmap Skin

In sys-ffv-global-settings the following option turns on skinning:

Setting Key: SkinId Setting Value: skinname (from sys-gui-skin-skinname)

Note: the Registry tab of the user record can be used to turn the new bitmap skins on or off by user.

2.32.2 Registry Setting to Configure Bitmap Skins

The registry entry defines the location of the new bitmaps, and enables you to configure their background and mouse-over colors, and the button bar width and height.

Registry Id: sys-gui-skin-skinname

Specifying the path to the ‘skinned’ bitmaps (required)

Setting Key: ButtonBitmapsPath Setting Value: directoryname

Where directoryname is the folder containing the skinned bitmaps, located in the directory containing the SAM Pro executable (e.g., SKIN1).

As of version 7.4.498.074, the folder SKIN1 will be included with zipped distribution image. The standard form of this option will be:

Setting Key: ButtonBitmapsPath Setting Value: SKIN1

Setting the Toolbar and Bitmap Background Color (required)

This release enables the user to specify the background color of the toolbar. This color will also be used to replace the 10% gray color (rgb 235 235 235 or windows color index 1546135) in the newer bitmaps installed in the image as well as those displayed in the top and side button bar skins. These buttons were designed for a light, pale colored background, and will not display well with a dark colored background. We have found that either the default light gray or a pale yellow display well.

Setting Key: ToolbarBackColor

Setting Value: (double-click to select a color or enter 1546135 for the pale gray)

Sets the Width of the sidebar and the Height of the topbar (required)

Setting Key: ToolbarWidth Setting Value: 104

Setting Key: ToolbarHeight Setting Value: 46

Setting the Mouse Over Color (optional)

The newer buttons (both the skinned buttons and the new buttons recently added to the image) now display a mouse over light blue color by default. The following registry selecting enables you to select your own color. Light colors are recommended. Note: this registry functionality is NOT supported in the Folders Viewer: the mouse over color is always a pale blue.

Setting Key: ButtonMouseOverColor Setting Value: double-click to select a color.

Setting the Mouse Over Border Colors (optional)

By default, when the pointer is placed over a button, a one-pixel width border is drawn around it. By default, the left-hand and top borders are white, and the bottom and right-hand borders are black. ButtonHighlightColorTopAndLeft and ButtonHighlightColorBottomAndRight indicate the colors used to draw the highlighting border around buttons as the mouse moves over top of them.

Setting Key: ButtonHighlightColorTopAndLeft Setting Value: (double-click to select a color)

Setting Key: ButtonHighlightColorBottomAndRight Setting Value: (double-click to select a color)

2.33 Purchase Order

Allow PO Type Change on Existing Record

In previous releases, users had the ability to go into purchase orders and change them from purchase orders to credit purchase orders and vice versa without any checks or tests. This had more impact on clients using the Unvouchered Option in the Accounting period as it produce an out-of-balance gl transaction. In this release, validation has been added to lock this down. If the PO is in add mode, the user is allowed to switch between the Purchase and Credit types. Once the record has been added, however, the user must cancel the PO, and add it as the correct type.

A registry entry (not recommended) is available to ignore this validation and restore the previous behavior and allow the PO Type to be changed on existing Purchase Orders:

Id: sys-viewer-vprchseordrlst

Setting Key: OkToChangePOType Setting Value: true

2.34 Recurring AP Journal (sys-viewer-vrcrrngapjrnl)

By default, the Recurring AP Journal prohibits the entry of AR Control, AP Control & Bank accounts on GEN lines. Some users have found that these validations conflict with their internal processing procedures: the following registry entry may be implemented turn the default error behavior into a warning. This option should only be set if a corresponding one exists in sys-viewer-vapjrnl.

Id: sys-viewer-vrcrrngapjrnl
Setting Key: IgnoreCase3193 Setting Value: true

2.35 SubAnywhere (sys-subanywhere)

An existing sys-subanywhere registry setting disables collateral from SubAnywhere from attaching to the site. In this release, you may also disable collateral from attaching to the equipment by implementing the following option:

Id: sys-subanywhere

Setting Key: AttachCollateralToEquipment Setting Value: false (default is true)

2.36 Start AP Payment Approved List (sys-start-sappymntapprvdlst)

This registry entry may be used to control the order this list appears in, and to set the Next Pay Date into the future for additional purchase control. .

Id: sys-start-sappymntapprvdlst

Setting Key: OrderBy    Setting Value: jb_id,wrkordr_id

This option enables the user to specify that the Start AP Payment Approved List is ordered by Job Id (in the PO Header), and then by Work Order Id (in the PO Header) within each Job.

Setting Key: CashManagerPayDate  Setting Value: 2099-12-31

This may be used to override the Pay Date entered on the Start AP Approved List (which may have been originally set on the Start AP Approved List PM). It would be used to make this process act like a 3rd approval function so that invoices approved in this fashion are NOT paid as part of the normal AP Check printing process (because the date is set so far in the future). To pay these checks, a cash manager would run AP Date to Pay, filtering on the date referenced in this entry in the Next Pay Date range. The cash manager could then review the entries, and select an appropriate Pay Date.

2.37 Stock Status Report Performance (sys-report-rstckstts)

A new enhancement is available that uses a temp table to improve the performance of the Stock Status Report. This enhancement was designed for SQL users but may also benefit Sybase users.

Id: sys-report-rstckstts

Setting Key: UseTempTable Setting Value: true

2.38 Email (sys-email)

Alternate Ports

This release (used in conjunction with the xmlToPdf.jar file dated 11/8/2011) supports alternate email ports for emails with .pdf attachments (controlled by the xmlToPdf.jar file) as well as emails without pdf attachments (managed by SAM Pro). The following two additional options in sys-email are required to support this functionality:

Setting Key: portsmtp Setting Value:port# (controls emails without pdf’s)

Setting Key: smtpPort Setting Value:port# (controls emails with pdf’s)

Secure Servers

This release also supports secure (SSL) email servers. To implement, the following additional registries are required:

Setting Key: useSSL  Setting Value: true

Setting Key: MailerMethod Setting Value: Java (required to send non-pdf emails securely)

Example: Use Port 465, Secure Server

Setting Key: portsmtp Setting Value: 465

Setting Key: smtpPort Setting Value:465

Setting Key: useSSL  Setting Value: true

Setting Key: MailerMethod Setting Value: Java

Note: the applicable PasswordSMTP, UserNameSMTP, and serversmtp options must also be set.

 

3. AP and Purchasing

3.1 Recurring AP Journal

This release corrects the calculation of the Recurring Lines Amount field based on the Quantity and Cost; previously, this calculation only supported Amounts under 100.00.

Previously, we enabled the IgnoreCase3193 registry option to allow users to enter (among other things) a bank account on the Recurring AP Journal Recurring Lines tab to support credit card/eft processing. In earlier versions, the Release Recurring AP Journal function did not evaluate this setting, and the post failed if a bank (or other denied) account was found. This problem has been corrected so the Release function successfully evaluates the sys-viewer-vrcrrngapjrnl for the IgnoreCase3193 option.

Validation has been added to prevent the entry of negative amounts in the following fields to prevent errors when these entries are released:

Main Tab: Recurring Amount:

Recurring Lines Tab: Quantity, Quantity Billable, Unit Cost, Amount, Revenue Rate, Amount Revenue

By default, the system prohibits the entry of AR Control, AP Control & Bank accounts on GEN lines. Some users have found that these validations conflict with their internal processing procedures: the registry entry detailed in user note 2.34 may be implemented turn the default error behavior into a warning.

This release corrects sporadic problem in Inventory History if an AP Journal entry for a PO referencing a Work Order with a difference location is deleted.

Validation has been added to not allow the record to be saved if the GL Bank Account field is completed and the Type ‘Check” is selected.

Corrects a problem with releasing entries if an Other Rate Id with a blank Job Cost Category was specified on the Recurring Lines tab.

Corrects an intermittent issue where the Check record was not always created for EFT or Credit Card transactions.

3.1.1 Main Tab

New Field: Day (0-31)
This new field enables the user to select the day of the month that will be used as the effective date for AP Journal entries generated from this record. Validation ensures that the Day value is not greater than 31.

The Start Release Recurring AP function has been enhanced to use the new value, if one is specified.  If the Day value is zero, then the existing code works as is, and the Effective Day of the generated AP Entry will be set from the Effective Date in the Release Recurring Journal range screen as in previous releases. 

If the Days value is not zero, the Days value will override the Effective Date of the release function. If this date doesn't fit within the Accounting Period Start/End Dates (for example, you are releasing AP Journals for February, and the Days field is set to 31), then the system will adjust the Date to fit (e.g., February 28 or 29).

3.2 AP Check

Corrects problem related to the Remit To address in the Purchase Order.

The Start and End dates have been promoted to being the first fields on the AP Check Range screen.

Range Screen - New Range: Invoice No:
This new range allows the SAMPRO user to print a check for a single vendor's invoice (or list of invoices) even though other invoices for the same vendor have the same Date to Pay.

3.3 Start PWP Billed Approval

This function no longer skips records with a zero total cost, hours or total revenue.

3.4 Void AP Checks

Validation has been added to prevent the user from voiding reconciled AP checks. In previous releases, the user was warned that a check was reconciled, but could in fact complete the void process.

3.5 Purchase Order

In previous releases, users had the ability to go into purchase orders and change them from purchase orders to credit purchase orders and vice versa without any checks or tests. This had more impact on clients using the Unvouchered Option in the Accounting period as it produce an out-of-balance gl transaction. In this release, validation has been added to lock this down. If the PO is in add mode, the user is allowed to switch between the Purchase and Credit types. Once the record has been added, however, the user must cancel the PO, and add it as the correct type. See user note 2.33 for a registry entry (not recommended) to ignore this validation.

See section 3.10 for changes related to the new Purchase Control enhancements in this release.

Unless disabled by registry, the first Equipment Id from the referenced Work Order defaults in PO detail lines. In previous releases, this resulted in the first Equipment Id from the Work Order being reloaded if the user changed the Job Cost Code or Billing Item AFTER specifying a different Equipment Id. This has been corrected so that the existing Equipment Id will not be changed when selecting a different Billing Item or Job Cost Code.

When adding a Purchase Order, the system will compare the Release Date with the PO header Job’s Date Closed. If the Release Date exceeds the Job’s Date Closed, the Purchase Order will not be saved. Note that if the Release Date is not completed, the system date will be used for the comparison. 

The user is now prevented from setting the PO Date Closed prior to the PO's creation date.

Credit PO's (both vouchered and not yet vouchered) can now be un-received (previously, only vouchered Credit PO’s could be un-received).

Previously, when a stock PO was created a Job Cost Category (but no Job), spurious job history with a committed cost and quantity (but no Job) was generated. In this release, changes to the Purchase Order, AP Journal and Inventory Receipts journals have been made to correct this problem.

If the sys-ffv-global setting 'DefaultEquipmentFromWorkorder' is set to false, the user is now allowed to set the Equipment Id back to blank in the Labor, PO and AP Journals. If this registry option (see user note 2.8.2) is not present or set to true, the Equipment Id must be completed if a Work Order Id is referenced.

3.5.1 Sub Tab

The system now allows negative Contract values on subcontractor lines. The system will warn the user when a negative value is entered, but will allow the PO to be saved.

3.6.1 Main Tab

New Field – Job Tax Status:
This display-only field has been added to the Main tab. The value is derived from the Job / Work Order entered in the PO header.

3.6 Report Purchase Order

Corrects display problem with extended price of Inventory on the printed purchase order.

3.7 AP Journal

This release corrects a Key is Missing error that occurred when the user attempted to delete a Material Returns line from an existing Credit Memo.

In this enhancement, the AP Journal Entry Type (Purchase or Credit Memo) has been added as a column to all of the list options for this viewer.

The registry option AttachCostsToARInvoiceForWO allows the user to attach vendor costs to AR Invoices when vouchering. In this release, attachment (whether manual or automatic) is no longer made to reversed AR Invoices.

When attempting to delete a journal entry, the system now checks the status of the Accounting Period earlier in the process. This prevents inappropriate changes to the Check records of manual checks and credit card transactions associated with AP Journal entries for inactive accounting periods.

If a manual check is entered, and then deleted, and the user elects to reuse check#, the system will now allow the number to be reused.

Validation has been added to prohibit the entry of AR Control, AP Control & Bank accounts on GEN lines. A registry entry may be used to disable this validation (see user note 2.12).

This viewer now supports the verification of reconciled check entries for multiple bank accounts.

If the sys-ffv-global setting 'DefaultEquipmentFromWorkorder' is set to false, the user is now allowed to set the Equipment Id back to blank in the Labor, PO and AP Journals. If this registry option (see user note 2.8.2) is not present or set to true, the Equipment Id must be completed if a Work Order Id is referenced.

3.7.1 Main Tab

Updated buttons that are easier to read on high-resolution monitors have been added to this screen:

New Field - Date Received:
This field may be used to record the date the Vendor Invoice was received by your company. Note that this field must be manually entered by the user: it does not default. If this field is important for reporting purposes for your firm, you may wish to make it a required field via registry.

Change Field: EFT/Credit Trx Id
In previous releases, the system erred when you added an entry with a single quote in this field, but allowed the entry to be saved, but it could not be deleted afterwards. In this release, the user is no longer allowed to enter the single quote in this field.

Enhanced Reports with Date Received (DAVAGE.rpt, CAPVAGE1.rpt and CAPVAGE2.rpt)

These reports are version 7.30, and must be dated 11/18/2010 or higher.

The Drill Down AP Aging report has been enhanced so that it may be aged by the Vendor’s Invoice Date (its current behavior), or the new Date Received field in the AP Journal. Note that if the Date Received field is blank, the date will be understood as 1900-01-01 and the amounts will appear in the 90+ Days aging column.

 

3.8 Preliminary Project Manager Approval of Held Vendor Invoices

3.8.1 Overview

This functionality enables your Project Managers to give preliminary approval to ‘requires approval’ Vendor Invoices either from the Project Managers Workbench, or via the new starter function Start AP Payment Approved List PM. Once approved by the Project Manager, these invoices will then be eligible for final approval during the standard AP Approve HELD Invoices (Start AP Payment Approved List) processing.

Important Note: If a Vendor Invoice is eligible for Project Manager Approval, it MUST be approved

First by the Project Manager (using the new Starter Function Start AP Payment Approved List PM or the Project Manager’s Workbench) AND

Second by the supervisor running AP Payment Approved List

3.8.2 Registry Option to Enable Project Manager Approval

New Registry Option to Require Preliminary Project Manager Approval of Vendor Invoices:

Id: sys-ffv-global-settings
Setting Key: ProjectManagerMustApproveVendorPayments  Setting Value: true (default is false)

This is option is required to enable your Project Managers to give preliminary approval to ‘requires approval’ Vendor Invoices. Once approved by the Project Manager, these invoices will then be eligible for final approval during the standard AP Approve HELD Invoices (Start AP Payment Approved List) functionality.

NOTE: AutoReleaseHeldVouchers and ProjectManagerMustApproveVendorPayments should NOT be implemented simultaneously.  If they are, the AutoReleaseHeldVouchers entry CONTINUES to rule the approval process, negating the whole purpose of Project Manager Approval.

Preliminary PM Approval applies in the following situations:

1. New registry setting noted above is in place.

2. Vendor Invoice must reference a PO that links to a job that has a Project Manager assigned to it.

3. Vendor Invoice must be 'on hold'.  (Use AP Terms Codes wisely)

3.8.3 New Function: Start AP Payment Approved List PM

Recent Update: This function matches the Vendor AP invoices for a job with the corresponding AR invoices for a job.  However, if the AP invoice had a blank job, it was matching it with AR invoices with blank jobs. In this release, the system restricts the amount collected in AR to history where the Job is specified.

Purpose:

This function enables Project Managers to give preliminary approval to ‘requires approval’ Vendor Invoices. Once approved by the Project Manager, these invoices will then be eligible for final approval during the standard AP Approve HELD Invoices (Start AP Payment Approved List) processing.

Usage:

To be eligible for PM Approval a Vendor Invoice must be 'on hold' AND Reference a PO that links to a job that has a Project Manager assigned to it. Only those invoices associated with the Project Manager running this function will appear on the list.

In addition, the registry option described in release note 3.8.2 must be in place.

Important Fields: Initial Screen

Date to Pay:
Enter the payment date for these invoices in mmddyyyy format.

Vendor Id:
Enter a Vendor Id to limit this list to a specific vendor. Multiple vendors can be specified by separating their Id's with a comma (ACME,JONES,BRILLIANT).

AP InvoiceNo:
The vendor invoice number recorded in the AP Journal. If blank, all eligible entries will be selected.

WorkOrder Id:
The work order with which this payment is associated. If you leave this range blank, all eligible entries will be selected.

PO Id:
To limit this function to a Purchase Order (or list of PO’s), enter the PO Id (or a lists of Id’s separated by commas). If you leave this range blank, all eligible entries will be selected.

After completing the Date and any desired range fields, click the Go button to display the Checklist confirmation screen.

Important Fields: Checklist Screen

Do
This field enables you to select which Invoices will be PM approved for payment. By default, no invoices are selected. Double-click on the Do field to select or deselect an item.

Vendor Name: A/P Invoice No: A/P Invoice (Amount): Balance:
These fields default from the AP Journal/History.

Pay Balance Button: When clicked, the button will fill in the PM Amount Approved with the Balance, and flag the Do check box.

PM Amount Approved:
The amount the Project Manager wishes to approve for the next payment. This amount may NOT exceed the invoice balance if a previous payment has been made.

WO Id: Job Id: Job Name:
These informational fields indicate the Work Order / Job this invoice is associated with.

Pay Date:
The date to appear on the AP check. This field defaults from the Date to Pay field in the AP Journal, but may be changed by the user).

Customer Name: AR Inv Id: AR Inv Amt: PO Id:
These display-only fields are maintained by the system.

Important Buttons:

Click the Check button to check (select) every item on the list.

Click to de-select every item on the list.

Click to view all attached documents for this invoice. Documents attached to the Vendor Invoice, Purchase Order, and AR Invoice will be combined into a .PDF file and displayed.

View Invoices Button: When the View Invoices button is clicked, all Vendor Invoices (typically scanned into the AP Journal or Quick Attached) included on this list will be displayed..

After making specifying the PM Amount Appr and Pay Date on any invoices you have flagged as Do, click the Go button. The information on the AP Approval PM will be used by the system when determining which Vendor Invoices will be eligible for final approval during the standard AP Approve HELD Invoices (Start AP Payment Approved List) processing.

3.8.4 PM Approving Held Invoices from the Project Manager Workbench

The Project Manager Workbench may also be used to approve Held invoices. To do so, select the A/P Summary tab. This tab lists vouchered Vendor Invoices associated with this Job. Double-clicking on a line will display the Vendor Invoice Record.

To PM Approve invoices, right click on the Invoice you wish to approve. When you do so, a data-entry box will appear prompting you to ‘Enter new values’. The following fields will appear:

Vendor Id and Name:
PO Id and Description:
Invoice No: Invoice Date: Invoiced (Amount):
Unpaid Retainage: Net Unpaid: Due Date:
Approved By: Date Approved:
These display-only fields are provided for your information from AP History, and summarized the current status of this Vendor Invoice.

PM Amount Approved: Next Pay Date:
These fields enable the project manager to approve invoices for payment.

Click OK to confirm the changes that you have made in this box; click CANCEL to abandon these changes. The changes made here will flag this invoice as PM Approved.

3.8.5 Changes made to AP Approve HELD Invoices (Start AP Payment Approved List)

New Fields:
PM Approve: PM Amount Approved: PM Date Approved:
If Preliminary PM Approval is enabled (see user note 3.8.1), and this was a Held Requires Approval Invoice, there fields will reflect the amount the Project Manager has approved. Note that the Approved amount cannot exceed the PM Amount Approved.

Has Notes:
If any Notes are associated with this Vendor Invoice, the box will be flagged. Notes for the selected line may be viewed or added by clicking the Notes button on the side button bar.

New Buttons:

Click to view all attached documents for this invoice. Documents attached to the Vendor Invoice, Purchase Order, and AR Invoice will be combined into a .PDF file and displayed.

View Invoices
When this button is clicked, all Vendor Invoices (typically scanned into the AP Journal or Quick Attached) included on this list will be displayed.

The Notes button enables you to view and/or add notes to the selected line’s Vendor Invoice.

If preliminary project manager approval is enabled, this button will be enabled. If there is a dispute between the user running the final approval and the project manager, click this button to email the Project Manager a message regarding the dispute. When you do so, an e-mail form will appear. By default, the email address referenced by your User record will appear in the From: box, and the Project Manager’s e-mail address will appear in the To: box. The Subject line will be completed as follows: Please see {my user Id} regarding Invoice#:. Add any attachments needed, or additional information in the Message section then click the Send Email button. You may wish to CC: yourself on the message.

3.9 Reorder Advice Report

In previous releases, quantities on order/received were not handled correctly if a PO was subsequently turned into a Change Order. In this release, PO-related data is correctly combined by Base PO Id. This report is part of SAM Pro and does not been to be imported.

3.10 Purchase Controls - Enhancement

New fields added to the Vendor, Insurance, and User records allows dollar limits to be placed on release purchase orders created by specific users, a PO Limit per Work Order, and the ability to block the release of PO for Vendors with expired Insurance.

3.10.1 Insurance Viewer

New Field: Block Purchases

If this field is flagged, and the Vendor’s Insurance is expired, a PO for this vendor may only be saved as Unreleased. The PO cannot be released until the Vendor’s insurance is renewed, and the Vendor’s Insurance Tab entries are updated. Note that today’s date is compared with the Start and End Dates on the Vendor Insurance tab in order to determine if the Insurance is expired. This prevents new PO’s from being backdated to when the insurance was in effect.

Note that this field is also displayed on the Vendor Insurance Tab, and the Purchase Order Main tab.

3.10.2 Vendor Viewer

Two new tabs, Defaults and User Fields, have been added to the parent select of the Vendor viewer. Several existing fields from the Main and Contacts tabs have been moved the Defaults tab for better organization.

Defaults Tab New Field: PO Limit per WO

This field comes into play if a WorkOrder Id is specified in the PO header. If this field is blank, this Vendor is not subject to a dollar limit on the PO. If this field is completed, only PO’s under this limit can be released. Note that the system checks the dollar value of all PO’s for this Vendor/WO combination when testing to see if the PO Limit is exceeded. In order to release the PO, this field must be edited in the Vendor record by a user with the authority to do so.

NOTE: the dollar amount of the released PO may also be limited by the MAX PO Amount found in the User record.

3.10.3 User Viewer – Registry Tab

This release implements the use of the Registry tab in the User Viewer to add / override sys-ffv-global-settings for this User. Since these settings are loaded when the user logs on, he or she must log on after User Registry changes are made to see them in effect.

In addition to global settings, the following option is designed specifically for use on this tab.

User Registry Option to Specify Maximum Dollar Amount of Released PO’s.

Key: maxpoamount Value: limit in dollars

If this User Registry entry not implemented (and the User is flagged as a Purchasing Agent), the user is not limited to the dollar amount of a PO that he can save as Released.

If this User Registry is implemented for a User flagged as a Purchasing agent, the PO cannot be released if the PO amount exceeds this field; the PO must be saved as Unreleased. A User (who is also a Purchase Agent) with a higher maxpoamount can edit and release the PO in this situation.

Example: To specify a $600 maximum release PO limit for this User:

User Registry: Key: maxpoamount Value: 600

NOTE: the dollar amount of the released PO may also be limited by the PO Limit per WO found in the Vendor record.

3.10.4 Purchase Order – Status Tab

New Fields:

User PO Limit:
This display field defaults from the maxpoamount key value on the User’s Registry tab. If this field is completed and the user is flagged as a Purchase Agent, it represents the maximum dollar amount of a PO that the user can save as released. If this limit is exceeded, the PO may be saved as Unreleased. A User with a higher PO limit can then edit and release the Purchase Order.

If this field is blank, a User PO Limit is not in effect.

Vendor PO Limit per WO:
This display field defaults from the PO Limit per WO field in the Vendor record. If the field is blank, a PO Limit per WO is not in effect.

Vendor WO Total (Other PO’s):
This display field is calculated by the system, and shows the total of all other PO’s for this Vendor which reference the same header WO Id as in this PO. If the dollar amount of this field plus the total dollar amount of this PO exceeds the Vendor PO Limit per WO, the PO can only be saved as Unreleased.

3.11 Start Create EOM Unvouchered AP GL Entries:

In previous releases, this function skipped GEN lines from Credit PO’s but picked up Inventory lines. In this release, applicable Inventory and Gen lines on Credit PO’s lines will be processed.

 

4. Client, Site, Equipment

4.1 Client Site Equipment

An additional 10 Client Site Equipment User fields have been added to the User Fields tab, for a total of 20.

A new field, Deny TA Access, has been added to the Main tab. An RAQ may be implemented to deny TechAnywhere users access to this equipment if the Deny TA Access box is checked. Note that a new v.cus is required in order to see the new field.

An obsolete field, Calendar Base Year, has been removed from Service tab. Users may need a new v.cus to see this change.

4.2 Client Site

In previous releases, the Client Site User 1 and 2 fields appeared on both the COP and User Field tabs. They are now only on the User Field tab as they should be.

4.2.1 Main Tab

The Call Script Id field on the Main tab has been relabeled to reflect its function: WO Closing Call Script id.

Changed Fields - Longitude and Latitude:
These fields were previously display-only. They have been exposed to enable the user to manually enter appropriate values.

4.2.2 PM Billing Tab

A registry entry is now available to provide default Income and Accrual GL Accounts that will be used if they are not completed on this tab. See user note 4.2.2 for details.

The PM Billing tab now has a full screen view, accessible by clicking the Magnify button.

The PM Billing Schedule should now be used as the one-and-only source for PM Billing information.  Other Master Contract entries continue to generated to this tab, contract changes, credit memos, revised billing, etc are now all manageable from this tab. The following enhancements provide the user with means to do so.

Enhanced Fields: Amt to Bill: Amt to Earn:
These fields (previously Bill Amount and Amount Earn) now allow entry of negative values. This allows users to effectively reverse errors in billing and amortization by adding a new line (with the appropriate negative values). After running Compute PM billing, the user should then print the negative dollar invoice (it will use the Client Site PM Billing line as the ‘source journal’). Note that validation prevents the entry of both positive and negative contract amounts on the same line. The entry of negative amounts is denied on lines flagged as 'renewable'.

When the Start PM Billing function is run, negative Amt to Earn (amortization) lines will result in a GL Journal entry with a negative debit to the accrued expenses account (the GL Debit account) and a negative credit to the sales accrued (the GL Credit account).

Changed Fields: Renewable Billings: Renewable Earnings:
These display-only fields appear at the top of the PM Billing tab, and were previously labeled ‘Total Billings’ and ‘Total Earnings’. They display the running total of the Amount to Invoice and Amount Earned of all lines marked as 'Ok to Renew' and have been relabeled to clarify their functionality.

Changed Field: Date:
In previous versions, this field was labeled ‘Bill Date’. The label has been changed to ‘Date.’

Changed Field: PM Inv No:
This field was previously labeled Invoice Nu; the label has been changed for clarity.

New Field: Invoice Status
This field comes from the Invoice Master record (if available):

When the PM Invoice No. field is blank, the Invoice Status is blank.
When a valid PM Invoice Id is shown, the Invoice Status comes from the associated Invoice Master record.
If the PM Invoice Id cannot be found in the Invoice Master table, the Invoice Status displays 'unknown'.

New Field: GLJ Trx Id:
This display-only field lists the GL Transaction Id of amortized lines that have been posted to GL.

If the line's amortization amount (Amt to Earn) is zero, the GLJ Trx Id displays 'n/a'.

When the line has an Earn amount but the posted-to-gl flag is false, the Trx Id display is blank.

If the system fails to find a qualifying transaction, the Trx Id display reads 'unknown'.

If multiple amortizations for the same accounting period have been made for the same job, only the most recent GLJ Transaction will be listed. If this is the case, the GLJ Transaction will be followed by an asterisk, indicated that multiple transactions exist.

Changed Field: Posted to GL?
In previous versions, this field was labeled ‘Po’. The label has been changed to clarify its function.

New Field: Invoice Description Extended
This field has been added to the Detail view of PM Billing tab to allow for a more detailed Invoice Description.  If completed, this field is written to the Invoice Description of Work Performed during the creation of PM Invoice-type work orders. Note that the older Invoice Description on the PM line is still written to the Revenue Adjustment line as in previous releases.

New Field: Work Order Id:
This field has been added to the detail view (accessed with the Magnify button) of these lines. If a PM Invoice Work Order was generated to bill this line, its Id will be displayed in this field.

Changed Field Labels: Client Site PM Billing Tab Detail View

GL Income (was GL Credit Id):
GL Accrual (was GL Debit Id):

These labels have been changed to better define their function.

4.3 Start Client Site Import

Purpose:

This function allows a user to import a pre-defined, comma separated ASCII file containing information needed to create new records and relationships between Clients, Client Sites, Client Site Equipment, Jobs, Cost Codes and Billing Items in the database. When the import function is run, the system will create a new Client Site along with one or more Client Site Equipment records referencing a newly created Job/Cost Code/Billing Item and Client combination based on the specified Client Id and Job Id used for cloning an existing relationship.

If any errors occur during the import (i.e. invalid Client, Job or other referenced table values) the entire import process will abort and an error report will be generated specifying what problems were experienced during the import. The user can then re-attempt the import after the errors are corrected.

Registry:

When this function is run, SAM Pro will open a browser window so that you may select the appropriate .cvs file for importing your client site data.

Registry Option to Specify Directory for CSV Site Import Files

Id: sys-start-Sclntsteimprt
Key: CSVDirectory=C:\ClientSites (A directory to place CSV files)

Usage:

The .csv file must contain a valid Client Id and Job Id (per row of data) that the system can use as a model for cloning. Any other fields from the Client Site record (parent only) may be specified in the file layout. Any specified field values that reference a table other than the Client Site must be valid values in the database. For example, if the Account Manager Id “Tim” is specified in the file layout then “Tim” must exist in the Account Manager table prior to importing the file.

Please contact your support representative for suggestions on managing your import file to ensure that dates and other fields are formatted correctly.

Imported data must be formatted as follows:

4.4 Client

4.4.1 Client Collection

The following updated buttons that are easier to read on high-resolution monitors have been added to this screen:

4.4.2 Client Collection Notes

This release corrects a problem where Collection Notes were not deleted properly if the user exited from SAM Pro immediately after deleting this type of note.

The following updated buttons that are easier to read on high-resolution monitors have been added to this screen:

5. Invoicing and AR Related

5.1 Revenue Adjustments

In previous versions, the Revenue Adjustment Table only supported Discounts for Labor, Material, Subcontract, Total, and Exception entries. A new field, Rate Type, has been added to the Revenue Adjustment Table (and it’s Labor, Inventory and Other Exception tabs). The Rate Type field has two options, Add and Deduct. These options enable the user to choose whether the percentage will be handled as a deduction (discount) or addition when the Adjust Revenue functionality is invoked in Work Orders and Quotes.

During data conversion from a previous release, existing Rate’s will be assigned the Rate Type of Deduct so that they will continue to be handled as discounts.

Note: the user was already allowed to manually select Add or Deduct on the Revenue Adjustment tab of Work Orders and Quotes. This enhancement extends this functionality to system-generated lines.

5.1.1 Revenue Adjustment Parent Tab

New / Changed Fields on Labor, Material, Other, Subcontract and Total Lines:

Change Field: Rate% (was Discount %)
Rate Type: Add Deduct
Select Deduct to apply the Rate% as a discount. Select Add to apply the Rate% as a markup.

5.1.2 Labor Exceptions, Inventory Exceptions, Other Exceptions Tabs

New Fields on Labor Exceptions, Inventory Exceptions, Other Exceptions
Add Deduct
Select Deduct to apply the Rate% as a discount. Select Add to apply the Rate% as a markup.

5.2 Record Billing Adjustments:

Rounding logic has been added to retainage calculations. This should correct sporadic problems where the retainage was off by a penny or two.

If the user clears the Next Invoice Id field, they are now asked if they meant to clear the field (Click Yes), or if was cleared in error (Click No to restore the field’s original contents).

5.3 Sales Summary By Sales Rep Report

Purpose:

This report lists Sales and Quota information for your Sales Reps for the selected month (current and previous year), as well as year to date figures for the current and previous sales year.

Report Description:

The Quota information on the report is obtained from the Sales Commission History Table: this includes entries generated from the Sales Rep viewer’s Quota tab, as well as manual entries made to the Sales Commission History table.

The Sales information on the report is obtained from Job History (the Job Invoice Amount is used to determine the total Sales amount) and the Job’s Commission tab (the Share % will be used to calculate how the Job Invoice Amount should be allocated among the Sales Rep’s if more than one is listed on the Job’s Commission tab).

The first page(s) list quota and sales dollars and percentages, broken down by Sales Rep and Job Type.

The last page provides a summary by Job Type for all Sales Reps included on the report.

Report Format:

  Current Month   Year to Date 

  Previous Year Current Year Previous Year  Current Year  

Sales Rep Quota Sale %  Quota Sale %  Quota Sale % Quota Sale %

Important Fields: Report Range Screen

Sales Year:
Enter the 4-digit year that you want the system to use as the current sales year.

Sales Month:
Select the month the system will use as the Current month.

Description:
Enter any text that you wish to appear on the header of this report.

Sales Rep:
If this field is blank, all Sales Reps for which there is data will be included on the report. If you only wish to run this report for a specific Sales Rep, enter the Sales Rep Id (or double-click to select from a list). Several Sales Reps may be listed by entering their Id's separated by commas.

Job Type:
If this field is blank, all Job Types for which there is data will be included on the report. If you only wish to run this report for a specific Job Type, enter the Job Type Id (or double-click to select from a list). Several Job Types may be listed by entering their Id's separated by commas.

Click the Go button to run the report.

5.4 Payment Type Viewer

New Field: GL Bank Account Id:
This field may be completed for Payment Types associated with COD payments. When a Payment Type is selected on the Work Order COD parent or child tab (or posted from TechAnywhere), the GL Bank Account specified in this viewer will be defaulted in. Note that the Work Order will deny changes to the GL Bank Account on the COD data entry forms when it has defaulted from the Payment Type

5.5 AR Sales Journal

Corrects a sporadic problem using the Create Credit Memo Button for a COP posting where the line amounts did not total correctly.

Updated buttons that are easier to read on high-resolution monitors have been added to the Main tab:

This release incorporates enhanced validation to deny changes to the Invoice Id for previously posted AR Sales entries and to insure that the specified Invoice Id must be appropriate for users’ security settings.

This release closes a loophole that allowed users to overwrite an existing Invoice Master record when crediting a Credit Memo without using the Credit Memo button.

Creating a Credit Memo from an existing Sales Journal entry now clears the Cost Billed on the child tab when the Create CM button is used.

Validation has been added to prohibit the entry of AP Control accounts on Prices lines.

Previously, we added a warning when the user clicked the Create CM button if the invoice balance did not equal the invoice total. The message has been improved so that if the invoice balance is zero, the message now displays as the following instead of display a blank instead of 0:

“Warning: Invoice Balance is Zero and does not equal Invoice Total: 79.54. Do you want to continue?”

5.6 Create PM Invoice

This release corrects an error that occurred if RININV4 was used for PM Invoices.

5.7 Other Rate

Changed Field: GL Credit Account:
If you will be interfacing WO Other to GL, this field should be completed if this Other Rate will be entered on the WO Other Tab. Note that this functionality may be used in conjunction with the expense of Assets on the Work Order Other tab and Job Journal Co. Equipment viewer.

This field also provides the default GL Credit on the Job Journal’s CoEquip Tab which enables chargeable Assets to be charged to a Job or Work Order.

5.8 AR Cash Receipts Journal

Updated buttons that are easier to read on high-resolution monitors have been added to this screen:

Previously, changes were not allowed to entries referencing an inactive accounting period. In this release, changes (and applicable reversing entries) to receipts in inactive accounting periods will be written to the open accounting period and effective date that the user selects. Changes are not allowed if the receipt has been entered in the Bank Deposit Journal.

5.8.1 Validations

The following validations have been added to prevent the Client Id in AR Cash Receipts entries from being changed:

1. The Client Id cannot be changed unless the AR Cash Receipts viewer is in Add Mode (this denies the user the ability to change the Client in existing entries.

2. The Client Id cannot be changed when the AR Cash Receipts viewer is in Add Mode if any child rows have been entered in the middle section of the screen.

3. Manually entered Invoice Ids (invcemstr) must be for the parent Client Id specified in the transaction.

5.8.2. Enter Invoices

The Remove Invoice button now correctly removes the selected line, not the following one.

 

5.9 Service Invoice

This release corrects a problem when the Max Tax per Invoice protocol was implemented (SalesTaxMaxPerInvoice=true in sys-ffv-global-settings) where sales tax was assessed on Use Tax jobs.

5.9.1 COD Work Orders

Corrects a ‘Key is missing error’ in recent versions that occurred when invoicing zero dollar COD invoices.

5.9.2. COD Work Orders and Template Clients

New validation ensures that template-type clients are only billed when the net invoice amount is exactly ZERO DOLLARS.

The Service Billing Worksheet report has been modified to display a very noticeable warning for each WO/Job invoice that would result in a template-type client being billed for any amount other than zero. The Service Worksheet report (SERVICEWORKSHEETv73b032.rpt dated 11/22/2011) must be imported to support this functionality.

The following changes have been added to the process of preparing Service Invoices:

When the Service Invoice report is run, the system compiles a list of each WO/Job combination for which a Template Clients would be billed a non-zero amount. This list will be displayed in a workspace viewer that the user may choose to close or print.

In addition, the system auto-saves the compiled list as a text file. If the dbreportfiles registry entry exists, the system will use it to get the location to save the file with the Template Client errors. If the dbreportfiles registry entry does not exist, the Sampro base directory will be used to save the file with the Template Client errors.

Work Orders that make this list CANNOT be included in the invoicing run.

This release allows zero dollar invoices with only costs (and no revenues/COD entries) to be billed to a template Client. In addition, the Service Worksheet processing no longer brings up the list of each WO/Job combination; this is reserved for Service Invoicing only.

6. General Ledger

6.1 Bank Reconciliation Journal

The GL Interest and Fees GL Accounts and Entities are now stored in the database for the Bank Reconciliation parent so they will always be available when a transaction is accessed for editing.

6.2 Recurring GL Journal

Recurring GL Journal entries are inactivated by setting the Last Effective Date to earlier than today. This enhancement adds a Last Effective Date range filter to the viewer list. This filter is preset to exclude entries with a Last Effective Date less than the current system date from the active list.

The following fixes have been implemented to prevent out of balance entries:

If you Delete lines, the totals on top are now updated.

If you elect to Copy lines (from insert), the totals on top are correctly updated.

On an existing entry, change a debit or credit amount but do NOT tab out of the field will no longer allow you to save the entry OOB.

6.3 GL Journal

The upper portion of the GL Journal has been adjusted to show more information without scrolling. The Debits and Total Credits fields have been moved to the top of the child (lower) section of the scroll for easier visibility.

A detail view of the child lines may now be accessed via the Magnify button. The detail view shows relevant Job and PO id values when available. 

7. Job Costing

7.1 Job Viewer

The system does not display Revenues, Invoices and Purchases if the Job is a Template or does not reference a Client Site. In this release, the messages that appear under these conditions have been made more specific (e.g., clicking the Revenues tab of a Template Job displays the message “Revenues data not available for Template Job”).

If you click the sidebar button Create PO in a Job record and the system date (today) exceeds the Job’s Date Closed, the message ‘Cannot Create Job PO for closed Job’ will be displayed; the Purchase Order viewer will not be launched.  

The Job Tax Status radio buttons have been reordered so that ‘Unknown’ appears first, and will be the default when a blank Job record is displayed.

Previously, if the CloneJobEquipmentExistingSite registry was enabled, cloning the job resulted in the existing site having its PM Billing lines changed to the newest job. In this release, the Site’s PM Billing Schedule is not changed as a result of the clone.

7.1.1 Job viewer – Budget Tab

By default the effective date of Budget Entries posted to Job History via the Budget tab is set to blank (1900-01-01). See user note 2.1.1 for details on a registry option that causes the software to use the Job’s Date Open as the Effective date for budget entries made to job history from this tab.

7.1.2 Job Prevailing Wages Tab

When using the Prevailing Wage logic on a job, the job cost calculated for overtime was incorrect. This has been corrected in this release so that the job cost is no longer inflated.

Relabeled Field - Base Rate: (was Package)
This field should be used to enter the base wage rate for this Prevailing Wage. If your data was converted from an earlier version, this field will contain the value stored in the field previously labeled Package. The system will sum the Fringe Rate and the Base Rate when determining whether to use the Prevailing Wage during Compute Payroll.

Example 1: Employee’s Regular Wages + Fringes Exceed Job Base + Fringes Amount

Base Rate: $25.00 / hour

Fringe Rate: $0.00

Wage Earnings: $24.00 / hour

Fringe 1: $2.50 / hour

Fringe 2: $1.50 / hour

Since the Employee’s regular Wages + Fringes total $28.00 / hours (greater than the prevailing wage Base + Fringe of $25.00/ hour), they will be used for payroll calculations for this Prevailing Wage job.

Example 2: Job Base Rate + Fringes Amount Exceeds Employee’s Regular Wages + Fringes

Base Rate: $40.00 / hour

Fringe Rage: $5.00 / hour

Wage Earnings: $27.00 / hour

Fringe: $1.00 / hour

Since the Employee’s regular Wages + Fringes total $28.00 / hours, the Prevailing Wage methodology will come into effect since the Base Rate + Fringe Rate = 45.00 / hour. The system calculates the Employee’s Wages as follows:

Wage Earnings Calculated Under Prevailing Wage: $44.00 / hour

Fringe: $1.00 / hour

Note that the Employee’s Wages + Fringes package now equals $45 / hours, the Prevailing Wage Job Package rate. The increased difference is added to the Employee wage.

New Field - Fringe Rate:
 This field enables you to separate Fringes from the Base Rate for prevailing wages. The system will sum the Fringe Rate and the Base Rate when determining whether to use the Prevailing Wage during Compute Payroll.

New Field - Certified PR Report Label:
The Certified Payroll report has been enhanced so that it uses this field (if completed) instead of the Labor Rate Description. If this field is blank, the Labor Rate Description will be used.

Note: the updated Report PR Certified Payroll Report (RPRCRPR.rpt) (dated 11/12/2010) is required to take advantage of the Label functionality.

7.1.3 Purchases Tab

In previous releases, a PO only displayed if the Job Id was completed in the header AND the PO had items. The following enhancements have been made to the current image:

If the PO has no items, it will display with “Purchase Not Itemized” in the Description field

PO’s will also be displayed if the header WO Id references the Job.

7.1.4 Job Main Tab

Updated buttons that are easier to read on high-resolution monitors have been added to this tab:

7.1.5 Job JC Summary Tab

This release corrects a display issue on the JC Summary tab: moving the mouse within this tab no longer results in buttons from the Main or Invoicing tabs showing through.

 

 

7.2 Project Manager Workbench – New Viewer

If you click the sidebar button Create PO for a selected Job, and the system date (today) exceeds the Job’s Date Closed, the message ‘Cannot Create Job PO for closed Job’ will be displayed; the Purchase Order viewer will not be launched.  

Purpose:

This new viewer is designed to enable a project manager to handle all critical functions related to a job including:

RFI/RFP/Submittal/RFQ document creation and tracking, Subcontractor PO management, Vendor Invoice Approval and Change Order Management.

Usage:

Now handles Long Strings in Document Replacement for MS Office 2010.

The Project Manager Viewer must be used to update the Project Manager record.

Since the Project Manager Workbench can be used to change the Job record itself, the user cannot use both the Project Manager Workbench Viewer and the Job Viewer to update the same Job simultaneously.

In order to use the RFI, Submittals, Transmittals, and RFQ functionality, a Word Document must be available for use as a template; see user release note 7.3 for details. Registry entries (see below) are required to specify the name and location of these documents.

Important Note on Customization Files:
If your firm’s customization file impacts the Job record, these changes will also be in effect in the Project Manager Workbench. Specific customization file changes to the Project Manager Workbench must be implemented by Data-Basics programming; see your support representative for details.

Registry:

Important Note on Registry Options:
Registry options specified in sys-viewer-vjb will also impact the Project Manager Workbench unless overridden by that option in sys-viewer-vjbpm

Option to Hide Employee Labor Cost on Cost Sources Tab

Registry Id: sys-viewer-vjbpm

Setting Key: HideEmployeeLaborCost Setting Value: true

By default, the Project Manager’s Workbench shows actual and committed cost for individual employees on the Cost Sources tab. When this registry option is implemented, individual employee labor costs will be hidden, but the Actual and Committed Costs included in the totals displayed on the Cost Sources tab.

Options to Specify RFI, Submittal, Transmittal and RFQ Document Templates

Id: sys-viewer-vjbpm  Name: View Project Manager Workbench

Setting Key: newTemplateRFI Setting Value: sharepath\filename.ext

Setting Key: newTemplateSubmittal Setting Value: sharepath\filename.ext

Setting Key: newTemplateTransmittal Setting Value: sharepath\filename.ext

Setting Key: newTemplateRFQ Setting Value: sharepath\filename.ext

These entries enable you to specify the Word documents that will be used as the start points for your RFI’s, Submittals, Transmittals and RFQ’s. A path is used to designate the file itself (if you are specifying a URL share path make sure that the directory containing the documents is shared).

Example:

 Setting Key: newTemplateRFI Setting Value: \\myserver\sampro\templates\RFI.doc

Option to Specify Reports Lists on the Reports Tab 

Id: sys-viewer-vjbpm Name: View Project Manager Workbench

Setting Key: reports Setting Value: reportfunctionid1,reportfunctionid2,...

where reportfunctionid1 is replaced by the Function Id of the Report that you want to appear on the Project Manager Workbench Reports tab. To identify the Function Id of a report that you wish to include, go to the Range screen for that report, and select Help from the menu. The Function Id will be listed on the drop-down Help box.

Example:

Setting Key: reports Setting Value: DJBPMR,DPMCCRPT

Registry Option to Set Effective Date of Budget Tab Entries to the Job Open Date

By default the effective date of Budget Entries posted to Job History via the Budget tab is set to blank (1900-01-01). This could cause issues when compiling a WIP summary report.  For example, suppose the user runs a WIP summary report for say 03/31/2010, and then places new jobs in service in April.  If the user must re-run the report for the end of March (03/31/2010) the totals will change (using the budgets from Job Viewer) whereas, using the Job Journal or if the budgets had a date they would have remained consistent. 

Id: sys-viewer-vjb (impacts both the Job and Project Manager Workbench)

 Or

Id: sys-viewer-vjbpm (impacts only the Project Manager Workbench)

Setting Key: BudgetEffectiveDate Setting Value: DateOpened

Note on Existing Data: when implementing this registry, you may wish to update the Job History Budget entries generated by the Job Budget tab to correspond to the Job’s Date Opened. An SQL script for this purpose may be run to update your data: contact your support representative for details.

Important Buttons:

If you select a Job and then click the Job Progress sidebar button, the system will open the Job Progress viewer for the selected job.  

Click this button to launch the Purchase Order viewer to create a PO for the selected Job. The Job Id in the new PO will be completed for you.

Important Fields (upper section):

Main Tab:

This tab displays pertinent fields for this Job and its related records.

Note: the following buttons (New RFI, New Submittal, New Transmittal and New RFQ) require the appropriate registry entries and document templates (see user note 7.3) to be operational.

When the New RFI button is clicked, the system will display a data-entry screen asking you to enter several values it will use to create the new RFI document. Enter the following fields:

Description: (Enter a brief description of the RFI)
Contact Id: (Enter or double-click to select the Job Contact that this RFI should be sent to)
Date Requested: (Enter or double-click to select the request reply date for this RFI)
Document Description: (Used in the SAM Pro document record associated with this file)

Once you have completed these fields, click OK to proceed. A copy of the RFI document template will opened, with the appropriate values (from the data entry screen and Job-related records) already completed. The document may be edited as needed. SAM Pro will automatically save an archive copy of the document when it is closed. This document may be accessed from the RFI tab, as is also attached to the Job record.

When the New Transmittal button is clicked, the system will display a data-entry screen asking you to enter several values it will use to create the new Transmittal document. Enter the following fields:

Description: (Enter a brief description of the Transmittal)
Contact Id: (Enter or double-click to select the Job Contact that this Transmittal should be sent to)
Document Description: (Used in the SAM Pro document record associated with this file)

Once you have completed these fields, click OK to proceed. A copy of the Transmittal document template will open, with the appropriate values (from the data entry screen and Job-related records) already completed. The document may be edited as needed, and sent it to the customer. SAM Pro will automatically save an archive copy of the document when it is closed. This document may be accessed from the Transmittal tab, and is attached to the Job record itself.

When the New Submittal button is clicked, the system will display a data-entry screen asking you to enter several values it will use to create you to values for creating the new Submittal document. Enter the following fields:

Description: (Enter a brief description of the Submittal)
Contact Id: (Enter or double-click to select the Job Contact that this Submittal should be sent to)
Document Description: (Used in the SAM Pro document record associated with this file)

Once you have completed these fields, click OK to proceed. A copy of the Submittal document template will open, with the appropriate values (from the data entry screen and Job-related records) already completed. This document may be edited as needed, and sent to the customer. SAM Pro will automatically save an archive copy of the document when it is closed. This document may be accessed from the Submittal tab, and is also attached to the Job record.

When the New RFQ button is clicked, the system will display a data-entry screen asking you to enter several values it will use to create the new Request for Quotation document. Note that at least one Contact MUST be specified on the Vendor Additional Contact tab for this functionality to be enabled. When the box appears, enter the following fields:

Description: (Enter a brief description of the RFQ)
Vendor Id: (Enter the Vendor from whom you are requesting this Quote)
Contact: (Double-click to select the Vendor Contact (on the Vendor’s Additional Contact tab) that this RFQ should be sent to)
Date Requested: (Enter the respond by date for this Quote)
Document Description: (Used in the SAM Pro document record associated with this file)

Once you have completed these fields, click OK to proceed. A copy of the RFQ document template will open, with the appropriate values (from the data entry screens, and Job-related / Vendor records) already completed. The document may be edited as needed, and sent to the Vendor. SAM Pro will automatically save an archive copy of the document when it is closed. This document may be accessed from the RFQ tab, and is also attached to the Job record.

JC Summary Tab

The JC Summary tab displays a Job Cost summary, as well as Job Progress information similar to what is available on the Project Manager Summary Report. This tab also includes Aged AR and Budget information.

Bill To Tab

NOTE: any changes that you make on this tab will be reflected on the Invoicing Tab of the Job Record.

These buttons enable you to copy the address from the Client or Site record to the Invoice Address fields below.

Invoice Address:

Note: these fields will be overridden by the information in the Billing Address Id. It is highly recommended that the Billing Address Id be used for the invoice address, especially in the case where you have Multiple sites/jobs which use the same CLIENT) in case the Client moves.   

Name on Invoice:
This field should contain the name that should appear on this invoice.

Attention Line:
This field enables you to specific an attention line for invoices generated for this job.

Street Address: City: State: Zip:
The address that invoices for this job should be sent to.

Billing Address Id:
This field enables you to specify the job billing address by selecting it from the Job Billing Address record. If this field is completed, the Invoice Address and the Invoice Email address (if auto-emailing of invoices is enabled via registry) for this Job will come from the Job Billing Address record. If the Billing Address Id is blank, the Invoice Address will come from the Invoice Address fields to the left.

Work Order Override:
If a Billing Address Id is specified in the Work Order, that record will override both the Job Billing Address Id and the Invoice Address/Invoice Email Address in the Job record.

Service Compute?
If checked, the service compute method will be used for this job, and invoices will be generated from the work orders associated from this job rather than via Record Billing Adjustments.

Invoice Email Address:
If the auto-emailing of service invoices is enabled, the system will email invoices to this address unless this field is overridden by the Billing Address Id in the Job or Work Order record.

Invoice:
 Report Id:  Report Query Id:
The default Invoice Report and Report Query formats to be used with this Job. Job Billing Items may specify different Report Queries (e.g., a Job Billing Item for Fixed Fee Contracts would specify a different Invoice Report Query than one designed for the Time and Materials Billing Item for the same Job).

Invoiced Thru
This field is automatically updated when the Compute Job Billing function is run.

Job Invoice Description:
This field prints on the construction invoice (rininv3 format). It may be updated from here or from the corresponding field in Record Billing Adjustments.

Computed Thru: JTD Retainage: Next Inv. Retainage: Invoice Status:
Next Inv.Total: Next Inv.Taxable Amount: Next Inv.Sales Tax: Next Inv.Deposit to Apply
These display-only fields are maintained by the system.

Contract Items:

ContractAmt – CO Amount - %Earned – Next Invoice – EarnedToDate – Stored Material – %Retainage - InvoicedToDate – CostToDate – CO?
This tab displays all active Billing Items / Change Orders associated with this Job.

You may double-click on a line to launch the Job Billing Item or Change Order viewer for that record.

To edit selected fields for the selected Job Billing or CO record, right-click on the line. When you do so, a data-entry box will appear prompting you to ‘Enter new values’. The following fields will appear:

Bill Item: (the Id of the selected Job Billing or Change Order record; this field is display only).

Original Contract: (if this is not a Change Order): the Billing Item’s Original Contract Amount; may be changed by the user from this screen instead of Record Billing Adjustments.

CO Amount: (if this is a Change Order): the CO’s Original Contract Amount; may be changed by the user.

Earned to Date% - Contract Earned:
These fields apply to fixed fee/contract billing. They may be updated to release charges for billing.

Bill Item Description: briefly describes this item.

Retainage %: the default retainage (or holdback) percent for this item.

OK to Bill? This box should be checked if it is OK to bill for this item, or blank if it is not OK to bill. Double-click or press the Spacebar to set/clear this field.

Date Started: When a billing item is first created, the Date Started default to today’s date; this field may be adjusted by the user to indicate the start of work or .

Date Completed:
The Date Completed field enables you to indicate that a contract item has been finished. This field is referenced when entering labor, material or other charges. If the Effective Date of the entry exceeds the Date Completed, the system will warn you of the problem but will not prevent the transaction from being saved unless the Prevent Use of Completed Job Cost Codes and Billing Items registry option is implemented.

Click OK to confirm the changes that you have made in this box; click CANCEL to abandon these changes.

Attachments Tab

This tab displays all Documents associated with the Job selected in the Workbench. Double-click on a line to display the document.

Category – Description – Tab Name – Reference Id – Date Logged – Time Logged Document Id – File Location
The display-only fields on this tab are maintained by the system.

Notes Tab

This tab displays the Notes associated with the Job or entered in the Workbench itself. Double-click on a line to display the Note.

Author – Summary – Date – Time – Access
The display-only fields on this tab are maintained by the system.

Reports Tab

This tab lists the Reports that have been specified for the project managers in your company via registry. Double-click on a Report to launch it. The report’s Job range (if it exists on the report) will be filled in with the selected Job. If a Project Manager range appears on the report, it will be filled in with the Project Manager’s Id.

RFI Tab

Number – Sent - Description – Recipient – Received – Document Id

This tab displays all RFI’s generated for this Job via the New RFI button. You may double-click on a line to display the RFI.

To edit selected fields for the selected RFI, right click on the line. When you do so, a data-entry box will appear prompting you to ‘Enter new values’. The following fields will appear:

Description: (Briefly descriptions the RFI – may be updated by the user)
Date Received: (Enter the date you received the reply from the customer).
Document Description: (Used in the SAM Pro document record associated with this file)

Click OK to confirm the changes that you have made in this box; click CANCEL to abandon these changes.

Transmittal s Tab

Number – Sent - Description – Recipient – Document Id

This tab displays all Transmittal Documents generated for this Job via the New Transmittal button. You may double-click on a line to display the Transmittal.

To edit selected fields for the selected Transmittal, right click on the line. When you do so, a data-entry box will appear prompting you to ‘Enter new values’. The following fields will appear:

Description: (Briefly descriptions the Transmittal – may be updated by the user)
Document Description: (Used in the SAM Pro document record associated with this file)

Click OK to confirm the changes that you have made in this box; click CANCEL to abandon these changes.

Submittals Tab

Number – Sent - Description – Recipient – Document Id

This tab displays all Submittal Documents generated for this Job via the New Submittal button. You may double-click on a line to display the Submittal.

To edit selected fields for the selected Submittal, right click on the line. When you do so, a data-entry box will appear prompting you to ‘Enter new values’. The following fields will appear:

Description: (Briefly descriptions the Submittal – may be updated by the user)
Document Description: (Used in the SAM Pro document record associated with this file)

RFQ Tab

Number – Sent - Description – Vendor Id – Vendor Name – Received – Amount - Document Id

This tab displays all RFQ Documents generated for this Job via the New RFQ button. You may double-click on a line to display the RFQ.

To edit selected fields for the selected RFQ, right click on the line. When you do so, a data-entry box will appear prompting you to ‘Enter new values’. The following fields will appear:
