Important Fields (Lower Section):

Contact Tab

The Contact tab enables you to attach one or more Contacts to the selected Job. Changes made to this tab will be reflected on the Job viewer.

Contact Id:
Enter a valid Contact Id (or double-click to select from a list). You may create as many lines as needed to accommodate all contacts. The display-only Name, Firm, Email and Phone number fields will default from the Contact record.

Contact Type Id:
This optional field defaults from the Contact record but may be changed by the user if needed.

Milestone Tab

This tab associates Milestones with this Job record. Milestones are used for reporting purposes. Changes made to this tab will be reflected on the Job viewer.

Milestone Id:
Enter a Milestone Id or double-click to select from a list.

Start Date: End Date:
The Starting and Ending dates for this Milestone.

Description:
A brief description of this Milestone.

Completed?
Check this field (by double-clicking on it) if this Milestone has been completed. When you do so, your User Id and the Date Marked will be displayed by the system.

Budget Entry Tab

Entries made in this tab will be written to Job History as Budget entries. Edits and changes to this lines will also be written to JCH. This tab also allows for the import of budget data from a .csv spreadsheet. Changes made to this tab will be reflected on the Job viewer. This tab provides a quick way to record budgets for small jobs, but does not replace the Job Journal budgeting functionality. Users that record Budget Changes should continue to use the Job Journal as the budget entry point.

By default, the Effective Date of budget entries generated from this tab is blank. A registry entry may be used to set the Effective Date to the Job’s Open Date (see Registry Entries section at the beginning of this user note).

Editing Budget Entries:
The Budget tab functions like the other SAM Pro journals. If it is necessary to change a line, simply change it to the desired value and save the record. If your firm needs Budget Change functionality, the Job Journal should be used to record Budgets.

Important Fields:

Hours: Quantity:
The Hours fields should be used to record labor budgets lines, and the Quantity field should be used to record material or other items. On a single line, fill in either the Hours or Quantity field.

Inventory Item:
This optional field would be used if you are budgeting for specific parts. Note that the cost / revenue for this part must be specified by the user (or imported from a spreadsheet); these values will not default from inventory history.

Cost Category:
Enter (or import) an appropriate Job Cost Category for this line. For example, a Cost Category of type Labor should be selected for Hours entries. This field is required.

Job Cost Code: Job Billing Item:
The Cost Code and Billing Item this budget is assigned to. These fields are required.

Unit Cost: Extended Cost:
The Unit Cost must be entered by the user or imported a spreadsheet. If entering the budget manually, the system will multiply the Hours or Quantity by the Unit Cost to calculate the extended cost.

Billing Type: Revenue Rate: Extended Revenue:
By default, the billing type is set to n/a so that the user can enter/import the Revenue directly. To have the system calculate the Extended Revenue for you, select a Billing Type and enter a Revenue Rate.

Important Buttons:

The Import Budget button may be used to import budget data from an estimator’s spreadsheet (see below for the format details).

When you click this button, the system will determine how any existing budget lines should be handled:

Click 'Yes' to REPLACE all existing lines on the Budget tab.
Click 'No' to ADD the imported lines to the Budget tab.
Click 'Cancel' to end the import without updating the budget lines.

If you click Yes (to replace) or No (to add the imported lines to the existing ones), a browser window will open. Browse to the desired spreadsheet and click Save.

If the system detects any problems with the spreadsheet, it will display them. The spreadsheet must be corrected before it can be imported. You may print and then close the ‘workspace’ listing of errors.

Once the Budget lines have been imported, remember to Save the Job record. Doing so will make the appropriate budget entries to Job History.

Spreadsheet Format:

The system expects a spreadsheet with 9 columns. During the import to the Budget tab, SAM Pro will validate that the formatting is correct, and that any referenced Inventory, Cost Code, Cost Category and Billing Item Id’s exist. The Description field must be completed for correct processing.

The first row should include only column titles, listed in bold below. The additional rows will contain the budget data itself.

Column 1: Hours – numeric field for labor budget lines – ######.## max

Column 2: Quantity - numeric field for material and other budget lines – #####.### max

Column 3: Inv Part # - text field; if included, must correspond to a valid Inventory Item Id – 30 alphanumeric max

Column 4: Unit Cost – numeric field – ######.#### max

Column 5: Unit Rev – numeric field – ######.#### max

Column 6: Cost Code – text field; must correspond to a valid Job Cost Code for this Job – 30 alphanumeric max

Column 7: Cost Cat – text field; must correspond to a valid Job Cost Category appropriate for this line

Column 8: Bill Item – text field, must correspond to a valid Job Billing Item for this Job – 30 alphanumeric max

Column 9: Description – used to enter a description for this entry – 40 alphanumeric max.

 Note that the description column must contain a value, even it is only a blank space.

Cost Sources Tab

Date – Source – Trx Id – Reference – Hours to Date – Quantity to Date – Actual Cost – Committed Cost

The Cost Sources Tab displays the actual and committed costs associated with this Job. These costs were written to Job History derived from the following sources: Work Order, Purchase Order, Credit Purchase Order, Labor, Payroll Adjustment and Inventory Adjustment Journals.

Cost Codes Tab

CostCode – Hours to Date – QtyToDate – Actual Cost – Committed Cost

This tab displays a summary view of the costs to date for each of the Cost Codes for this Job. Since this information is pulled from Job History, only those cost codes which have Job History will appear. For each Cost Code, quantities, Committed Costs and Actual Costs are summarized. Double-clicking on a line will launch the Cost Code viewer.

PO Id – Description – QtyOrdered – U-M Unit Cost – Amount – QtyReceived – QtyVouchered – Vendor Name

This tab lists the Inventory and General information from Purchase Orders associated with this Job. This tab is updated as PO’s are entered, cancelled, received and vouchered.

Subcontract POs Tab

PO Id – Vendor – Description – Orig Amount - %Earned - $Earned – CO Amount – Approved – Start - End

This tab lists the Subcontract information on the Purchase Orders associated with this Job. To edit selected fields for the PO, right click on the line. When you do so, a data-entry box will appear prompting you to ‘Enter new values’. The following fields will appear:

PO Id: - Vendor Name: - Description:
Original Amount: Change Order Amount: Total Contract:
These display-only fields are provided for your information; changes must be made directly in the purchase order.

Percent Earned:  Earned Amount:
If work is progressing on this line, enter either the total Percent or the Amount Earned (to date) and the system will calculate the other. These fields (along with the Retainage and previously vouchered amount) control the dollar amount that may be paid to the subcontractor/vendor.

Retainage %
The percent retainage to be withheld for this line (if any).

Click OK to confirm the changes that you have made in this box; click CANCEL to abandon these changes. The changes made here will be reflected in the purchase order.

Invoices Tab

Invoice Id – Invoice Date – Amount Billed – Amount Paid – Invoice Status

This tab lists the invoices associated with this job. If invoices are archived on your system, double-clicking on this line will display an image of the invoice.

A/P Summary

Status – Vendor – Invoice No. – PO Id – Description – Inv Date – Invoice Amount – Due Date – Retainage – AmtPaidPO – Net Unpaid – Approved By – Approved - PayDate

This tab lists vouchered Vendor Invoices associated with this Job. Double-clicking on a line will display the Vendor Invoice Record. Vendor invoices associated with both Purchases and Credit PO’s appear.

To PM Approve a PO, right click on the line. When you do so, a data-entry box will appear prompting you to ‘Enter new values’. The following fields will appear:

Vendor Id and Name:
PO Id and Description:
Invoice No: Invoice Date: Invoiced (Amount):
Unpaid Retainage: Net Unpaid: Due Date:
Approved By: Date Approved:
These display-only fields are provided for your information from AP History, and summarized the current status of this Vendor Invoice.

Pay Balance Button: When clicked, the button will transfer the Net Unpaid to the PM Amount Approved. Clicking the Pay Balance button correctly sets the PM Amount Approved to a negative value for a Credit PO entry.

PM Amount Approved: Next Pay Date:
These fields enable the project manager to approve invoices for payment.

(See user note 3.8 for detailed information on PM Approval of Held Invoices).

Click OK to confirm the changes that you have made in this box; click CANCEL to abandon these changes. The changes made here will enable payment to be made to this vendor and be reflected on this tab.

Progress Tab

Bill Item – Cost Type – Code Code – Cost Category – Budget - %Used – Actual – Committed – To Complete –
Projected - %Complete – Over (Under) – ProgressAsOf – Last Cost – Last Budget

This tab summarizes progress billing on this job.

7.3 Project Manager Workbench: Word Documents for use as RFI, Transmittals, Submittals, and RFQ Templates

Clicking the RFI, Submittal, Transmittal, or RFQ button in the Project Manager Workbench will enables the user to launch a Word Document where certain fields been preset with information from your SAM Pro database. ‘Token replacement’ (a form of search and replace) will be used to populate your document with the pertinent information from your SAM Pro database. Standard Microsoft Word features (such as the use of the Date field to generate today’s date) are also supported.

All fields using their database field name from the following tables can be used preceded by a '<' and suffixed by a '>':

Job (jb)

Client (clnt)

Client Site (clntste)

Project Manager (prjctmngr)

Project Manager Contact (pm_cntct)

Job Contact (jb_cntct)

Vendor (vndr)

Vendor Contacts (vndrcntct)

Job Log (jbclg)

Examples:

The standard RFI document (RFI.doc) provided by support contains the following text and tokens:

Request for Information #<jbclg_nmbr> Date

Fax #: <jb_cntct_cntct_phne_fx> Job #: <jb_id>

Phone: <jb_cntct_cntct_phne> Project:<jb_nme>  

Reply To: <pm_cntct_cntct_nme>

Attn: <jb_cntct_cntct_nme> Requested Reply Date: <jbclg_dte_rqstd>

Request:

<jbclg_dscrptn> 

When the user clicks the RFI button and completes the data entry fields, a copy of the RFI document will open, with the tokens replaced with the values from the data entry fields as well as the tables associated with the Job you have selected in the Project Manager Workbench. For example, if was the first RFI for this job, and if the user clicked the RFI button on August 30, 2010, the following document will be launched in MS Word:

Request for Information #1 August 30, 2010

Fax #: 216-555-1242 Job #: C15342

Phone: 216-555-1423 Project: Cranbrook Mall Renovation

Reply To: Gerry Hanson

Attn: Tom Barry Requested Reply Date: September 15, 2010

Request:

Mall HVAC specifications. 

In this example, the Requested Reply Date and Description would be entered by the used in the RFI data-entry form. At this point, the user would simply edit the document as needed, and send it to the customer. SAM Pro will automatically save an archive copy of the document when it is closed.

List of Tokens:

The following is a list of the more popular tokens:

Job Id=<jb_id>

Job Name=<jb_nme>

Job Alpha=<jb_alpha>

Job Invoice Name=<jb_invce_nme>

7.3.1  PM Workbench / External Apps

As we have done in the WO, Quote, PO and Shop Packet in previous SAM Pro versions, this enhancement allows Crystal Reports to pick up the specific ID (Job ID in this case) that is currently active in the program (PM Workbench in this case). With this new ability, Crystal Report Functions added to the Reports tab of the PM Workbench do not require the user to enter in the Job ID if the report is job based. The Crystal Report must use a parameter named exactly jb_id in order for it to have SAM Pro pass it to the report.

In the specific example of how it is being used, the Client wanted to print out a “log record” of Submittals and RFI requests made for the job so that they could give that document to the Client/Architect. Without this enhancement, they would have to double-click on the Crystal Report Function in the Reports tab and remember the job id so they could manually fill it in. With this feature, the user immediately gets the report to run with no interaction for that specific job they are on.

 

7.4 Job Progress Viewer

If you right-click on the Job Id (when a member of User Group All), the system no long asks if you wish to customize the field. Note that low-level code now disallows viewers from re-viewing themselves, so it is no long possible to open the Job viewer from the Job Progress viewer.

This release corrects a reported problem with calculation of the Margin %. This problem was caused by the budgeted revenue amount being truncated in the work area.

7.5 Job Billing Item

The system does not display Revenues, Invoices and Purchases if the Job is a Template or does not reference a Client Site. In this release, the messages that appear under these conditions have been made more specific (e.g., clicking the Revenues tab of a Template Job displays the message “Revenues data not available for Template Job”).

Corrects overlapping fields problem with the Fee Taxable Box.

7.6. Job Template

The Job Tax Status radio buttons have been reordered so that ‘Unknown’ appears first, and will be the default when a blank Job record is displayed.

7.7 Job Cost Category

PM (Project Manager) filtering has been applied to this viewer: if the PM Filter is completed in your user record, only those Billing Items that are eligible for your setting will appear.

Changed Field: GL Expense Account
This field also provides the default GL Debit Account for Work Order Other lines if the Accounting Period option Work Order Other to GL is flagged.

7.8 Job Journal

This release corrects a sporadic error that resulted in the Job Journal posting incorrect reversals to GL history.

Expenses posted to GL History now have the source journal correctly identified as Job Expense, not Job Labor.

7.8.1 Job Journal Expenses Tab

The Extended Revenue now automatically defaults if the Billing Item is not Fixed Fee. For Billing Items that are flagged as Fixed Fee, Allow Extras, it is still necessary to flag the Extra box in order for the Extended Revenue field to default.

7.9 Start Reverse Job Invoice

Invoices corresponding to the user’s PM (Project Manager) Filter may be selected.

When reversing a service invoice, the user is now prompted with: "You are reversing and invoice related to Work Order <wrkordr_id). Would you like to set the Work Order Status to Invoice Ready?" If the user clicks yes, the system now changes any work order technician lines currently set to Billed to Invoice Ready and recalculates the Escalation Status (setting it to Invoice Ready unless other Tech lines override this setting). If the user clicks no, the system reverses the invoice but doesn't change the WO Escalation status / tech lines.

7.9.1 Reversing PM Invoices

The default behavior of Start Compute Job Invoices is now to deny the reversal of PM Invoices. The PM Billing Schedule should now be used as the one-and-only source for PM Billing adjustments; the preferred method to reverse PM Invoices is by:

1- Adding a new line (with the appropriate negative values) to the Client Site PM Schedule

2- Run Compute PM Billing

3- Print the Negative Dollar invoice

A registry entry (see user note 2.24) is available to allow (with a warning) the reversal of PM Invoices.

7.10 Project Manager Viewer:

If you click the sidebar button Create PO for a selected Job record, and the system date (today) exceeds the Job’s Date Closed, the message ‘Cannot Create Job PO for closed Job’ will be displayed; the Purchase Order viewer will not be launched.  

7.11 Start Job Cost Allocation

Corrects the Start Job Cost Allocation ‘Key is missing’ error that occurred when attempting to enter the Start Date.

 

8. Inventory

8.1 Inventory Adjustments Journal

New Field: Bill Item
You may now specify the Job Billing Item when doing Job-related transfers and adjustments. The Billing Item will default from the Cost Code (if specified in the Cost Code), but may be changed by the user.

New Field:
Transaction Type:

Loc-to-Loc
Loc-to-Job
Job-to-Job
Job-to-Loc
Adjustment

This new field implements validation logic that ensures that the data entry for Transfers is consistent with the selected Transaction Type.  For example, entry of job-related data is not permitted on a Loc-to-Loc (Location to Location) transfer transaction. Before entering your transfer data, select the appropriate Transaction Type.

The Transaction Type of Adjustment permits data entry according to the previous rules due to the wide variety of adjustments that may be made. During data conversion, existing records will be displayed as Adjustments.

8.2 Inventory Physical Count

This release corrects a problem in the List Physical Count report: the List Missing Items option, as well as the First and Last Uncounted fields now work properly.

Implement Export/Import Mechanism Via Spreadsheets

This enhancement has been made to facilitate the ease of data collection for physical inventory counts by exporting a spreadsheet file with the suggested list of parts to count for the batch’s Location. This spreadsheet may then be updated using a spreadsheet program, and then imported into the Physical Count Viewer so that the adjustments may be computed.

To implement this enhancement, two new buttons have been added to the Physical Count Viewer; ‘1b. Build Export Files’ and ‘2b. Import Entries.’ If these two buttons are used, the ‘1a. Load OnHand’ and ‘2a. Print Report’ buttons should NOT be used.

Build Export Files Button
When this button is clicked, the system opens a window requesting the Activity Window in Days to ensure that inactive, old stock that is not currently on hand at the location will be excluded from this process. Depending upon your firm’s needs and business cycle, an appropriate number of days could range from 3 months (90 days) to a couple of years (730 days).

Once the user has entered the desired number of days and clicked the OK button, the system will generate a comma separated ASCII file that can be opened in Excel. A browser window will be opened to allow the user to select the name and save location of this file. The file will contain all inventory items that are currently on hand in a user specified location (truck) along with any inventory items that have an on hand quantity less than or equal to 0 that have any on hand activity (+/-) within the Activity Window in Days.
The fields in the ASCII file will contain:

Inventory Item Id
Inventory Item Name
Count (this will be blank for all parts listed and will need to be filled out by the user):
                note that any count left blank will be treated as zero when the file is imported
Comment 1
Comment 2
Sequence No.

Import Entries Button
This release also adds functionality will allow you to import the ASCII file (once it’s filled out) so that the system can calculate the adjustments necessary. To do so, simple click the Import Entries button, point to the applicable file when the browser window appears, and click Open.  The data (excluding the sequence number) you entered in the spreadsheet will be imported.

Next, click the Compute Adjustment button and then Save the batch. At this point, you may make any further adjustments needed, and click the Post Adjustments button to update the physical inventory for this location.

8.3 Report Stock Status Report

A "Print Summary Only" box has been added to this report. When checked, only the summary sections of the report (for Locations and Groups) will be printed.

8.4 Inventory Item

The Equipment Type Id has been added as a Range Field to the Inventory Item Filter Screen.

Corrects the Inventory Serial Tab 'openLabTestResults' Not Understood error when double-clicking on a line. The Serial/Lot Master is now correctly displayed.

The Locations, Purchases, YTD, and Orders tabs no longer display spurious information for the blank record.

This release corrects a Last Unit Cost problem that occurred sporadically with new Inventory items.

8.4.1 Inventory Item Vendors Tab

The Inventory Item Vendor Tab’s Price field is no longer updated by Credit PO’s.

8.4.2 Price Code Handling – change to default behavior

This change impacts the Work Order, Quote, Client Order, and CSRAnywhere (Quote Management).

The Inventory Item allows for 10 levels of Material Pricing, but Price Codes only allow for 5. In this situation, if a client normally had material price level 7, and Price Codes were in effect, the system would use markup pricing instead.

In this release, with price codes in effect, and the default price level from the Client Site or Job is greater than 5, the system now defaults price level 1 from the Price Code. A registry entry (see user note 2.4.9) is available to always default Price Code Level 1.

8.4.3 Purchases Tab

The Purchases Tab was not displaying On Hand values correctly if a receipt was made on the base purchase order, the purchase order was made a change order, and then the remainder was received. This problem has been corrected.

8.4.4 Pricing / Costing Tab

An Updated button that is easier to read on high-resolution monitors has been added to this tab:

 

8.5 Location viewer

Corrects the Inventory Serial Tab 'openLabTestResults' Not Understood error when double-clicking on a line. The Serial/Lot Master is now correctly displayed.

New Tab: Location Items

This record now displays correctly if one or more inventory items on the Location Items tab have a quantity-on-hand of 100,000 or more.

This release corrects a discrepancy between the On Hand figures between the Location Viewer's Location Item tab and the Inventory Viewer's Location tab. The calculation used to display the Locations Items tab no longer includes the quantity bought to a Job in the On Hand column.

The Location viewer has been enhanced to query both the Inventory Item and the Inventory History tables for info about the Location record being viewed.

New Button: Import Stock Levels

The Import Levels button helps get a new truck 'started'. 

1. Create a new Location record.

2. Push the Import Stock Levels button.

3. Enter the Id of the Location from which to 'clone'.

4. A check list is constructed from invntryitmlctn data based on the source Location.  The user can select which Inventory Items to include.  The Picking Sequence, Reorder Level and Order Up To values can be edited as necessary.  When the GO button is pushed, all selected records will be added to the invntryitmlctn table for the new truck.

Note: Using Import Stock Levels to update Existing Sites (Trucks)
This functionality can also be used for existing Trucks / Locations. If an item already exists at the location you are updating, any ‘on hand’ data will not be changed. However, the existing Picking Sequence, Reorder Level and Order Up To values will be reset from this function.

8.6 Inventory Receipts Journal

Corrects a problem where Use Tax was not correctly written to the Tax History table when items were received in this viewer.

If a Work Order is specified in the PO, the system now sets the client site equipment when creating IRJ general item entries.

This release corrects a problem where the received cost was not reset if a user received an inventory item, unreceived it, and re-received it.

The user is now required to specify an accounting period before changing any of the detail lines.

8.6.1 Un-receiving a PO

This release corrects a problem with un-receiving an item on a PO if it was received and then vouchered (but not yet paid) in an accounting period that had since been closed. Although the user could change the effective date and accounting period in the AP Journal, the delete the journal entry (thereby making the PO eligible to be un-received), they received an error message that the line was still vouchered in the Inventory Receipt Journal. The code has been changed so that the PO can now be successfully un-received in this situation.

8.7 Inventory Restock processing

In previous releases, the system deleted closed (completed) Inventory Restock transactions. This resulted in a lack of an appropriate audit trial for this function. The default in this release is to not delete restock records when they are closed.

To set the software to re-enable deletion for closed entries, set the following registry entry:

Id: sys-viewer-vrstck
Setting Key: DeleteClosedTransactions Setting Value: true

A Status filter range has been added to the Inventory Restock List and Inventory Restock Pick List Entry viewers. By default, this range is set to Open. To view both Open and Closed entries, click the All filter button. To view only Closed entries, click the Closed filter button.  

8.7.1 View Inventory Restock List

New Fields: Status: Open Closed
Closed By, Date Closed, and Time Closed

These display-only fields are maintained by the system. A Restock entry will be closed by the system when the Close Pick Ticket button is clicked in the View Inventory Restock Pick List Entry viewer. The Closed By, Date Closed, and Time Closed fields will also be set at this time.

New Tab: IMH

Item Id: Location On Order: To Pick: Transferred: Received:

This tab displays the Inventory History summary for this entry.

When a Restock entry is first created, the On Order value of the Restock To Location, and the To Pick: value of the Order From Location will both default from the Quantity to Pick on the Items tab.

When the Pick List Entry has been completed, the Transferred and Received columns will be updated, and the On Order and To Pick columns revised.

When the Close Pick Tick button is clicked in the Restock Pick Ticket Entry viewer (and the record saved), Inventory History will be adjusted so that any remaining On Order / To Pick quantities are zeroed out.

8.7.2 View Inventory Restock Pick List Entry

New Fields: Status: Open Closed
Closed By, Date Closed, and Time Closed

These display-only fields are maintained by the system. A Restock entry will be closed by the system when the Close Pick Ticket button is clicked. The Closed By, Date Closed, and Time Closed fields will also be set at this time.

Changed Button: Close Pick Ticket

In previous versions, the system deleted Inventory Restock and Inventory Restock Pick Ticket Entry records when the Pick Ticket was closed. In this release, these records are only deleted if the DeleteClosedTransactions is set to true in the sys-viewer-vrstck entry.

8.8 Start Inventory Item Cost Update

Corrects a problem where this function was not updating the Item’s Average Cost field (use for third-party reports) with the ‘calculated’ average cost that is displayed in the Item Viewer.

8.9 IM History

This release corrects a system primitive error that only occurred if sys-startscreen-filter was set for IM History and he/she attempted to create or select a named range.

8.10 Inventory Item Stock Status viewer

This function now excludes non-inventory items. This release also corrects a display issue with the On Hand and Available quantities – these fields now correctly display their values to the right of the decimal point on the selected line.

 

9. Payroll

9.1. PR Adjustment Journal

The ability to post the Earning Type from the Earnings tab is now implemented as a table change.

9.2 Payroll Period

In previous releases, an attempt was made to allow the user to maintain multiple default payroll periods by security. On further consideration, this was decided that this is not a good idea. The validation has been changed so that only one payroll period can be saved as the as the default.

9.3 Report PR Export

Previously, this function attempted to consolidate multiple entries for the same date. In this release, these entries remain broken out as they should be.

The function Report PR Export creates a text file that payroll companies will use to generate paychecks. A report for the user to review/file will also be printed.

Paycor (see user note 9.3.1) and Paychex (9.3.2) versions are currently supported; the report version that is generated is controlled via registry. See user note 9.3.3 for details on updating the Pay Type, Other Rate and Tax Authority records to support this functionality.

9.3.1 Report PR Export (Paycor)

The function Report PR Export creates a text file that Paycor will use to generate paychecks.

Usage:

This functionality requires that a vrgstry.cus file with the necessary permissions be in place. It may be necessary to run Start Update Functions to see this report. Note that this report is part of the image itself and does not have to be imported into the database.

The report function Report PR Export must be run AFTER the Compute Payroll function is run for the desired Payroll Period.

The report will be saved in the directory specified in the sys-pr-export registry as PAYCOR-payrollperiodid.txt (for example, if the payroll period id was 10June, the filename would be PAYCOR-10June.txt).

Important Note on Paycor PRS Codes:
In order for the data in the PR Export Report to be interpreted correctly, the appropriate codes (consult your Paycor documentation) must be present in your data – either in the PRS fields in the Tax Authority, Pay Type, and Other Rate records, or as the Id’s of these record (the record Id will be used if the PRS field is blank).

To Skip Hours Sent to Paycor:
To skip the hours sent to Paycor for a specific Pay Type, enter <skip> in the Pay Type’s PRS Code field.

Report Range:

Payroll Period:
Enter the Payroll Period you wish to run the report for. This field is required.

Employee Id:
An Employee Id or list of Employee Id’s may be specified if you wish to filter this report to specific employees.

Report Format:

Emp #
This column is pulled from the Employee Id.

Reg Hours
Hours entered for this Employee with a Pay Type using the Category ‘Regular’ will be listed in this column.

OT Hours
Hours entered for this Employee with a Pay Type using the Category ‘Overtime’ will be listed in this column.

Coded Hours
Hrs Code
Hours entered for this Employee with a Pay Type using the Categories ‘Doubletime’ or ‘Other’ will be listed in the Coded Hours column. If the PRS Code is set in the Pay Type record, it will be used to complete the Hrs Code column; if the PRS Code field in the Pay Type record is blank, the Pay Type Id will be used to set the Hrs Code column.

Note: the PRS Code should NOT be set for Regular or OT Pay Types.

Errngs1  
Ern Cde 1
The Errngs1 column is only set for bonuses (Labor Journal entries with Earnings but with NO hours) and for Labor Journal reimbursable entries recorded on the Labor Journal Other tab. For reimbursables, the Ern Cde 1 column is set from the PRS Reimb Code (if completed) in the Other Rate record. For Bonuses, the Pay Type PRS Code: field (if completed) will be used to set the Ern Cde 1 column; otherwise, the Pay Type Id will be used.

Exc Rate
This field displays the base rate for Regular, Overtime and Hours. Note that the rate for Overtime Hours and Coded Hours is NOT marked up in this report: it will be handled by Paycor.

Exc Dept
This column specifies the local Tax Auth this line is associated with. If the PRS Tax Code is set in the Tax Authority record, it will be used to complete the Exc Dept column; if the PRS Tax Code field in the Tax Authority Type record is blank, the Tax Authority Id will be used to set the Exc Dept column.

Registry:

This registry setting is required for the Paycor reporting functionality.

Id: sys-pr-export

Setting Key: Format  Setting Value: Paycor

This registry option specifies that the Paycor formatting will be used in the Report Payroll Export function.

Setting Key: PathName Setting Value: path

This registry option specifies the complete path of the directory to which SAM Pro will export the Paycor file.

9.3.2 Report PR Export (Paychex)

The function Report PR Export creates a text file that Paychex will use to generate paychecks as well as a printed, formatted version that you may retain for your records.

Usage:

This functionality requires that a vrgstry.cus file with the necessary permissions be in place. It may be necessary to run Start Update Functions to see this report. Note that this report is part of the image itself and does not have to be imported into the database.

The report function Report PR Export must be run AFTER the Compute Payroll function is run for the desired Payroll Period.

When you print the report, a formatted version of the report will be printed, AND the text version of the report will be saved in the directory specified in the sys-pr-export registry as client#-ta.txt (for example, if your client number (as specified in the sys-pr-export registry) is 12345, the filename would be 12345-ta.txt. This text file should be used as directed by Paychex when reporting on your company’s payroll.

Important Note on Paychex PRS Codes:
In order for the data in the PR Export Report to be interpreted correctly, the appropriate codes (consult your Paychex documentation) must be present in your data – either in the PRS fields in the Tax Authority, Pay Type, and Other Rate records, or as the Id’s of these records (the record Id will be used if the PRS field is blank). Note that Paychex PRS codes are up to two characters in length.

Report Range:

Payroll Period:
Enter the Payroll Period you wish to run the report for. This field is required.

Employee Id:
An Employee Id or list of Employee Id’s may be specified if you wish to filter this report to specific employees.

Report Format:

Emp #
This column is pulled from the Employee Id.

Earnings Code:
Depending on the type of line (pay, bonus or reimbursables), this field will be set from either the Pay Type (pay and bonuses) or the Other Rate (reimbursables) records. Consult your Paychex documentation for the correct 2 character codes.

If the Earnings Code is set from the Pay Type, the PRS Pay Code field will be used (if completed). If this field is blank, the Pay Type Id will be used to set the Earnings Code.

If the Earnings Code is set from the Other Rate, the PRS Reimb Code field will be used (if completed). If this field is blank, the Other Rate Id will be used to set the Earnings Code.

Hours Override Rate
Hours entered for this Employee at this pay rate. For Overtime and Doubletime hours, the Override Rate is already marked up by SAM Pro (be sure this is specified to Paychex).

Amount  
The Amount column is set for bonuses (Labor Journal entries with Earnings but with NO hours) and for Labor Journal reimbursable entries recorded on the Labor Journal Other tab. For reimbursables, the Earnings Code column is set from the PRS Reimb Code (if completed) in the Other Rate record. For Bonuses, the Pay Type PRS Code: field (if completed) will be used to set the Earnings column; otherwise, the Pay Type Id will be used.

Override State
This column specifies the state Tax Authority this line is associated with. If the PRS Tax Code is set in the Tax Authority record, it will be used to complete the Override State column; if the PRS Tax Code field in the Tax Authority Type record is blank, the state Tax Authority Id will be used to set this column.

Override Local
This column specifies the local Tax Authority this line is associated with. If the PRS Tax Code is set in the Tax Authority record, it will be used to complete the Override Local column; if the PRS Tax Code field in the Tax Authority Type record is blank, the local Tax Authority Id will be used to set this column.

Registry:

This registry setting is required for the Paychex reporting functionality.

Id: sys-pr-export

Setting Key: Format  Setting Value: Paychex

This registry option specifies that the Paycor formatting will be used in the Report Payroll Export function.

Setting Key: PathName Setting Value: path

This registry option specifies the complete path of the directory to which SAM Pro will export the Paychex file.

Setting Key: ClientNumber Setting Value: client#

This registry option specifies the client number assigned to your firm by Paychex. It will be used to generate part of the filename of the Paychex file.

9.3.3 Records Setup for Report Payroll Export (Paychex and Paycor)

Pay Type Record:

New Field: PRS Pay Code

Paycor Users:
Hours entered with a Pay Type using the Categories ‘Doubletime’ or ‘Other’ are listed as Coded Hours and require a Paycor code (consult your Paycor documentation for a list of valid codes). If this field completed, it will be used to set this code; if this field is blank, the Pay Type Id will be used instead.  

For Bonuses, the Pay Type PRS Pay Code: field (if completed) will be used to set the Ern Cde 1 column; otherwise, the Pay Type Id will be used.

Note: the PRS Pay Code should NOT be set for Regular or OT Pay Types.

To Skip Hours Sent to Paycor:
To skip the hours sent to Paycor for a specific Pay Type, enter <skip> in the PRS Pay Code field.

Paychex Users:
Paychex requires that Pay Types of all Pay Categories (Regular, Overtime, Doubletime and Other) are associated with a valid Paychex Earnings Code. The PRS Pay Code field will be used (if completed); if this field is blank, the Pay Type Id will be used to set the Earnings Code. Consult your Paychex documentation for a list of valid, 2 character Earnings Codes.

Other Rate Record:
New Field - PRS Reimb Code:

Paycor Users:
Other Rates that may be used for reimbursable expenses for employees (entered on the Labor Journal Other tab) must have a valid Paycor Earnings code. This field (if completed) is used to set the Ern Cde 1 in the Paycor report; if it is blank, the Other Rate Id will be used. Consult your Paycor documentation for a list of valid Earnings codes.

Paychex Users:
Other Rates that may be used for reimbursable expenses for employees (entered on the Labor Journal Other tab) must have a valid Paychex Earnings code. This field (if completed) is used to set the Earnings Code field in the Paychex report; if it is blank, the Other Rate Id will be used. Consult your Paychex documentation for a list of valid Earnings codes.

Tax Authority Record:
New Field - PRS Tax Code:

Paycor Users:
The Exc Dept column on the Paycor report specifies the local Tax Auth a line is associated with. If the PRS Tax Code is set in this local Tax Authority record, it will be used to complete the Exc Dept column; if the PRS Tax Code field in the Tax Authority Type record is blank, the Tax Authority Id will be used to set the Exc Dept column. It is not necessary to set this field for State, Federal or Other Tax Authorities as these are not needed for Paycor reporting.

Paychex Users:
Paychex uses the information in State and Local Tax Authority records to populate the Override State and Override Local columns of its report. If the PRS Tax Code is set in the Tax Authority record, it will be used to complete the applicable Override State or Override Local column; if the PRS Tax Code field in the Tax Authority Type record is blank, the Tax Authority Id will be used to set the State or Local Override column.

9.4 Start CPP Time Import

Purpose:

This Starter provides an import function for adding time and job cost information collected by Complete Payroll Processing’s (CPP) Web based time sheet program to the Sam Pro Labor Journal.

Usage:

The Starter function allows a user to browse to a CPP populated .csv formatted file, open the file and have its contents imported into a data edit screen for review, possible correction and ultimate import into Sam Pro. Once imported, the time data will be editable via the standard Sam Pro Labor Journal just like time manually entered into the Labor Journal. There will be a unique Labor Journal transaction for each employee/payroll period combination specified in the import file. There is no planned functionality for “un-importing” or reversing the data after a successful import is completed.

IMPORT FILE SPECIFICATION

The file definition for the .csv (comma separated ASCII) file is as follows:

Field 1: Hours- 999.99 (required)

Field 2: Effective Date- yyyymmdd (required)

Field 3: Work Order Id-up to 10 char. alpha numeric.

Field 4: Job Id-up to 10 char. alpha numeric (required if work order id not specified)

Field 5: Job Cost Code-up to 30 char. alpha numeric (required if work order id not specified)

Field 6: Job Cost Category Id- up to 10 char. alpha numeric (required)

Field 7: Pay Type Id- up to 10 char. alpha numeric (required)

Field 8: Payroll Period Id- up to 10 char. alpha numeric (required)

Field 9: Employee Id- up to 10 char. alpha numeric (required)

Any field that currently defaults when entering time into the Labor Journal but not specified in the file layout will continue to default based on current default rules. For example, the Job Billing Item which isn’t being supplied in the import file will default from the Job Billing Item stored in the Job Cost Code specified in the file. The Labor Rate Id, also absent from the import file, will default from the stored Labor Rate Id in the specified employee record.

Registry:

Specify File Location

Id: sys-start-scpptmeimprt Name: Start CPP Time Import

Setting Key: CSVDirectory Setting Value: path

If not set, the default is the SAMPro base directory (containing the v.exe).

Specify Labor Rate Override

This option allows the user to specify the Labor Rate Id to use when a specific Pay Type Id is specified in the import file. If no cross reference is specified in the registry, the Labor Rate Id (absent from the import file), will default from the stored Labor Rate Id in the specified employee record.

Id: sys-time-import-Labor-Rates
Setting Key: PayTypeID Setting Value: LaborRateId

 Example: Setting Key: reg-admin Setting Value: admin

FUNCTIONALITY

When a user launches the new starter function a standard Windows browser launches so that the user can navigate to the location of the import file. When user selects the file and open, the system will generate an editable selection screen containing a two-row entry for each row found in the import file. The top row will display only the values found in the import file; the bottom row will display editable, validated matches found in the Sam Pro database.

Do Skip
Check Do to process this entry; Check Skip to skip this entry.

Emp. Id Import Hrs Eff. Date PayPrd Id: WO Id: Import Job Id: Cost Code Cost Cat: Import Pay Type:

The top row is from the import file, and may not be edited.

Emp. Id Hours: Eff. Date Payroll Period: WO Id: Job Id: Cost Code Cost Cat: Pay Type Id:

The bottom row list the Sam Pro defaults, and the WO Id, Job Id, Job Cost Code, Job Cost Category and Pay Type Id may be edited. If Sam Pro does not have a matching database value for a specified field in the import file (i.e. invalid Work Order, Job, Cost Code, Cost Category, Employee, Effective Date, Payroll Period or Pay Type) the Sam Pro default line value will be left blank and importing of the line will be prevented until a user manually provides a valid value.

If the system finds an exact duplicate entry already existing in the Sam Pro Labor Journal, the word “Duplicate” will be displayed on the row and the Do check box will be automatically un-checked. The user can override this condition by re-checking the Do box.

After verifying the import information and making any necessary corrections the user will push the GO icon and the system will create and post all necessary Labor Journal entries in Sam Pro. There will be one Labor Journal Transaction Id for each employee/Payroll Period combination found in the import file. A message “Successfully imported” will be displayed.

9.5 Time Entry Wizard

Purpose:

The Time Entry Wizard allows labor that is being charged to a work order to be entered in a user-friendly start time and end time basis and have the system work out the details of regular, overtime and double-time labor and pay rates. When time is posted from the Wizard to the Work Order, the system automatically calculates straight time, time and a half (o/t) and double time for both pay and bill hours based on a shift definition defined in the Technician record and regular time billing period defined in the Work Order’s Job record.

Usage:

A customization file is required to run this module.

Setup:

Job Record:

Customization - New Fields on Job Invoicing Tab:

Regular Billing Start Time:
Regular Billing End Time:
These fields default what are considered regular hours for this job for week days that are not defined as holidays on the calendar. The Wizard will use the applicable Labor Rate (Regular, Overtime, Doubletime and Travel Regular, Overtime and Doubletime) on the Technician Defaults tab for Billing based on these hours.

Saturday Included:
Sunday Included:
Checking these boxes enables Saturday and/or Sunday work to be defined as Regular Billing when determining the Labor Rate to use.

Technician Record: Defaults Tab

Start Time:
Quit Time:
These fields provide the shift information for regular time for this Technician which Pay Type to use (Pay Type Id:, Overtime, or Doubletime).

Customization –

New Fields on Technician Defaults Tab:
 Labor Rate Id’s for Travel Time:
 Regular:
 Overtime:
 Doubletime:

These fields are used for defaulting Travel Labor Rate Ids for regular, overtime and double time for the Time Entry wizard. Note that the Labor Rates for work hours (for Regular, Overtime and Doubletime) must also be completed on this tab.

Registry:

 Id: yourcompany-calendar

Setting Key: date in yyyy-mm-dd

Setting Value: Name of Holiday

The holidays defined by this registry will be considered double time pay days by the Technician Time Entry Wizard.

Example: Setting Key: 2010-12-25 Setting Value: Christmas

Labor Rate Record:

The Job Cost Category field should be completed for Labor Rates used for Technician Time Entry.

Payroll Period:

A default Payroll Period must be specified. The Technician Time Entry Wizard will ONLY post time to the work order if the effective day falls within the Default Payroll Period.

Running the Time Entry Wizard:

The Technician Time Entry Wizard is launched by clicking the Enter Time button on the Work Order’s Main tab (requires a special v.cus file).

Validation checks for closed Accounting Periods and Closed Payroll period. If Payroll has already been computed, a warning is issued and stops the posting wizard, however, after acknowledging the message and returning to the wizard you can select to FINISH and it will post the hours.  Any subsequent use of the wizard will be fine (no warning message).  The wizard also checks for printed/paid employees. In this case, the message states employee has been paid this is not allowed and you cannot by-pass or post the hours. 

The following fields should be completed on the wizard:

Date Worked:
The day the work or travel was performed: this must fall within the date range of the default Payroll Period to be entered in the Wizard.

Start Time: End Time:
The Start and End Time (entered in military time) worked or traveled.

Technician:
The Technician whose time you are entered; you may double-click to select from a list of Technicians assigned to this Work Order. Note that although you may type in the Id of a Technician that is not assigned to the Work Order, the post will fail if the Technician Id is not entered correctly.

Client Site Equipment Id:
The Equipment the Technician worked on; you may double-click to select from a list of Equipment listed on this Work Order. Note that the Wizard will not let you enter an Equipment Id that is not listed on the Work Order’s Equipment tab.

Travel?
Check this box (by double-clicking or pressing the Spacebar when the caret is on it) if you are entering Travel time on this line.

Shift Override?
Check this box (by double-clicking or pressing the Spacebar when the caret is on it) if the work or travel time you entered should be handled as Regular Time (work or travel), regardless of the Start and End Times that are set in the Job record.

Buttons:

Cancel: click the Cancel button to cancel out of the Wizard without posting any lines to the Work Order.

Remove Line: click this button to clear the selected line. Any fields that defaulted in will do so again.

Finish: When you click this button, the lines that you entered will be added to the Work Order Labor tab, provided that no errors were found. If necessary, the system will automatically create as many work and travel lines as needed in the Work Order based on

The Date, Start and End Times you entered

Whether you flagged lines as Travel or Shift Override

The Information in the Job (Regular Billing Start and End Times, Include Saturday / Sunday)

The Start / End Time in the Technician Record

The Company Calendar holiday information (based on the Registry entry)

Important: You must SAVE the Work Order to retain the lines that you posted to the Labor tab from the Technician Time Entry wizard.

Technical Details:

When above information is entered in the wizard, the system will calculate regular, overtime and double time pay and bill hours based the following rules and write to the Labor tab of the work order:

Any hours worked before the Technician Start Time or after the Technician End Time defined in the Technician record will be considered overtime pay and default the calculated hours and Technician Overtime Pay Type Id found in the Technician record and other entered information to the Labor entry screen on the Work Order.

Any hours worked before the Regular Billing Start Time or after the Regular Billing End Time found in the Job referenced in the Work Order will be considered overtime billing and default the calculated hours and the Technician Overtime Labor Rate Id found in the Technician record along with other entered information to the Labor entry screen on the Work Order.

If any of the hours worked are on Saturday, they will be considered overtime pay and overtime bill unless the referenced Job has the "Saturday Included" box checked which will then calculate overtime pay but regular time bill if hours are within Reg. Billing Start/End times defined in Job record. If any of the hours worked are on Sunday, they will be considered overtime pay and overtime bill unless the referenced Job has the "Sunday Included" box checked which will then calculate overtime pay but regular time bill if hours are within Reg. Billing Start/End times defined in the Job record.

If any of the hours worked are on a defined company holiday or a Sunday, they will be considered double time pay and double time bill hours.

If Travel check box is marked, default the appropriate Travel Labor Rate Id from Technician Record.

If Shift Override check box is marked, treat hours worked as regular time.

9.6 PR Check

The Payroll Period Start and End dates, and the Check Date, have been added to the Recap portion of the Payroll Check stubs.

This release adds support for the option to suppress PTO section on MICR printers when the Registry Id is GL Bank Account specific.

This release corrects a PR Check PTO Summary issue in recent images. Holiday hours (for example) were being incorrectly included in the PTO summary as negative hours.

The Range field has been removed from the report range screen.

9.7 Void PR Checks

Validation has been added to prevent the user from voiding reconciled PR checks. In previous releases, the user was warned that a check was reconciled, but could in fact complete the void process.

9.8 Earnings

Validation has been added to make the user aware that Earnings records defined as 'non-taxable wages' do not make sense.

9.9 Generate Recurring Labor Journal

This release corrects an hours calculation error that occurred if the Cycle range was completed.

Corrects problem in recent versions where Labor Journal Entries were not generated by this function.

The Help=>About This Product window accessed from this screen now displays the correct Function Id.

9.10 Labor Journal

The Labor Journal now supports prevailing wage calculations on lines that are work order based. Previously, only Job-based lines were supported.

9.10.1 Hours Tab

This release corrects the Hours tab so the Job Id field no longer overlaps the Job Cost Code.

Changed Field: Equipment Id
If the sys-ffv-global setting 'DefaultEquipmentFromWorkorder' is set to false, the user is now allowed to set the Equipment Id back to blank. If this registry option is not present or set to true, the Equipment Id must be completed if a Work Order Id is referenced.

9.10.2 Other Tab

Changed Field: Equipment Id
If the sys-ffv-global setting 'DefaultEquipmentFromWorkorder' is set to false, the user is now allowed to set the Equipment Id back to blank. If this registry option is not present or set to true, the Equipment Id must be completed if a Work Order Id is referenced.

9.11 ADP Payroll Import

This enhancement allows the import of files where the GL Entity field is blank.

9.12 Employee Record

9.12.1 Other Tab

New Field: Annual Hours
This new field allows the Annual Standard Hours used in various payroll calculations for salaried workers to be employee-specific. When the new field’s value is zero, the system uses the global standard (as set by the StandardAnnualHours option in sys-ffv-global-setting (see user note 2.8.7), or by 2080 (if this registry entry does not exist). This enhancement allows the user to control the Standard Annual Hours so that the pay rate written to job history will use the ‘correct’ rate (Salary / Standard Hours) without having to run Compute Payroll to have the pay rate updated to the correct effective rate (= Salary / Pay Periods / Hours Entered).

9.12.2 Checks Tab

This release filters the Checks list to exclude rows where both the Payroll Period and Effective Date are empty.

 

9.13 Canadian T4 Forms

Box 24 will now be blank if it is the same as Box 14.
Box 26 will now be forced to blank.

9.14 “Percent of Wages” Vacation Accruals

This enhancement implements vacations accruals with a 'percent of wages' option for Canadian Payroll scenarios and possibly for certain US setups. This enhancement also excludes vacation pay used in the current period from vacation accrual calculations for current period.

Important Note:
SAMPRO does NOT have support for multiple percentages per employee in a single pay period. All percentage rate changes must coincide with the starting date of a Pay Period.

9.14.1 Employee Record

New Field: PTO Tab – Prcnt:
The percent of wages field (Prcnt:) allows this Paid Time Off to be calculated as a Percent of Wages rather than a number of Hours. Any one PTO line can have either Hours or Percent but not both.

9.14.2 Pay Type Record

Category Field – New Options: Vacation Holiday Other

These fields are used in the Compute Payroll process that calculates percent-of-wage PTO earnings accruals for Employees with a PTO line having the new Percent field filled in.  Validation code has been added to enforce proper use of Hours Type and Category combinations as follows:

When Hours Type is 'Worked', Category must be 'Regular', 'Overtime', or 'Doubletime'.

When Hours Type is 'PTO', Category must be 'Holiday', 'Sick', 'Vacation' or 'Other'.

When Hours Type is 'Other', Category must be 'Other'.

New Field: PTO Accrual Method: Hours Percent CurrentPayRate

This field allows for specification of the PTO Accrual Method.  Three options are currently supported.

'Hours' is the default.

'Percent' is the new method implemented for Canadian Vacation pay.

'CurrentPayRate' is the alternate methodology implemented with the registry entry ShowPTOAvailableAs=dollar in sys-report-rprchck.

The Pay Type viewer will default the methodology to 'Percent' for Canadian v.cus file users whenever the Pay Type's Category is set to Vacation for new or changed records. Note that Pay Types that existed before these enhancements should be manually updated.

The Employee viewer now has code that validates the use of the PTO amounts (hours or percent) relative to the Pay Type's Accrual Method.

9.14.3 Compute Payroll

This enhancement has been implemented in the Compute Payroll process to calculate percent-of-wage PTO earnings accruals.  This code is triggered by the Employee PTO line having the new Percent field filled in.  The percentage is applied to the employee's Modified Gross Wages for the period.  Modified Gross Wages are defined as the employee's gross wages less any wages classified as the same Pay Type Category (i.e. 'Vacation') as the PTO.

In other words, don't accrue vacation earnings against vacation being paid out.  The key to this is matching up the Pay Type Category selections.

The resulting calculations are stored in the PRH Hours table's Earnings Accrued field.  A new field has been added to PRH Hours to store the Percent captured from the Employee PTO line at the time of the compute. 

New Field Range Screen (Canadian Customers Only):

Paid Time Off: Accrue?

As with previous versions of SAMPRO, PTO accruals are calculated during the Compute PR process and are subject to the Accrue PTO flag from the Pay Period record.  Some special situations can be controlled by creating special Pay Periods and not selecting the Accrue PTO option.  A Christmas Bonus payroll would be one such example.

In other situations it might be more beneficial to have Accrue PTO selected in the Pay Period but have the option to override it during the Compute PR process.  The Compute PR input screen has been changed (Canadian customers only) to allow an override of the Pay Period's Accrue PTO option. 

9.14.4 Payroll Adjustment Journal

Hours Tab New Field: %Accr
To facilitate the loading of beginning balances, the Payroll Journal has been modified to allow entry of the Accrued Percent.  Values entered into this new field are posted to the corresponding field in the PRH Hours table. 

9.14.5 Payroll Period

Changed Field: Accrue PTO Hours?
The field previously labeled 'Accrue PTO Hours?' has been changed to the more generic 'Accrue PTO?'.  Note that the functionality has NOT changed. 

9.15 Worker’s Comp State

New Field: WC Gross from Prevailing Wages: Exclude Fringes
Workers comp 'wages' typically should not include any amounts related to prevailing wage fringes (entered in the Fringe Rate field of the Job’s Prevailing Wages tab).  This new behavior is activated by flagging the Exclude Fringes field in the appropriate Workers Comp State records.

9.16 Deductions Viewer – Support for Third Party Sick Pay

This enhancement supports coding for third-party sick pay. If the W-2 Category field is set to 12:J, anytime an amount is found for Box 12 Code J, the system will mark the Box 13 check box labeled Third-party Sick Pay on the W2.

9.17 Report PR W-2

This release supports the formatting changes in the W3 form printed for 2011 taxes.

An earlier release increased the size of Box 12 Code Fields from 1 to 2 characters. These codes are specified in the W-2 Category fields of the Deduction and Earning viewers. This enhancement was specifically added to support the after tax contributions to Roth retirement plans which requires codes AA or BB.

9.17.1 W-2 Category Fields Added to Tax Authority and Tax Table

Tax Authority – General Ledger Tab

New Field: W-2 Category Employee

This field supersedes the use of the User 1 field for the handling of box 12 and 14 codes, and for titles for unemployment insurance. The User 1 field is still supported if this field is blank. 

New Field: W-2 Category Employer
Reserved for Future Use.

Tax Table

New Field: W-2 Category Employee

This field supersedes the use of the User 1 field for the handling of box 12 and 14 codes, and for titles for unemployment insurance. The User 1 field is still supported if this field is blank. 

New Field: W-2 Category Employer
Reserved for Future Use.

9.18 W2 Magnetic Media

Box 12 Support: This enhancement supports the inclusion the W2 Category fields in Deductions & Earnings records in the Report W2 Electronic File functionality. Previously, only 401k deductions were supported.

Revised Report: RW2EF.rpt: The revised Report W2 Electronic File, dated February 17, 2011, must be imported to support the new Box 12 functionality. This report is suitable for version 7.2 and up.

The revised Report W2 Electronic File (RWEF.rpt), dated 3/1/2011, also supports the new Box 12 functionality for Third Party Sick Pay. The Third Party Sick Pay flag in type RW records will be set if any PR History is found with a W2 Category of 12:J.

In this version, a registry entry is now required to set Position 174 on the RE line as the default has been changed to blank to accommodate special processing for the state of Maryland. The following option is now required for federal processing with this report.

9.19 Compute PR (Canadian PR Issues)

This release corrects the application of CPP, EI and PPIP credits; eliminate excessive use of rounding, and implements use of standard tax credit.

9.19 Remote Time Entry

A new version of the Remote Time Entry executable (time_expense_viewer.exe), dated 2/11/2011, supports the printing of reports under newer OS such as Windows 7. Contact Support if this updated file is needed.

 

10. Quote Master

10.1 Quote Viewer

The sys-viewer-vqte option ApprovalWizardDefaultTechStatus is used to set the default status in the Approval Wizard's Technician pane. In recent 7.3 releases, this option worked correctly UNLESS the technician was a subcontractor. In this release, the software has been corrected so that the ApprovalWizardDefaultTechStatus is also used for subcontractor technicians.

Corrects an issue in recent releases where Notes attached to the Site were displayed when you clicked the Quote viewer’s Notes button: Notes attached to the Quote are now displayed.

The registry option SetSourceWOStatusOnApproval was inadvertently omitted in early 7.3 releases. This functionality has been restored.

If Outlook is enabled in the sys-email registry entry, the regular SAM Pro email form will appear when the Vendor Approval button is clicked.

When you begin to add a Quote in Quote Master, the system will now ask if you wish to view the Notes associated with the Site you selected (either directly or by choosing a source Work Order). The registry options described in user notes 2.3.1 and 2.3.2 may be used to alter this behavior.

10.1.1 Main Tab

Updated buttons that are easier to read on high-resolution monitors have been added to this tab:

New Field: Job Id:
This field defaults from the Work Order (if one was selected) or may be selected by the user to provide the default Job when the Quotemaster Wizard is run. This Job’s Material Price Level will used for default pricing on the Quote’s Inventory tab, overriding the Client Site Material Price. If the Job Id is not completed, the system will continue to use the Site’s Material Price Level.

If the Job Id is selected manually, the system now defaults in the Report Id, Quote Notes and Small Print from Job's Site, and the Branch Id will be set from the Job (if completed in the Job record) or from the Job’s Site (if the Branch is blank in the Job but completed in the Site).

10.1.2 Revenue Adjustments Tab

Improved handling of Yes/No answers to “Revenue Changes Detected: do you want to adjust the revenue” prompt. Now, if you answer Yes, the system will update the Revenue Adjustment tab for you. If you answer No, the Revenue Adjustment tab will not be revised by the system.

When the Revenue Adjustment Id is changed on a Scope and it detects there are already revenue adjustment lines, the user is warned to remove the Revenue Adjustment Lines before trying to change the Revenue Adjustment Id.

On fixed price scopes, and using a Revenue Adjustment with the Totals field set, the TaxType Id is now set to ‘ n/a’. Previously, it was not set at all.

10.1.3 Scope Tab

This fix corrects a problem in recent 7.3 release where blank lines in the Quote were not being deleted. Note that additional validation has been added so that the user is not allowed to blank the Option Code; a message is displayed advising the user to use the Delete Line button instead.

When entering a flat rate to a quote scope line, the scope of services in the quote scope line now always defaults from the corresponding field in the flat range category.

Equipment Id:
The system no longer defaults in the Equipment Id if multiple Equipment lines exist on the WO. The Equipment Id will only default if a single piece of Equipment appears on the source Work Order.

Copy From Button:
A new button, Copy From, has been added to the Quote Scope line.  Pushing the button launches a new wizard that lets the user complete the selected scope line by copying the details from existing scope lines AND the Labor, Inventory, Material, Sub and Other lines associated with these Scope Options.

Note that the user is responsible for managing revenue adjustments: these will NOT be generated if a line is copied.

To use this feature:
Your Quote must have one or more options that you wish to copy from. Next, add a new Scope line, complete its Option Code, change (or select) the Equipment Id if needed, and Save the Quote.

Select the Scope Option line you just added, and then click the Copy From button. The Copy From Options Wizard will appear:

Copy From Options Wizard – Select Option Codes Screen:

Ok – Option Code – Quote Amount – Fixed Price – Scope of Services

This screen allows you to select one or more existed options to update the selected scope option with – flag the OK box to select the Option Codes to Copy From. If more than one Option Code is selected, system will include details from all selected options and combine the Scope of Services text.

Click the Next button to continue.

Copy From Wizard Options Wizard – Edit Option Screen

Fixed Price:
If this is a Fixed Price quote, this field will default from the Option(s) you selected in the previous screen. It may be adjusted if needed.

Note: If you are cloning from a non-fixed fee quote and enter a fixed fee in the wizard, the prices on the detail lines for the new option will be cleared.

Quote Amount:
 If this is NOT a Fixed Price quote, this field will default from the detail lines associated with the Option(s) you selected in the previous screen. It is display only; any changes to the amount should be made to new option’s detail lines after running this wizard.

Scope of Services: This field defaults from the Option(s) you selected in the previous screen. It may be adjusted if needed.

Click the Finish button to complete the copy or Cancel to cancel this operation.

10.1.4 Inventory Tab

The Inventory Item Id is now a required field.

The Vendor Part number now correctly writes to the corresponding field in the PO that is created when the approval wizard is run. The Vendor Part Number on the PO also updates the Inventory Item’s Vendor tab.

10.1.5 Cloning a Quote / Additional Validation

This release adds enhanced validation so that the Quote's Client Site CANNOT be changed if any Scope or Equipment Tab lines have the Equipment Id completed. This includes the user changing the Site directly, or changing the source wo or job to one referencing a different site.

The software supports the ability to ‘clone’ an existing quote’ When the user enters 'new' in the quote id of an existing quote and tabs out of the field, a new quote record is generated with the following changes implemented:

On the Scope tab, set all options to Open, clears the WO Id and Job Billing Id (if they exist), as well as the Opened, Accepted, Approved and Declined Fields.
On the Inventory Tab, clear the PO Id and Vendor Quote No.
On the Material Tab, clear the PO Id and Vendor Quote No.
On the Subcontractor Tab, clear the PO Id and Vendor Quote No.
On the Notes tab (header info) set the Status to Open, Status Category to Active, and Status date to today.

The new quote may now be edited (subject to the enhanced validations) and saved. The system will assign the appropriate Quote Id when record is saved.

10.1.6 Notes Tab

Quote User fields 3-10 have been added to the Notes tab. Previously, only two User fields were available.

10.2 Quote Master Approval Wizard

The work order registry option DenyChangesToQuoteMasterLines prevented Quote Master from writing to work orders in recent release. This problem has been corrected.

In this release, the approval wizard sums the Subcontractor lines so that only one line for each Subcontractor will be written to the work order’s Tech tab, and the quote will post successfully.

The system now warns the user if the Technician line being generated is for the same date/technician combination that already exists in the Work Order. If the user chooses to continue, the Technician line in the Work Order will be replaced by the Wizard’s Tech line.

If the Client is on Credit Hold when a new work order is generated, the Tech Tab child lines are set as they should be for the type of technician they are assigned to, and the Work Order’s Escalation Status is set to Credit Hold and Credit Hold box is flagged. A Credit Manager must clear the Credit Hold box on the Work Order before it will appear on the Dispatch Board, or be released to a technician.

Previously, if an Accounting Period was not flagged as Default, the posting of PO's from the Quotemaster Wizard failed. The following enhancement (when generated PO’s):

1. Uses the default Accounting Period (if it exists),
2. If no default exists, it uses the 'first' active accounting period with today's date in the date range. 
3. If both of the above fail, the Wizard warns the user, and the PO post fails as in previous releases.

This release corrects a problem that occurred if the user immediately logged out of SAM Pro after the Approval Wizard was run: a new Work Order was created, and nothing else (no PO, no update to the Quote).  Also in this release, new Work Orders generated by Quote Master will have their Description field set to 'Quote: #####'.

If a quote was set up to generate multiple PO's; only the last one (on the QM Wizard PO screen) was actually created if the user made no changes when the wizard was running. This has been corrected.

In this release, 'waitcustapprvl' from has been removed from the default 'AutoUpdateWOTechStatusIgnore' list so that their status can be appropriately updated.

10.2.1 New Option: Create Job Budget

A new option, Create Job Budget, has been added to the Quote Master Wizard. When selected, it will update the Job’s Budget tab. When new option is selected, the Quote Master data entry forms follow in this order:

Default Job Structure:
Previously, the Default Job Structure screen information defaulted from the Job Id from the Work Order record. It now uses the new Job Id from the Quote record if it has been entered. 

Job Budget Defaults
Data from the Job Budget Defaults form is written to the Job Budget tab (and Job History) as budgeted cost.

Billing Defaults (when Scope has Fixed Price)

10.3 Quote Master Flat Rate Wizard

Selecting a Flat Rate has been wizardized. Additional forms have been added to the old Flat Rate import screen for Labor, Material and Inventory (based on the Flat Rate Category child tables) to allow the user to edit hours and quantities before the lines are imported into the Quote. These additional screens are accessed by clicking the Next button on the Flat Rate Wizard.

If the user simply wishes to import the flat rate without adjusting the hours or quantities, the Finish button may be clicked. Note that the Flat Rate’s Pretax Price (if specified) will be used to set the Fixed Price on the Quote Scope.

11. Service Management

11.1 Work Order Viewer

The Work Order Closing Call Script and Service Recommendation functions have been reinstated, correcting a problem in earlier versions of 7.3.

WO Inventory (and other journals): This release implements enhanced journal validation logic to prevent sporadic posting reversals with inappropriate Transaction Ids. If this situation is about to occur, the erroneous reversal is suppressed AND an error is written to the error log noting the reversal suppression. This release also corrects a sporadic Inventory History reversal handling issue when the WO Inventory tab includes a combination of quoted and unquoted lines.

Due to the work in the above enhancement, a registry entry is now required to display the WO Inventory / IM History Tab Mismatch Alert: see user note 2.4.7 for details.

If you click the sidebar button Create PO, and the system date (today) exceeds the Work Order header’s Job Date Closed, the message ‘Cannot Create Job PO for closed Job’ will be displayed; the Purchase Order viewer will not be launched.  

If you click the sidebar button Material Requisitioning, and the system date (today) exceeds the Work Order header Job Date Closed, the message ‘Cannot Run Material Requisitioning for closed Job’ will be displayed; and the Requisitioning wizard will not be launched.  

When processing Required Resource Inventory, the Import Cost Wizard now skips truck stock that has already been entered on the Work Order Inventory tab.

In previous releases, the blank Work Order record’s Purchases, Quote and TechAnywhere tabs were filtered to NO Work Order Id instead of showing nothing (or 0's). This has been corrected.

If the sys-viewer-vwrkordr registry option DefaultJobByEquipmentId is set to true, the system now only changes the job when the Equipment Id is changed.

Single Quotes (‘) entered in the Work Performed field of the Equipment tab are no longer doubled when they are written to the Invoice Description of Work Performed when the Build Description button is clicked.

11.1.0 Main Tab

The WO Printer and Event buttons have been moved to the side button bar. The Ok To Invoice and Preview buttons have been moved to the Invoicing Tab.

11.1.1 New Child Tab – COD

Note: also see user note 11.1.10 for COD Enhancements.

Purpose:

This tab allows multiple payments (such as part check, part cash) to be recorded on a work order. Entries on this tab should ONLY be made for COD work orders, NEVER for billable work orders. If TechAnywhere is implemented, this tab will be populated when the TechAnywhere Post is run for COD Work Orders.

The following should be set up correctly in order for entries on this tab to be processed correctly:

- The Work Order’s Job should reference an AR Terms record that is correctly configured for COD’s.

- The COD box in the Job’s AR Terms record must be checked. The AR Terms Id defaults from the Job when the Work Order is loaded, so the Job’s AR Terms record must be set correctly from the beginning.

Usage:

When generating a Service Invoice:

If one or more COD child tab lines are present where the Payment, Amount and Reference No. are completed, but the Invoice Id and CRJ fields have NOT yet been filled in by the system, the system will use the information on the COD child tab.

If no lines (or only lines with the Invoice Id and CR Trx Id fields completed) are present in the COD child tab, the information on the parent COD tab is used.

Note : TechAnywhere COD’s:
For COD Invoices generated from TechAnywhere, the appropriate AR Sales AND Cash Receipts entries will be generated when the TechAnywhere Post is run. In addition, a copy of the Invoice the Tech printed for the customer will be downloaded from TechAnywhere and attached to the Work Order (but not the Client).

Note: If this Tab is not Visible
When this setting is present, the new WO-COD child tab is not visible and therefore not available.

Id: sys-start-ssrvcebllngcmpte Setting Key: UseSJForCOD Setting Value: true

Important Fields:

Payment Type Id:
Enables the user to record the exact type of COD payment (e.g.,, cash, check, credit card, etc.). A payment type of “none” is useful for estimates and no charges.

Amount:
The amount of the payment received.

Reference No.:
Typically, the check number or credit approval number.

Invoice Id:
This display-only field will be completed by the system when the invoice is generated.

GL Account Id:
This display-only field defaults from the Payment Type Id.

CRJ Trx Id:
This display-only field will be completed by the system when the invoice is printed and the Cash Receipt entry is generated (manual entries) or posted from TechAnywhere.

11.1.2 Required Resource Tab

Registry Entries:

To Default Vendor:

The Vendor (in the inventory item record) does not default when you enter a Required Resource line manually or as a result of generating a PM Work Order with flagged parts - the idea being that aggregation will be used. Customers that wish to generate individual po's for the work orders required resources must individually set the Vendor Id in each line. The registry entry detailed in user note 2.8.3 changes this behavior so that the system will default in the Vendor Id from the Inventory record (if set) on manual Work Order Required Resource entries and on Create PM Workorders.

Do Not Write Required Resources to PM Work Orders

If your firm uses required resources, the following registry option discussed in user note 2.11.2 may be used to prevent the writing of PM parts to the Required Resources tab for non-subcontractor technician (Required Resource lines are never written if the PM is created for a subcontractor technician.

New Functionality: Import Required Resources from Job Cost Budget Entries

When you click the Import Required Resource button, the system will now ask 'Do you want to Import Required Resources from JC History?'

If you answer ‘no’, the original import from a text file will run.

if you answer ‘yes’, this new functionality invoke. A form prompt will ask for a required date and how to set the hold flag. Then all JC History budget material lines that match the Job/Cost Code/Billing Item id's specified in the work order header that HAVE NOT already been requisitioned will appear in a check list. Select the ones you want and press the GO button. All selected lines will be added to the Required Resource table and the Workorder will be redisplayed.

Assorted Updates

Corrects ‘Key is missing error’ importing required resources from JC history.

Defaulting of the Equipment Id on the WO's Required Resource tab now works the same as it does for Labor, Inventory, etc. If one piece of Equipment is listed on the Equipment tab, its Equipment Id will default when a Required Resource line is entered. If more than one piece of Equipment is listed on the Work Order, the Equipment Id does NOT default so that the user can select the correct item.
