This defaulting methodology is true for lines manually entered by the user as well as those imported from Job History or an external file via the Import ReqRes button.

Note: the Equipment on the Required Resource pick lists is limited to the Equipment on the Work Order Equipment tab. The user is not permitted to select Equipment not on the Equipment tab.

11.1.3 Labor Tab

This release corrects the posting of WO-Labor to Job History when the Work Order is set to Invoice Ready so that employees are not paid for Quoted lines.

If user enters the Hours first, and then sets the Start End times (resulting in the Hours changing), the Revenue Amount is now updated correctly.

The Start/End times from the Labor Journal (if included in the customization) are now used to update the Work Order Labor tab when labor is imported to the Work Order via Import Costs.

The system now warns the user when entering time for a terminated employee; the Date Terminated (from the Employee record) will be included in the warning.

Due to popular demand, the tab order has been changed so that the Description comes after the Effective Date – in previous versions of 7.2 and 7.3, it was after the flat rate field. If your upgrade to this version did not require a database conversion, you will require a new v.cus file to see this change (contact your support rep).

This release corrects the revenue calculation of the first Labor line if the registry option (in sys-viewer-vwrkordr) DefaultLineDateFromDateWorkCompleted=true is implemented; previously, the Date validation was skipped when the Date defaulted in.

11.1.4 Technician Tab

New Button: TechFinder:
A TechFinder button has been added to the Technicians tab. When clicked, the TechFinder opens, with the work order's Client Site Zone and the Certification for the first piece of equipment on the Equipment tab passed to the TechFinder filters. When the user completes the TechFinder processing, the system returns the selected Technician Id, Date and Time to the appropriate Technician line.

Tech Unavailability: The following enhancement is enabled if the registry option IdentifyUnavailableTechs in sys-viewer-vdsptchbrd is set to true and time off has been entered on the Technician record’s Unavailable tab. When the Tech Id or Date Scheduled is added or changed, the user will be warned if the Technician is Unavailable.

Changed Button: Release to Tech
A new registry option allows the user to define the statuses impacted by the Release to Tech button. See user note 2.8.12.

Changed Field: Log Type Id
A new log order log type of 'No Bill' has been implemented.  The expected usage is for PM work orders that have been pre-billed on PM Invoices. The precedence falls between Billed and Cancelled. If the Work Order Log type of No Bill has precedence, its Work Order Escalation Status will be set to ‘No Bill’ and the Escalation Category will be set to Billed.

11.1.5. COD (Parent Tab)

The following validation has been added to the WO’s parent COD tab:

1. Warn the user when any field is changed on the COD parent tab and the Work Order's terms are not COD.

2. Default the COD GL Account Id from the new field in the Payment Type record when the Payment Id is changed.

3. When selected Payment Type record includes a default GL Account, do not permit changes to the COD GL Account Id.

4. Treat COD Reference No and Payment Type Id as required fields when COD GL Bank Account Id is not empty.

Note: also see user note 11.1.10 for COD Enhancements

11.1.6 Revenue Adjustments

This version corrects processing when the Import Cost Wizard was invoked with NO lines being imported; Revenue Adjustments are now successfully computed.

When the work order's Work Type is 'PM Invoice', changes are not allowed on the Revenue Adjustments tab.  This includes line inserts and deletes. The previous behavior (to allow changes) can be restored with the following registry setting:

Id: sys-viewer-vwrkordr
Setting Key: PreventRevenueAdjustmentAccessOnPMInvoices Setting Value: false

(default true)

11.1.7 WO Import Costs Wizard

Inventory Screen

Changed Field: Qty Used
This field is now display-only; it defaults from the quantity allocated to this Work Order from the Purchase Order or Required Resource transfer.

New Field: Actual Used
This field defaults from the Qty Used field, and should be used to specify the number of this item that were actually used on this work order. If the user sets the Actual Used to less than the Qty Used, the system will handle the process of returning the unused product to the truck or other location. For example, if 50 items were allocated (Qty Used = 50) on the purchase order, and only 8 were actually used on this work order, two lines would be written to the Work Order Inventory Tab: +8 (those actually used) and -42 (returned to stock – to correct Inventory History which shows all 50 going to the Work Orders).

11.1.8 Work Order Other Tab

This update concerns users recently upgraded from v7.1 or earlier. When the date on Other tab entries originally entered in an earlier version was changed, and then the work order was invoiced, the date for this invoice detail did not match the new date on the Other tab. This has been corrected.

Insert Line with Copy is once again enabled for all lines except the following: Insert-with-copy IS disabled when the line being copied references a closed Accounting Period that has the new WO-Other-to-GL option turned on.

This release corrects “Runtime error: Key is missing” problem when changing the Cost Code.

The following new fields have been added to this tab to enable the expensing of company assets, as well as to enable Work Order Other to GL functionality. See user note 19.6 for additional information on the changes to the Accounting Period, Other Rate, and Cost Category records required to support this functionality.

New Fields (click the Magnify button to view):

Asset Id:
Enter the appropriate company equipment Asset Id if you wish to charge it to this Work Order. The Other Rate Id (and the associated Cost and Revenue fields) will default from the Asset record’s Operating Other Rate field. An Asset must be flagged as Chargeable to be entered in this fields.

o Operating o Idle
This field controls whether the Operating Other Rate or Idle Other rate will default from the asset record.

Posted toGLH:
The system will flag this display-only field when a WO Other line is posted to GL.

Period Id:
This field will be completed by the system using the default Accounting Period; however, it will only be used to write to GL History if the Accounting Period has the WO Other to GL option flagged. The system will validate that the Effective Date falls within the selected accounting period if the Accounting Period’s WO Other to GL field is flagged.

GL Debit Id:
This field will default from the Job Cost Category GL Expense field and should reference a Cost of Sales account. However, it will ONLY be used to write to GL History If the selected Accounting Period has the WO Other to GL option flagged

GL Credit Id:
This field will default from the Other Rate’s GL Credit Account. However, it will ONLY be used to write to GL History If the selected Accounting Period has the WO Other to GL option flagged.

11.1.9 Work Order Purchases Tab

If multiple inventory receipt journal entries are made for the same PO, the WO Purchases tab now displays the Job Quantity and Quantity Vouchered correctly.

11.1.10 Work Order Invoicing Tab

Work Orders that reference a Template-type Client will be only eligible for billing if the invoice total is ZERO; see user note 5.9.2 for available details on this validation.

This release includes updated buttons for Ok to Invoice, Build Description, Print Worksheet, Print Invoice, Compute Taxes and Reset Tax Type. The Preview (Camera) button has been added to this screen (but its use is deprecated.)

COD Enhancements

This enhancement addresses two issues with COD invoicing:

1 - what to do when a work order for a COD Job (referencing a generic COD client) has receivables or overages, and must therefore be linked to an actual Client record.

2 - what to do when a work order for a COD Job (referencing an actual client) has receivables or overages, and must therefore recorded with ‘due’ (not COD) terms.

The solution to both these issues is the addition of two new fields to the Work Order Invoicing tab, Override Terms Id (overrides the AR Terms Code in the WO Header Job) and Override Client Id (overrides the Client in the WO Header Job). When these fields are completed in a Service Compute Work Order, the override field will be used instead of those in the Job Header when the Invoice is computed and posted for the Job reference in the WO Header.

An updated Service Invoice Report is required for this functionality: see the revised report section below.

Registry Entries:

Id: sys-viewer-vwrkordr

The following registry entries are required to enable use of the Work Order’s Override fields, WO Terms Id and WO Client Id:

Setting Key: AllowClientOverride  Setting Value: true (default is false)

This registry option is required to enable use of the Work Order’s Override Client field. If your firm normally uses a generic COD Client for COD work orders, set this value to true to enable the user to select / create on the fly an actual Client record to apply the overage / receivables to.

Setting Key: AllowTermsOverride  Setting Value: true (default is false)

This option must be set to true to allow the Override Terms Id in the Work Order to be set by the user.

 

If the technician calculates sales tax for COD work in the field, then set:

Setting Key: ServiceComputeSaleTaxEdits Setting Value: true

Id: sys-sales-journal

Setting Key: clientjobmismatch  Setting Value: warning

This entry overrides the default error checking in the Sales Journal (which currently prevents you from mismatching the Job and the Client on a single entry.) This registry setting NOT required if AllowClientOverride=false AND your firm uses a separate JOB for each COD (it doesn’t use template COD jobs).

Id: sys-start-ssrvcebllngcmpte

Setting Key: UseSJForCOD  Setting Value: false     (or registry option absent)

The system must auto create the cash receipt – this option CANNOT be set to true.

Work Order Invoicing Tab:

Changed Field: AR Terms Id relabeled as Job Terms Id:

This display-only field defaults from the WO header Job.

New Fields:

Job Client Id:
This display-only field defaults from the WO header Job.

Override Terms Id:
If enabled by registry, this field may be used to override the AR Terms Code in the WO header Job.(displayed as Job Terms Id).

Override Client Id:
If enabled by registry, this field may be used to override the Client in the WO header Job.(displayed as Job Client Id). Typically, this would be used if a Work Order for a COD Job (referencing a generic COD client) has receivables or overages, and must therefore be linked to an actual Client record for tracking AR. When the Work Order is invoiced, the AR Sales and Cash Receipts (if applicable) entries generated will reference the Override Client.

Examples:

The Override Client Id field would be set:

a) to take a COD Workorder and create/specify a BILLABLE client for when a COD payment was not received due to homeowner not home or tech lost the check.

b) if an over/under payment is received so that the balance due is put is assigned to actual client.

Important Note: no JOB is created - so that next time service work done for COD client, COD payment is still expected. If you have to turn a COD client into a 'real' billable account then you MUST set-up a Service Job and change the site's default equip from defaulting to the COD job template to your new billable service job.

The Override Terms field would be set:

In case of issue a (above), change the terms from cod to DUE.

Revised Reports: serviceinvoice.rpt and serviceworksheet

If the Billing Address Id is completed, the billing address for the Service Invoice and Worksheet come from this field. If the Override Client Id is completed, but the Billing Address Id is not, the billing address for the Service Invoice and Worksheet come from the Override Client record.

Updated reports are required to support this functionality:

SERVICEWORKSHEETv73b032.rpt

SERVICEINVOICEv73b032.rpt

A Note on Report Naming:

The version and build number of the first Version/Build a report is valid for will now be appended to the filename of the user reports generated and update by our Data-Basics report writers. Note that is NOT necessary to change the filename before imported the report into a database: SAM Pro will use the internal Report Id and Name when updating / adding the report.

When this Wizard is invoked, the system now defaults the Location from the Work Order header.  This Location can be overridden by the user, but can never be blank.

The Metrics tab is now correctly updated when equipment is added, inserted or deleted from the Equipment tab, as well as when the Equipment Id is changed.

11.2 New Call

Previously, if you decided that your site/equipment selections were not correct and entered a different search string, fields that were previously completed were not automatically cleared. In this release, whenever a user tabs out of the search text box in New Call 1, all fields except the Service Category be cleared in preparation for selecting a new Site and Equipment..

Corrects a “Key is missing” error in 7.3.498.093 that occurred when the user attempted to add a work order that had been created from a web log.

Tech Unavailability

This enhancement is enabled if the registry option IdentifyUnavailableTechs in sys-viewer-vdsptchbrd is set to true and time off has been entered on the Technician record’s Unavailable tab. If the Technician and Date scheduled are both entered, a Warning will appear saying the Tech is Unavailable when the New Call is saved.

When you use New Call to create a Work Order from a Web Log, the Web Log's change entry is now updated with the Date, Time, and User Id and the description WOFromNewCall .

The Client Site’s WO Other tab may be used to generate standard trip/truck charges to Work Orders created in New Call (this feature is not recommended for TechAnywhere users as this information is not uploaded to the TechAnywhere device). Previously, the Sales Tax Group and Type for the Work Order Other lines generated in this fashion were derived from the Sales Tax Group on the Client Site COP tab. In this release, the system uses the Sale Tax Group in the Job record when generating the Work Order Other tab line.

Corrects a display issue that occurred if a Site with a Service Manager was picked a second time; this Service Manager Id was selected correctly, but not redisplayed in the field.

11.2.1 New Call - New COD Site

Previously, the Zip Code’s Branch ID & Service Zone were displayed when the New Call New COD Site view was first accessed, but as soon as you select one of your COD templates, the Service Zone was overridden from the COD Site Template, even if blank. This behavior has been changed this so that information from the Zip code is not overridden by blank Branch and Service Zone fields from the COD Site Template.

Corrects an error encountered if the Service Manager was set in the CS Equipment record associated with the Site template.

Corrects a problem where the Equipment the first WO created for a new COD site referenced the COD template, not the new site. Contact your service representative if existing data needs to be corrected.

When a new COD Site is created, the Account Manager, Sales Rep, Service Manager and Dispatcher are now set from the Site Template.

When a COD work order is created using this function, the Account Manager, Service Manager, Dispatcher and Sales Rep now default from the Site if the corresponding fields in the selected Equipment are blank.

NOTE: this enhancement requires a revised v.cus file if upgrading to this image did not trigger a data conversion.  If your firm uses the standard WinII file, the new file vWinII.cus has been added to the master zip file, and may be renamed as v.cus in the user’s environment for this field to be available. If your firm uses a custom v.cus file, contact your support representative for a new one if you wish to see this field.

Important Note on Metrics: when a work order referencing a log form is created in SAM Pro, metrics will only be written to the work order metrics tab if the Technician is not a TechAnywhere tech (e.g., Remote Access is set to None) or no Tech is specified. If the work order initially assigned to a technician with remote access, metrics will be uploaded to the technician’s device, and then posted to the work order in SAM Pro when they have been completed in the field.

Classic Board: On the Classic board, unavailability is indicated with a red background on the column or row header displaying the Technician’s information for those days that he or she is unavailable. On the Power board, a currently unavailable Technician’s line in the Technician Summary (upper portion of the board) will be displayed in red.

11.5 Archive Workorders

The two new functions, Start Archive Work Orders and Start Autoarchive Work Orders are designed to allow high-volume customers to set older Work Orders to an Archived status. The Update Function may need to be run to access these functions. To be eligible for archiving, the Work Order’s Date Closed must be set, and the Escalation Status would typically be set to Billed or Cancelled.

When Work Order is Archived, a Tech line will be added set to the Log Type of Archive with will override all other statuses when setting the Escalation Status and Status Category. To ‘unarchive’ a Work Order, the user can simply delete or change the ‘archived’ Tech line and save the Work Order.

Archived Work Orders will not appear on the Dispatch Board, but are still listed in the New Call WO pane.

A new button, Archived, has been added to the Work Order List; clicking this button filters the list to Archived Work Orders only.

11.5.1 Start Autoarchive Work Orders

This function is designed to be run as a scheduled event. The following registry options must be in effect.

Registry setting parameters:

Id: sys-start-sautoarchivewo

Setting Key: DaysOld  Setting Value: #days

If this was set to 180 days, the work order would have to have a date closed on it 180 days or earlier than today to enable it to be archived.

Setting Key: EscalationStatuses  Setting Value: billed,cancelled

This is the recommended setting. Archiving ‘uncompleted’ work orders with this function is NOT recommended as they may have unbilled costs.

11.5.2 Start Archive Work Orders

This is the manual process to archive work orders.

Archive Workorders Range Screen Important Fields:

Date Opened / Date Closed:
At least one of these fields must be completed:

If you set the Date Opened, only Work Orders created on or before that day will be eligible for archiving.

If you set the Date Closed, only Work Orders who’s Date Close is set to that day or before will be eligible for archiving.

If you set both fields, the Work Order must meet both the Date Opened and Date Closed criteria to be eligible for archiving.

Site ID
Job ID
Work Order ID
Site Status (e.g., if site is inactive, archive the WO’s)
Escalation Status (defaults to billed,cancelled,completed,no bill)
It is recommended that at least one of these ranges is completed to limit the work order eligible for archiving.

Warning: use with caution the first time – this is computationally intensive the first time you run it.

Completed Work Orders: You may use this function to archive completed work orders. However, care should be taken to verify that they do not include unbilled costs.

Click the Go button to display a list of eligible Work Orders.

Archive Work Orders Checklist Screen:

Do
This field enables you to select which scheduled Work Orders should be archived. A check appears in the Do field if an item is selected; by default, all Work Orders are selected. Double-click on the Do field to select or deselect an item (or press the Spacebar when the caret appears on this field).

WO Id: - Site Id: - Job Id: - Site Status: - Escalation Status:
This fields are displayed to help you determine which Work Orders should actually be archived.

Important Buttons:

Click the Check button to check (select) every item on the list.

Click to de-select every item on the list. Click to Archive the selected Work Orders.

11.6 Start Create PM Work Orders

A new Job Id Range Filter has been added to Start Create PM WOs function. This enables the user to limit this functions to a specific Job or Jobs. This filtering impacts lines entered directly on the Client Site Equipment PM Schedule tab, as well as lines that will be generated from Master Contract.

When Required Resource processing is enabled for Create PM Work Orders, and the registry options are in order so that Requires Resource lines should be written, the Equipment Id on the Required Resource line is now completed from the Client Site Equipment record that needed the line.

If your firm uses required resources, a new registry may be used to prevent the writing of PM parts to the Required Resources tab for non-subcontractor technician (Required Resource lines are never written if the PM is created for a subcontractor technician). See user note 2.11.2 for details.

11.7 Scheduled Event Manager

This release corrects problems with handling read-only documents.

11.7.1 Scheduled Events

New button - Fix Tokens

If the user wishes to manually release a scheduled event, click this button causes the system to evaluate and replace any tokens. Previously, the user had to manually replace all tokens.

11.8 Escalation Profiles

New Field: Obsolete
By default, this field not checked. If it is checked, the record is considered Obsolete.

Note that although validation logic denies direct entry of obsolete record Ids, the Escalation Manager will continue to use obsolete Escalation Profiles if they are attached to work orders / web logs.

When you check the Obsolete field, the following message box will be displayed:

"You have elected to obsolete this record. Would you like to see existing references to this record?"

If you click Yes, the system will display a viewer that provides click-through access to all tables referencing this record. It is strongly recommended that you edit active Client Sites / Equipment to replace Obsolete Escalation Profiles.

11.8.2 Web Log Profiles

This enhancement allows escalation management to sense and trigger events based on web log changes (e.g., to Canceled or Duplicate), allowing the user to define escalation profile rules to send email notifications automatically.

11.9 Notification Categories

New Field: Obsolete
By default, this field not checked. If it is checked, the record is considered Obsolete.

Note that although validation logic denies direct entry of obsolete record Ids, the Escalation Manager will continue to use obsolete Notification Categories if they are in Escalation Profiles if they are attached to work orders / web logs.

When you check the Obsolete field, the following message box will be displayed:

"You have elected to obsolete this record. Would you like to see existing references to this record?"

If you click Yes, the system will display a viewer that provides click-through access to all tables referencing this record. It is strongly recommended that you edit active Escalation Profiles to replace Obsolete Notification Categories.

11.10 WO List Report

11.11 Technician Viewer

11.11.1 Remote Access Tab

Changed Field: Remote Device Type:

A new option named 'Android' has been added.

The option named 'Windows' replaces the old option named 'XP'.  Automated data conversion is not necessary as 'XP' and 'Windows' will be equivalents inside the SAMPRO and DB Exchange code.  However, when a SAMPRO user loads an XP-type Technician record into the viewer, the following message will be display:

This Technician Device Type is being switched from ‘XP’ to ‘Windows’.
Please save the record to make the change permanent.

The user should click OK to clear the message, and save the Technician record.

11.11.2 New Tab – Unavailable

Purpose:

Specify the days a technician is unavailable for regular work.

Usage:

The Dispatch board (both Power and Classic) are now able to indicate that a Technician is unavailable. A registry entry (see user note 2.28) is required to turn this functionality on. On the Classic board, unavailability is indicated with a red background on the column or row header displaying the Technician’s information for those days that he or she is unavailable. On the Power board, a currently unavailable Technician’s line in the Technician Summary (upper portion of the board) will be displayed in red.

Important Fields:

Schedule Category:
The general reason for the unavailability (e.g., Sick, Jury Duty, Vacation).

Tip:
An administrator may customize this field via the Custom Fields functionality to change its label, and to define a list of acceptable values for it.

Start Date: End Date:
The days the Tech will not be available for work.

Schedule Note:
Any brief notes on this specific unavailable time.

11.14 Master Contract

11.14.1 Setup/Renew enhancements

In previous releases, the user could not use the AutoPopulate button to adjust Inspection and/or Advanced Billing for the current date range if these lines already existed on the Master Contract: the message 'Start Date cannot precede Original End Date' was displayed. In this release, the user is only restricted from using the AutoPopulate button if any of the existing scheduled or billed lines have been used to generate corresponding lines in the Client Site PM Billing or Client Site Equipment PM tables. Further, if these lines exist, the message has been clarified to display: "Advanced Billing and or Schedule lines have already been generated for this date range; the Start Date cannot precede the original End Date".

If the deprecated RemoveValidations registry option is in effect, the “Warning – This action will replace the existing schedule. Any previously generated invoices and work orders will still exist. Are you sure you want to continue?” will be suppressed if the Auto Populate button is pressed but no ‘used’ advanced billing or inspection lines are found.

11.15 Web Log

The Status field may once again be set by the user.

New Field:
Previous Status: New Acknowledged Unacknowledged Cancelled Duplicate
These fields are maintained by the system, and are used in by escalation management to sense and trigger events based on web log changes (e.g., to Cancelled or Duplicate), allowing the user to define escalation profile rules to send email notifications automatically

11.16 Start Archive Work Orders

Purpose:

This function is designed to allow high-volume customers to set older Work Orders to an Archived status. To be eligible for archiving, the Work Order’s Date Closed must be set, and the Escalation Status would typically be set to Billed or Cancelled.

When Work Order is Archived, a Tech line will be added set to the Log Type of Archive which will override all other statuses when setting the Escalation Status and Status Category. To ‘unarchive’ a Work Order, the user can simply delete or change the ‘archived’ Tech line and save the Work Order.

Archived Work Orders will not appear on the Dispatch Board, but are still listed in the New Call WO pane.

A new button, Archived, has been added to the Work Order List; clicking this button filters the list to Archived Work Orders only.

Usage:

This function may be run by the user to archive selected work orders.

Warning: use with caution if many work orders are being archived (e.g, the first time the function is run) – it is a CPU intensive function.

Important Fields: Range Screen

Date Opened / Date Closed:
At least one of these fields must be completed. Workorders opened on or before the Date Opening, or closed on or before the Date Closed will be archived (subject to entries in the other range fields.

Client Site ID, Job ID, Work Order ID
These fields enable you to archive only specific work orders, or only those associated with specific jobs or site.

Site Status:
This field could be set to inactive to archive work orders for inactive sites.

Escalation Status:
By default, this range is set to

billed,cancelled,completed,no bill

This range should be used with caution for completed work orders, however, as they may have unbilled revenues.

When all fields are correctly completed, click the Go button to proceed. A checklist of all work orders corresponding the criteria you specified will be displayed.

Important Fields: Checklist Screen

Do
This field enables you to select which work orders will be archived. By default, all work orders are selected. Double-click on the Do field to select or deselect an item (alternately, press the spacebar when the caret appears on this field); an "x" appears in the Do field when that work order is selected.

Work Order Id: Site Id: Job Id: Site Status: Escalation:
These fields are displayed for informational purposes so that you can verify which work orders should be archived.

Important Buttons:

Click the Check button to check (select) every item on the list.

Click to de-select every item on the list.

When you click the Go button, a Tech line will be added set to the Log Type of Archive to all selected work orders. This will override all other statuses and set the Escalation Status to Archived.

11.17 Start Autoarchive Workorders

Purpose:

The function Start Autoarchive Work Orders is designed to allow high-volume customers to set older Work Orders to an Archived status.

Usage:

This function is designed to be run as a scheduled event. The following registry options must be in effect. Contact your support representative for assistance in setting this up.

Registry setting parameters:

Id: sys-start-Sautoarchivewo

Setting Key: DaysOld Setting Value: #days

If this was set to 180 days, the work order would have to have a date closed on it 180 days or earlier than today.

Setting Key: EscalationStatuses Setting Value: billed,cancelled

This is the recommended setting. Archiving ‘completed’ work orders with this function is NOT recommended as they may have unbilled costs.

11.18 Service Evaluation Enhancement

Note: Changes to Default Behavior:
When a work order is created all service evaluation questions from the Work Order’s Service Evaluation table are moved to the Work Order Evaluation child table and the answers are set to unknown.

The Service Evaluation Wizard is now titled as the Unanswered Service Evaluation Wizard. Only unanswered questions (where the answer is set to unknown) will appear on the Wizard. The Wizard will be launched as discussed in section 11.18.1 below.

11.18.1 Service Evaluation Record - Category: General (new option)

This new option allows the inclusion of general questions to be included in Service Evaluations. The Unanswered Service Evaluation Questions Wizard will be invoked when the Work Order Escalation Status is set to the value (or one of the values) defined in the sys-viewer-vwrkordr registry’s GeneralEvaluationLogTypes option. Note that all unanswered questions (including Closings and Invoicing questions) will be displayed in the wizard when it is invoked in this fashion.

11.18.2 Work Order Service Evaluation Changes

When a work order is created all service evaluation questions from the Work Order’s Service Evaluation table are moved to the Work Order Evaluation child table and the answers are set to unknown.

The name of the Service Evaluation Wizard has been changed to the Unanswered Service Evaluation Wizard because only unanswered questions (answers are set to unknown) will be included when it is run. As is previous releases, the wizard will be invoked when the work order is completed or invoiced.

In this release, the Unanswered Service Evaluation Questions Wizard will be also be invoked when the Work Order Escalation Status is set to the value (or one of the values) defined in the sys-viewer-vwrkordr registry’s GeneralEvaluationLogTypes option. All unanswered questions (including Closing, Invoicing and General questions) will be displayed in the wizard when it is invoked in this fashion.

When the wizard pops up based on the registry setting, ALL unanswered questions will appear, but the user is NOT required to answer any of the questions.

When the 'closing' wizard pops up, any unanswered CLOSING or GENERAL-type questions will appear. The user is NOT required to answer any of the questions.

When the 'invoicing' wizard pops up, ALL unanswered questions will appear. The user IS required to answer each question.

11.18.3 Registry Entry to Implement

A new registry entry is required to implement this enhancement:

Id: sys-viewer-vwrkordr

Setting Key: GeneralEvaluationLogTypes  Setting Values: list of work order escalation statuses.

When the Workorder is escalated to one of the registry statuses listed, all unanswered questions are displayed in a Wizard and must be answered.

11.19 Log Form Lines Viewer (Metrics)

Two rows in the same Log Form record may not contain identical Heading and Line contents. This viewer now displays the following error if you attempt to save the record with this situation: “LogFormLinesByDescriptionByParentRn for table ‘lgfrmlne’ would not be unique.” The user must edit the one of the offending row entries to insure its uniqueness before the record can be saved.

Example:

Not Allowed:

Row 1: Heading: Pressure Line: Test 1

Row 2: Heading: Pressure Line: Test 1

Allowed:

Row 1: Heading: Pressure Line: Test 1

Row 2: Heading: Pressure Line: Test 2

 

 

12. TechAnywhere

The sys-ffv-global-settings registry includes an option, BranchSequence = nextwo, that enables a branch prefix to be prepended to the Work Order Id. TechAnywhere now checks to see if it should use a branch prefix and use it when posting NewWOs message.

Tech Anywhere now supports COD payments when the message payload contains multiple Workorders.

This release fixes the handling of Negative Values with a minus sign in first character. Also sets the price for Labor/Inventory and Other lines. The extra flag is set, the billing rate id to 'unit price'.

12.1 TechAnywhere Post

Corrects issue with Labor Rate erroneously defaulting from the Employee record if the client’s customization includes reordering of the Labor Journal Hours tab. See case for details.

This release corrects a problem where the Work Order Updates from TechAnywhere caused a WO Tech RN change. Also improves email alert processing.

Corrects Tech Anywhere intermittent issue posting COD multiple times.

The posting of new work order messages can now handle the time scheduled of "00:00", a valid time format for midnight.

Fixed problem where work orders created from TechAnywhere would have initial status of "Pending" rather than "Unacknowledged".

Now properly posts flat rate items from TechAnywhere Android.

This release reduces the amount of memory required to process TechAnywhere message data. Previously, memory spikes on large messages might cause out of memory errors.

Inventory from TechAnywhere can be posted to the default accounting period, even if the effective date is outside of the period range. A registry entry is now available to adjust either the date or accounting period to keep them in sync.  See user note 2.9.2 for details.

The system now verifies that a TechAnywhere message contains the following before posting: Date Scheduled, Time Scheduled, Technician Id, Site Id and Equipment Id. If any of these fields are missing, the message fails and sends an email alert.

The security override from the Work Order is correctly applied to Labor Journal, Purchase Order, Sales Journal, and new Site Equipment records during the TechAnywhere Post UNLESS the record is included in the sys-securityexceptionsbytable registry entry (specifying that its security should be zero).

In previous releases, all TechAnywhere attachments came in with the Web Viewable CRM, Web Viewable CSR, and Web Viewable Tech flags checked. For signatures captured in TechAnywhere, all 3 are now cleared.

In this release, the TechAnywhere event manager no longer attempts to re-post messages with the status of "PostedBy User". This allows clients to resume processing of posting other messages by restarting the TechAnywhere event manager.

This release corrects the reference number written to the WO COD tab during the TechAnywhere post so that the Check Number (and not the Message Id) is displayed.

If the amount of data entered into the recommendation field by the tech surpasses the 1024 character limit, SAM Pro truncates the data so it will fit into a weblog and post the message.

Signature data now removed during the posting, inspecting, or exporting of messages. The signature data is still stored on the receipt that was generated in the field and attached to the SAM Pro records.

Previously, if an Inventory Item Id was changed and the technicians were not instructed to perform a sync to retrieve inventory, the tech would apply the old ID to Workorders which resulted in the post failing. The system now uses the Inventory RN (internal number) during the post to the work order and when using required resources.

Posting Required Resources from Tech Anywhere now sets the Equipment Id.

The TechAnywhere Post now supports allow multiple payment methods (e.g., the customer pays part in cash, part by credit card).

Invoices created by TA will use the standard Invoice Next Numbers from Sampro. The Invoice Description field will have the TA Reference Invoice Number (for auditing).

GL accounts for COD payment entries and the cash receipt are now taken via GL account listed in payment type.

12.1.1 Registry Entry for COD Work Orders: do not post to AR Sales / Cash Receipts

A new registry Item has been added to allow COD-type work orders to be invoiced from SAM Pro instead of occurring as part of the TechAnywhere post. This allows the back office staff to review the Tech Anywhere COD Invoices before posting to AR.

Id: sys-techanywhere

Setting Key: AutoPostCOD Setting Value: false or true

The default is true. If the option is absent or set to true, the current default is retained: the post will create an Invoice, AR Sales Journal, and Cash Receipt.

When the Setting Value is false, the behavior is completely changed. AR Sales Journal, Cash Receipt and Invoice Master records are NOT created. All imported lines come in without an AR invoice reference ID so that they can be billed normally via Service Compute. AR entries can then be created through SAMPro.

Note: Previously, AutoPostCOD (false) created a one-sided GL History entry. Now the post no longer creates a one-sided GL history line, or an invoice master with the status of New. The Invoice Master should not be needed as TechAnywhere does not assign invoice IDs as it has in the past.

12.2 TechAnywhere Event Manager

This release corrects a Tech Anywhere and Scheduled Event Manager Posting Conflict.

In this release, 'billed' has been added to the list of work order log types that get skipped in the update SQL when the TechAnywhere Event Manager runs.

12.3 Remote Tech – Blackberry/Mirifex

Corrects problem with Blackberry uploads including a Resolution code.

Corrects problem where Blackberry/Mirifex Posting was hanging due to Work Order's "open remote techs" warning message.

12.4 Start Purge Message Table

Important Note: The correct registry Id for this function is sys-start-sprgemssge (was previously documented as sys-start-sprgemssgetble).

This release: adds a commit at the end of processing; corrects a Sybase (-157 error); and implements a progress meter.

13. ServiceChannel FMMS

This release includes improved support of message handling in New Call.

This release ensures that the data from multiple ServiceChannel tracking #'s is separated into individual files for proper processing.

To prevent naming conflicts, the Archive and Reject folders are included in the naming conflict resolution.

Better handling of bad data occasionally sent to us from ServiceChannel.

When the Upload to Service Channel button is pushed in the Quote Viewer, a confirming message ('This Quote has been queued for uploading to ServiceChannel') is displayed.

Also corrects issue with the Proposal Upload.

Internal fixes to databridge.

The Quote upload was only uploading Scopes with a status of 'Open': this has extended to include Scopes with a status of 'Printed'.

The SAM Pro data are now always updated when an Invoice has been uploaded to Service Channel.

The Invoice Date uploaded to Service Channel now includes the time using the format 'mm/dd/yyyy hh:mm' where the hh:mm represents the current time.

The ServiceChannel invoice upload is now successfully gets the User Id and Password from the registry

13.1 Message Viewer

The Message viewer now hides the message type of FMMS. The default setting of the Message Type range has been changed from !SageQuest to ~SageQuest,FMMS.

13.2 Multiple Company/PIN Support

This release allows our ServiceChannel FMMS bridge to support multiple companies (ServiceChannel PIN's) if needed. To support this, additional sampro registries can be made in the form of:

sys-fmms-vendor-ServiceChannel-pin-XXXX

This registry setting should only need to contain the user/password (InvoiceUID & InvoicePWD) options for that particular company (pin), but could be used to override other settings if needed. All other registry settings default from the base registry setting (sys-fmms-vendor-ServiceChannel), and the "pin" registry can be used to override the settings on a pin by pin basis.

14. SageQuest

When Work Orders were uploaded to SageQuest, they were previously sent using an hours format like “estimatedHours=2.5”. At SageQuest’s request, we now convert estimated hours from hours to seconds before we send it up to them.

Web Services / Sagequest: Internal changes to increase performance.

14.1 SageQuest / TechAnywhere

TechAnywhere records the date and time that a status change was made. So the tech may make a status change of onsite at noon, but if he is out of range that status change may not get updated till he is in range (let's say 1:30).

Previously, the TechAnywhere Post updated SageQuest at the time the post occurred. (in our example the post time would be 1:30). The problem was that SageQuest knows when the vehicle arrives (noon) but the status change time is 1:30. This made the Workorder Variance report incorrect.

To correct this problem, fields have been added to the Work Order Technician tab with the status change date and time, not the time posted. When TechAnywhere posts it updates these fields with the date and time that a status change was made (noon). The SageQuest integration now uses these fields when they are populated with relevant data to send the correct time up to SageQuest.

14.2 Sagequest / Escalation Management

Sage Quest: If the Work Order Escalation Status is set to Cancelled, Credit Hold, or Archived, SAM Pro will send a message to SageQuest to say that it is cancelled; the Work Order is then removed from the SageQuest map.

14.3 SageQuest Garmin Support

The CreateStopForWorkorder functionality is now only called if the status of a work order is changing TO the registry set (stop value).

14.4 SageQuest / Client Site

This release handles an error that occurred when the Sage Quest interface was on and the user loaded a client site record with the Site Latitude field is blank, and Work/Ship Street Address includes the @ character.

 

15. Manufacturing / Client Orders

15.1 Shop Order

15.1.1 Transfer Tickets

Shop Order Transfer Ticket – New Fields
Full Orders Only
If this field is checked, only Shop Order Transfer Tickets for Full Orders will be printed. The definition of a Full Order is:

1. All BOM items are released to pick
2. No BOM items are on backorder for the shop order

Work Order Id:
Work Order Type:
These range fields have been added to enable the user to filter Shop Order Transfer tickets to those generated by Material Requisitioning. For example, to print tickets for only those Shop Orders generated by Service Work Orders, you would enter the word Service in the Work Order Type range. To limit the tickets to those generated by PM Work Orders, enter P% in the Work Order Type Range.

The Work Order Id range can be used to generate the Shop Order Transfer Tickets for a specific Work Order, or several Work Orders as a comma-delimited list  (11101, 11154, 11213).

11.1.2 Shop Order Pick List Entry

This release corrects reversing logic when a line is deleted so that the default date and accounting period are set correctly.

15.2 Client Order

COP Sales Tax Handling: The system now allows changes to Sales Tax Group in Client Orders. The Client Site COP Tax Exempt field in tax calculations is now included in COP Invoice calculations. If this box is flagged, sales tax will not be included on the COP Invoice.

When COP orders are invoiced, extraneous pricing lines (with only a GL Entity and a Revenue Type) are no longer written to the AR Sales Journal.

The GL Entity for lines designated as Drop Ship PO is now transferred to the PO that is generated.

15.2.1 Items Tab

This version includes assorted enhancements to make this work as described below:

Enhanced Substitute Item Number Functionality:
1. When entering an order line, enter the item number the customer thinks he is getting in the Inventory Item Id field – not the Substitute Item Field. This will properly load up the item description and the cost for the last time the customer ordered that item. It will also set the Substitute item number to the item number entered.

2. Then, change the item number in the Inventory Item Id field to the item number actually to be shipped.

3. The system will ask if you want to copy this to the substitute item number field. Answer ‘No’.

4. Proceed as usual. At this point, the first field on the child tab is the 'actual' item number. That is, this is the item that is withdrawn from inventory. The 'substitute' part number only appears on paperwork. The customer thinks that they are getting the 'substitute' item but they are really getting the 'actual' item.

The ‘substitute’ item will appear on the COP Invoice and Order Acknowledgement that is sent to the customer.

On the Pick Ticket, the first page lists the Substitute Item so that this page may be sent to the customer as a packing slip. The second page of the Pick Ticket is flagged as “INTERNAL COMMENTS – DO NOT SHIP THIS PAGE TO CLIENT”, and shows the part substitution as follows:

***** PART NUMBER SUBSTITUTION *****

For this Part Number Substitute this Part

123100*   123105

15.2.2 Cancelling Client Orders

In this release, a Client Order may be cancelled if a Pick Ticket has not been printed for any of the Items on the order. Cancelling an order will automatically reverse its backorders/allocations from IM history.

COP Processing has been disabled for Cancelled Orders as follows:

Pick Tickets cannot be printed for Cancelled Orders.
View Client Pick List Entry is disabled for Cancelled Orders.
View Client Order To Ship is disabled for Cancelled Orders.

New Fields: Client Order Parent Screen

Cancelled Date: Cancelled By:
These fields may only be completed if a Pick Ticket has not yet been printed for any of the items on the order. When you save this Order with these fields completed, it will be Cancelled and the system will automatically reverse its backorders/allocations from IM history

New Tab: IM History

This tab displays a summary of the Inventory History for this client order. If you cancel a Client Order by completing the Cancelled Date and Cancelled by fields, existing allocations/backorders for this order will be reversed, and this tab will be blank.

New Tab: Pick Tickets

This tab displays the Pick Ticket detail for this order. If you cancel a Client Order by completing the Cancelled Date and Cancelled By fields, pick tickets are no longer applicable for this order, and this tab will be blank.

Client Order Range View

New Range: Date Cancelled
A new range, Date Cancelled, has been added to the range view. This range is prefilled to exclude orders cancelled today (and in the past) from the list of Active Client Orders.

15.3 Fill Shop Backorders

This version corrects a problem with partially filled shop backorders.

Also corrects a sporadic problem handling negative quantities.

15.4 Shop Order

The Transfer Qty BO'd has been added to the BOM full screen view of the Shop Order. 

15.5 Shop Order (Transfer Ticket) Pick List Entry

Entering a non-zero value in the Qty Transferred field now forces the Transfer Done field to True: this field must be flagged for correct processing.

17. CRMAnywhere

17.1 Quote Page

The sidebar graphic now correctly appears on the Print Quote page. The Quote now also supports the CRMReportType registry option of pdf; if this option is implemented, the Quote itself will be displayed in pdf format.

The Quote page now displays tables for Quote and Site attachments that are flagged as CRM Viewable.

17.2 View Invoice Page

If the user clicked the link “View Invoice PDF” before the PDF had been generated, the 404 page not found error appeared. The software now waits a bit before attempting to display the file.

17.3 CRM Anywhere / CSR Anywhere Header Graphics

This enhancement may be enabled to improve the way the page headers in CRMAnywhere and CSRAnywhere are handled. Modifications to your existing graphics will be needed to support the change.

When these functions were first implemented, lower resolution screens were the norm, and the CSRAnywhere and CRMAnywhere headers were designed be left justified on 600X800 pixel screens, with the HTML generated by SAM Pro centered.

To be more suitable for larger screen, the following registry entry may be used to enable the centering of headers with an appropriate background graphic, and a right-justified graphic to complete the screen:

Id: web-settings
Setting Key: NewHeaders Setting Value: true

If this registry is implemented, changes will need to be made to existing graphics – be sure to save the original versions of all graphics first:

1. The right-hand side of a header gif should be cropped and saved as right.gif. This graphic will appear at the right-hand side of the header for all pages.

2. The portion of the header gif’s containing the title (e.g., Main Menu, View Quotes, etc.) should be cropped to remove the left and right portions of the graphics, and resaved under their original name. These graphics will be centered in header.

3. A one or two pixel wide vertical slice of the graphic’s background should be cropped and saved as slice.gif. This graphic will be repeated as the header background.

The web server should be restarted after the registry change has been made and the revised graphics installed.

17.4 CRMAnywhere Open Requests Page

Registry entry to allow sorting of open work orders and service request lists if multiple sites are involved. This option should be use with caution as it may impact performance.

Id: web-settings

Setting Key: AllowMultiSiteSorting Setting Value: true

 

17.5 CRMAnywhere – Appointment Confirmation

This enhancement is designed to allow customers (typically residential customers not normally set up with a full Web User account for CRMAnywhere) to log on via an email link and confirm or reject an appointment for a service call. The customer will receive an email generated via escalation manager that will include a link to the CRMAnywhere Appointment Confirmation page; once there they can confirm or reject the appointment.

17.5.1 Graphics Setup

A banner for the Confirm Appointment page, named appointment.gif, and a sidebar logo named sidebarLogoOnly. They should conform to the standards for the other CRMAnywhere banners and sidebars:

If the web-settings registry specifies the New Headers format (Setting Key: NewHeaders Setting Value: true):

The right-hand side of the header should be named right.gif. It should be 68 pixels high, and wide enough to display the desired graphic. This graphic is also used in the other CRMAnywhere screens.

The gif containing the title (e.g., Confirm Appointment) should be wide enough to display the appropriate title, and be 68 pixels high. This graphic will be centered in the header, and must be named appointment.gif.

A one or two pixel wide and 68 pixel high vertical slice of the graphic’s background should be named slice.gif. This graphic will be repeated as the header background, and is used in the other CRMAnywhere pages.

A sidebar area - 112 pixels wide by 440 pixels high, named sidebarLogoOnly.gif. Note that a menu will NOT appear on the sidebar in the Confirm Appointment screen.

If the web-settings registry does NOT specify the New Headers format:

The gif containing the title (e.g., Confirm Appointment) should be wide enough to display the appropriate title, and be 68 pixels high and of the same width as your other CRMAnywhere banners. This graphic will be left-justified against the sidebar graphic. It should be named appointment.gif.

A sidebar area - 112 pixels wide by 440 pixels high, named sidebarLogoOnly.gif. Note that a menu will NOT appear on the sidebar in the Confirm Appointment screen.

17.5.2 Registry

This registry setting is required to implement the Appointment Confirmation functionality.

Registry Id: web-settings-guest

URL for Guest Page

Setting Key: URL Setting Value: URL of guest page

Statuses for Confirmed and Rejected Work Order

These options control the status changes that will occurred when the customer confirms or rejects the appointment. Only WO Tech lines with the Date/Time Scheduled that match the web page get updated to the new status. The WO Escalation Status gets updated when the WO is escalated which happens shortly after updating the WO Tech lines.

Setting Key: ConfirmedStatus Setting Value: valid WO log status (e.g., Scheduled)

Setting Key: RejectedStatus Setting Value: valid WO log status (e.g., Rescheduled)

Messages for Confirmed and Rejected Work Orders

These options specify the message to display when an appointment is confirmed or rejected.

Setting Key: ConfirmedMessage Setting Value: message for confirmed appointment

Setting Key: RejectedMessage Setting Value: message for rejected appointment

Specify the password and user id for the Guest page

Note that system, not the user, will manage the login using the following settings.

Setting Key:GuestUID Setting Value: guest

Setting Key: GuestPWD Setting Value: guest

 

17.5.3 Web User Account for Appointment Confirmation

A Web User account must be set up for use as the guest account.  The Web User Id and Password must be consistent with the registry settings. It is not necessary to specify the Web Profile.

17.5.4 Escalation Profile

New Token: ^confirmappointmentlink^

A new Escalation Profile token has been implemented as part of this enhancement.  The token entered into the profile should read ^confirmappointmentlink^.  This token will be replaced by a web link to the guest page when the scheduled event executes; the customer will simply click this link to access the Appointment Confirmation page.

The link consists of these components: the URL from the registry entry, the guest account login from the registry, the work order id and rn, and the scheduled event id which generated the e-mail. The id, rn and event values are extracted from the link and used to 'authenticate' the incoming request.  SQL statements confirm that the values make sense relative to one another.  Access is denied when the link's values are not successfully authenticated.

Example: Escalation Profile

Source: workorder

Action Type: notification

Notify Id: clientsite (pick the Notification record pointing to the Client Site email)

Status From: any

Status To: Waiting Service (or Unacknowledged or Pending)

Time Base: creation

Day: Hrs: Min: 1 (minute)

Email Subject: Please Confirm Your Appointment

Email Text: Please click on the following link to confirm or reject your appointment:

^confirmappointmentlink^

Appointment Confirmation Page

If confirmed, the work order status will change to "scheduled" (or any value you set).

If rejected, the work order status will change to "Rescheduled" (or any value you set).

17.6 Site View Page

In previous releases, if the registry option disablecrmmanagequotes was set to true in the web-settings registry to remove the Manage Quotes page, the Quote table was also suppressed in the Site View page. In this release, the Quote table is also suppressed in the Site View page when this option is implemented in the registry tab of the Web Profile or Web User record.

19 Asset Costing and Tracking

19.1 Overview

SAM Pro Version 7.3 supports Asset Costing and Tracking. A new Asset record has been added that may be used to record equipment assets that your firm owns or leases for the purposes of:

Preventive Maintenance Tracking

Costing / Billing to Direct and Overhead Jobs

Record Expenses (for user reporting purposes)

Related Record Setup:

Job Cost Category

New Selection Cost Type: Equipment
The new Selection Cost Type of Equipment has been added to the Job Cost Category. This option should be selected for Job Cost Categories that are used to charge company equipment (Assets) to jobs to enable proper tracking of costs and reporting. The Posting Cost Type of Other should be chosen when the Selection Cost Type of Equipment is selected.

Other Rates

Create Operating and Idle Other Rates to be used when charging company equipment Assets to Jobs in the Job Journal. The GL Credit Account field must be completed. The Cost Category selected should have a Selection Cost Type of Equipment.

Asset PM Type (see user note 19.2).

Asset Type (see user note 19.3)

Asset (see user note 19.4).

19.2 Asset PM Type Viewer

Purpose:

Define the types of maintenance required by your company equipment Assets (e.g., Change Oil).

Usage:

Referenced in the Asset record’s Maintenance tab.

Important Fields:

Asset PM Type Id:
Uniquely defines this type of preventive maintenance (e.g., Oil, Lube, etc.).

Asset PM Type Name:
Briefly describes this type of maintenance. Not required but strongly recommended.

Obsolete?
If this field is checked, the record is considered Obsolete, and it may not be directly specified during data-entry (either by entering the Id or selecting it from a list). Obsoleted records can be edited and the Obsolete option can be un-done when necessary. When you check the Obsolete field, the following message box will be displayed:

“You have elected to obsolete this record. Would you like to see existing references to this record?”

If you click Yes, the system will display a viewer that provides click-through access to all tables referencing this record:

Usage:

Referenced in the Asset record’s Main tab.

Obsolete?
