19.4 Asset Viewer

This release corrects a spurious ‘Job is a Template record’ message that previously occurred when the user attempted to clear the Default Overhead Job fields from the Costing tab.

Purpose:

The Asset record may be used to record assets that your firm owns or leases for the purposes of:

Preventive Maintenance Tracking

Costing / Billing to Direct and Overhead Jobs

Recording Expenses (for user reporting only

Usage:

Currently, the Job Journal Co.Equipment Tab and the Work Order Other Tab may be used to charge equipment Assets to a particular direct or overhead Job. If the Work Order Other tab is used, the Accounting Period’s WO Other to GL field must be flagged.

New Reports:

Asset Profitability (RASSTPRFTBLY.rpt): This report compares Earned Revenue with Overhead Costs for the time period the user selects to calculate the Asset Profitability and Asset Cost/Hour for each Asset on the report, as well as a report total profitability. See user note 1.1.21 for details.

Asset Usage (RASSTUSGE.rpt): This report provides Overhead and Distributed usage for the time period the user selects. See user note 1.1.22 for details.

Important Fields – Upper Section:

Main Tab:

Asset Id:
Uniquely defines this company Asset (Truck001, Backhoe003, Computer010).

Asset Type Name:
Briefly describes this Asset - not required but strongly recommended.

Asset Type Id:
Select an appropriate Asset Type for this record.

Manufacturer:  Manufacturer Model: Model Year:
These informational fields are recommended but not required.

Serial Number:
The manufacturer's serial number.

License Number:
This field would typically be used to record the current license plate number of a vehicle. If your firm operates in multiple states, you may wish to include the state designation in this field (e.g., OH RHI-3234).

Asset Type: Owned Leased Other
Select the appropriate Type for this Asset depending upon whether it is Owned or Leased by your firm.

Warranty Info:
This field may be used to brief describe the warranty coverage on this asset.

Inactive?
If this box is checked, this item will be considered Inactive. It should be flagged if this Asset is sold or decommissioned so that it will not appear on the active Assets list.

Asset User 1 2 3 4 5
These optional fields may be used for entering any information your company wishes to retain or use for custom reporting purposes.

Costing Tab

Chargeable:
This field should be flagged if this Asset is chargeable to direct or overhead Jobs.

Default Overhead:
Job Id: Cost Code: Bill Item:
Enter the default Overhead Job that is used to collect the costs associated with owning and operating this asset (oil change, replace belts, etc.).

Operating Other Rate Id:
Idle Other Rate Id:
If this Asset is chargeable, select the appropriate Other Rates to be using for Operating and Idle time. The Operating rate will provide the default Other Rate for this Asset in the Job Journal Co. Equipment Tab.

Misc Tab

Purchase From: Date Purchased: Purchase Value:
These fields may be used to record the acquisition information for this Asset for reporting purposes.

Sold To: Date Sold: Proceeds:
These fields may be used to record the sales/de-acquisition information for this Asset for reporting purposes.

Residual Value:
Expected value when fully depreciated.

Important Fields – Lower Section:

Maintenance Tab

The Maintenance Tab is used to define the Preventive Maintenances that should be performed on your equipment Assets. The entries made in these tables may be used for informational and reporting purposes.

PM Type:
Select the type of maintenance to be performed. Double-click to select from a list of Asset PM Types. One line should be entered for each type of maintenance this Asset requires.

Interval: Interval U-M:
These fields enable you to specify the interval between maintenances, such as 1000 Miles or 300 Hours.

Current Reading: Current Date:
Typically, these readings would be taken on a regular basis and updated in this tab. The Reading should be recorded using the same unit of measure as specified above for the interval.

% Used:
This field indicates the percentage of the maintenance interval that has been used up since that last PM was completed. If this value exceeds 100%, the PM is overdue.

Example: Maintenance Overdue

Interval: 1000 Current Reading: 1550 Last PM Read: 425

In this case, the percent used is 112%. This calculated by the system as follows:

((Current Reading – Last PM Read) / Interval) * 100 = ((1550 – 425) / 1000) * 100 = 112%

Last PM Read: Last PM Date: Last PM By:
These fields should be updated when the PM is actually preformed.

Click this button to view additional fields.

Reading Type:
Typically, this would be used to record whether the Current Reading was an Actual, Estimate or Remote reading.

Flag Within:
This field is available for reporting purposes to identify how close a asset should be to completing its maintenance interval before it is flagged for maintenance.

Service Parts Id: Service Tasks Id:
Reserved for future use.

Expenses Tab

This tab may be used to record expenses of this Asset for user reporting and informational purposes only. The Job Journal must be used to associate costs with a particular direct or overhead job.

Start Date: End Date:
The day range during which these expenses occurred.

Amt/Period:
The amount of expenses incurred during the period defined by date range.

Asset Expense Type:
This field may be used for informational / reporting purposes.

Description:
A brief description of the expense.

Usage Tab

This tab displays the usage of this Asset from Job History. The Company Equipment tab of the Job Journal must be used to charge Assets to direct or overhead Jobs.

The following fields will be displayed:

Date – Quantity – U-M – OtherRate – Unit Cost – Unit Price

Job – CostCode – BillItem – WorkOrder – CostCategory – Invoice Id


19.5 Job Journal: New CoEquip Tab

A new child tab, CoEquip, has been added to the Job Journal to enable the user to charge assets to a Job or Work Order.

Asset Id:
Enter the company equipment Asset Id you wish to charge to a Job / Work Order. The Other Rate Id (and the associated Cost and Revenue fields) will default from the Asset record’s Operating Other Rate field.

Quantity: Qty Billed:
The quantity (hours, days, mileage) charged for this equipment. The Actual (Used) and Billable Quantities may be specified separately. The Quantity Used will be used for costing, and the Quantity Billed will be used to compute revenue for billing purposes. Note that the Quantity Billed field defaults when you enter the Quantity Used, but may be adjusted by the user if needed.

Period: Effective Date:
These fields from the corresponding fields in the Main tab when you tab out of the Quantity field, but may be changed by the user if needed.

Job Id:
The Id of the Job this line is being entered against. If this is a Service Compute job, the WO Id should be entered first.

Job Cost Code Id: Job Billing Item Id:
Enter the appropriate Id's for this Job or double-click to select from a list.

Cost Category:
The field defaults from the Asset record. Only Cost Categories with a Select Posting Type of Equipment may be selected. This field is required.

WO Id:
If this line is to be applied to a specific Work Order, enter its Id (or double-click to select from a list). If this is a Service Compute job, the WO Id must be entered.

Equipment Id:
If the user enters a Work Order Id, the system will default in the first piece of equipment on the Work Order’s Equipment tab UNLESS this behavior is disabled via registry.

Unit Cost: Extended Cost:
If needed, enter the costing information into one of these fields. The system will calculate the other.

Revenue Rate: Extended Revenue:
The system calculates the Extended Revenue based on the Revenue Rate, Billing Rate Type, and Quantity.

Other Rate Id:
This field defaults from the Asset record Operating Other Rate field. The Other Rate selected must have the GL Credit field completed. If this entry is being made to log Idle time, click the Magnify button and select the Idle option.

Extra?
If this entry is for an "extra" (not explicitly included in a contract), check this box (by double-clicking or pressing the Spacebar). Doing so flags this item as eligible for invoicing as a contract extra.

Click this button to view additional fields.

o Operating o Idle
This field controls whether the Operating Other Rate or Idle Other rate will default from the asset record.

GL Info:
GL Account Id:
This field defaults from the Cost Category’s Expense Account field but may be change by the user.

GL Credit
GL Account Id: GL Entity Id:
These display-only fields default from the Other Rate record.

19.6 Work Order Other to GL (including the expensing of Assets)

19.6.1 Accounting Period

New Field: Work Order Other to GL:
In previous releases, the GL was never impacted from Work Order Other tab entries. In this release, the Work Order Other tab will write to GL if this field is flagged.

Note: the sys-viewer-vwrkordr registry option RestrictWOOthercost should NOT be set to true if this option is enabled.

19.6.2 Other Rate

Changed Field: GL Credit Account:
If you will be interfacing WO Other to GL, this field should be completed if the Other Rate will be entered on the WO Other Tab. Note that this functionality may be used in conjunction with the expense of Assets on the Work Order Other tab and Job Journal Co. Equipment viewer.

This field also provides the default GL Credit on the Job Journal’s CoEquip Tab which enables chargeable Assets to be charged to a Job or Work Order.

19.6.3 Cost Category

Changed Field: GL Expense Account
This field also provides the default GL Debit Account for Work Order Other lines if the Accounting Period option Work Order Other to GL is flagged.

19.6.4 Work Order Other Tab

New Fields (click the Magnify button to view):

Asset Id:
Enter the appropriate company equipment Asset Id if you wish to charge it to this Work Order. The Other Rate Id (and the associated Cost and Revenue fields) will default from the Asset record’s Operating Other Rate field. An Asset must be flagged as Chargeable to be entered in this fields.

o Operating o Idle
This field controls whether the Operating Other Rate or Idle Other rate will default from the asset record.

Posted toGLH:
The system will flag this display-only field when a WO Other line is posted to GL.

Period Id:
This field will be completed by the system using the default Accounting Period; however, it will only be used to write to GL History if the Accounting Period has the WO Other to GL option flagged.

GL Debit Id:
This field will default from the Job Cost Category GL Expense field and should reference a Cost of Sales account. However, it will ONLY be used to write to GL History If the selected Accounting Period has the WO Other to GL option flagged

GL Credit Id:
This field will default from the Other Rate’s GL Credit Account. However, it will ONLY be used to write to GL History If the selected Accounting Period has the WO Other to GL option flagged.

20. SubAnywhere

In this release, the Work Performed is always posted to the Work Order. Previously, Work Performed was not being posted if the Original Work Order Id was completed.

This release improves client side performance issues, quote editing, and negative number handling.

An existing sys-subanywhere registry setting disables collateral from SubAnywhere from attaching to the site. In this release, you may also disable collateral from attaching to the equipment by implementing the option detailed in user note 2.35.

21. IVR

The Logging Pane now updates and Success messages are returned.

This release corrects a problem where the IVR System was posting incorrect 'date logged' to work order log table when status changes were posted.

 

 

Recent Updates and Enhancements

7.3.498.097

COP Acknowledgement Report: This report now suppresses the estimated sales tax if the Site COP tab has the Tax Exempt box flagged.

CRM Anywhere: Previously, if the option disablecrmmanagequotes was set to true in the web-settings registry to remove the Manage Quotes page, the Quote table was also suppressed in the Site View page. In this release, the Quote table is also suppressed when this option is implemented in the registry tab of the Web Profile or Web User record.

Email: This release supports alternate email ports as well as support for secure servers (SSL). See user note 2.38 for the registry options needed to support one or both of these enhancements.

Inventory Receipts Journal: Corrects a problem where Use Tax was not correctly written to the Tax History table when items were received in this viewer.

Quote Master Approval Wizard: The work order registry option DenyChangesToQuoteMasterLines prevented Quote Master from writing to work orders in recent release. This problem has been corrected.

Revised Reports:

Report W2 Electronic File: The Audit Report option of Report W2 Electronic File (report RW2EF.rpt dated 2/21/2012) has been modified so that the totals row is offset so that larger payroll amounts do not overlap. In addition, a new registry option is REQUIRED for federal processing. See user note 1.1.15 for details.

Drill Down AP Aging: The updated report (DAPVAGEv73b033.rpt dated 2/28/2012) corrects a problem that only occurred if you ran this report with the Invoice Detail option set to Yes. Previously, this resulted in the associated drill-down displaying the incorrect Vendor Name; this has been corrected.

Recurring AP Journal

Corrects the calculation of the Recurring Lines Amount field based on the Quantity and Cost; previously, this calculation only supported Amounts under 100.00.

Release Recurring AP Journal: this function now supports the IgnoreCase3193 registry option to allow users to enter a bank account on the Recurring AP Journal Recurring Lines tab. Previously, the function did not evaluate this option, and the post failed if a bank account was found.

Service Management:

Log Form: Two rows in the same Log Form record may not contain identical Heading and Line contents; this release improves error handling of this situation. See user note 11.19 for details.

New Call (Original Screen):
When a user tabs out of the search text box in New Call 1, all fields except the Service Category are now cleared in preparation for selecting a new Site and Equipment..

The Log Form Id: field has been added to this screen. It defaults from the Equipment record, but may be changed by the user to select which log form id will be specified on the new work order. See user note 11.2.4 for important details on the v.cus file that may be required for this enhancement, as well as important notes on using metrics.

Work Order:
Corrects a sporadic Inventory History reversal handling issue when theInventory tab includes a combination of quoted and unquoted lines.

A TechFinder button has been added to the Technicians tab. When clicked, the TechFinder opens, with the work order's Zone and the Certification for the first piece of equipment on the Equipment tab passed to the TechFinder filters. When the user completes the TechFinder processing, the system returns the selected Technician Id, Date and Time to the Technician line.

The Metrics tab is now correctly updated when equipment is added, inserted or deleted from the Equipment tab, as well as when the Equipment Id is changed. See user note 11.1.15 for details.

Sub Anywhere: In this release, the Work Performed is always posted to the Work Order. Previously, Work Performed was not being posted if the Original Work Order Id was completed.

Tech Anywhere Post

Corrects issue with Labor Rate erroneously defaulting from the Employee record if the client’s customization includes reordering of the Labor Journal Hours tab. See case for details.

This release corrects a problem where the Work Order Updates from TechAnywhere caused a WO Tech RN change. Also improves email alert processing.

Corrects Tech Anywhere intermittent issue posting COD multiple times.

7.3.498.095

Revised Report: Service Invoice: Certain custom formats specify that the work requested / performed is suppressed. Previously, if these formats were included in a service compute run with (for example) FORMAT_11 formats, the suppression was not turned off for the FORMAT_11 work orders, resulting in the Work Requested not printing when it should. The service invoice (serviceinvoicev73b032.rpt) report dated 2/13/2011 corrects this problem at the work order and equipment levels.

Tech Anywhere

The posting of new work order messages can now handle the time scheduled of "00:00", a valid time format for midnight.

Fixed problem where work orders created from TechAnywhere would have initial status of "Pending" rather than "Unacknowledged".

Now properly posts flat rate items from TechAnywhere Android.

Inventory Stock Status Report: this enhancement uses a temp table to improve the performance of this report. See user note 2.37 for the registry option to implement.

New Call New Client (Flashlight) Screen: two new fields, Log Form Id: and Escalation Profile Id: have been added to the Equipment section of this screen so that the user can specify them when creating new equipment and generating a work order.

7.3.498.094a

New Call: Corrects a “Key is missing” error in the previous release that occurred when the user attempted to add a work order that had been created from a web log.

Work Order: This update concerns users recently upgraded from v7.1 or earlier. When the date on Other tab entries originally entered in an earlier version was changed, and then the work order was invoiced, the date for this invoice detail did not match the new date on the Other tab. This has been corrected.

TechAnywhere Post: This release reduces the amount of memory required to process TechAnywhere message data. Previously, memory spikes on large messages might cause out of memory errors.

COP Sales Tax Handling: The system now allows changes to Sales Tax Group in Client Orders. The Client Site COP Tax Exempt field in tax calculations is now included in COP Invoice calculations. If this box is flagged, sales tax will not be included on the COP Invoice.

7.3.498.093

Registry Entry for Start AP Payment Approved List: this registry entry may be used to control the order this list appears in, and to set the Next Pay Date into the future for additional purchase control. See user note 2.36 for details.

CRM Anywhere: The system now uses the registry for web-dir setting when displaying splice.gif and right.gif (previously they were hard coded hard coded to exist in \web directory).

Employee Check Tab: This release filters the Checks list to exclude rows where both the Payroll Period and Effective Date are empty.

PR Checks: The Payroll Period Start and End dates, and the Check Date, have been added to the Recap portion of the Payroll Check stubs.

Tech Anywhere: Inventory from TechAnywhere can be posted to the default accounting period, even if the effective date is outside of the period range. A registry entry is now available to adjust either the date or accounting period to keep them in sync.  See user note 2.9.2 for details.

Tech Anywhere: SAM Pro now verifies that a TechAnywhere message contains the following before posting: Date Scheduled, Time Scheduled, Technician Id, Site Id and Equipment Id. If any of these fields are missing, the message fails and sends an email alert.

WO Inventory (and other journals): This release implements enhanced journal validation logic to prevent sporadic posting reversals with inappropriate Transaction Ids. If this situation is about to occur, the erroneous reversal is suppressed AND an error is written to the error log noting the reversal suppression.

WO Inventory / IM History Alert: Due to the work in the above enhancement, a registry entry is now required to display this alert. See user note 2.4.7 for details.

7.3.498.091

AP Performance: This release includes performance enhancements to the View AP Date to Pay, Start AP Payment Approved List, and Start AP Payment Approved List PM functions.

AR Cash Receipts Journal: In the Enter Invoices screen; the Remove Invoice button now correctly removes the selected line, not the following one.

General Updates:

Logging In: This release includes updated Login and Load bitmaps for 2012.

Type-Ahead /Autosearch Enhancement: This release extends this functionality to any column that has been pre-sorted in ascending order by clicking its column header. See user note 1.2.13 for an example.

Job Journal Expenses Tab: The Extended Revenue now automatically defaults if the Billing Item is not Fixed Fee. For Billing Items that are flagged as Fixed Fee, Allow Extras, it is still necessary to flag the Extra box in order for the Extended Revenue field to default.

Payroll:

W2 Reporting: supports the formatting changes in the W3 form printed for 2011 taxes.

Report PR Export: Previously, this function attempted to consolidate multiple entries for the same date. In this release, these entries remain broken out as they should be.

Earnings and Deduction Groups: When a line is added to the Labor Journal or the Work Order Labor tab, the earnings and deductions groups for the default Pay Type now complete properly, and compute the pay and cost after all Technician defaults are loaded.

Revised Report W2 Electronic Files: In the revised report dated 1/17/2012, Position 174 on the RE line is now set to N for kind of employer by default - no additional registry options needed for most users. For details, see user note 1.1.15.

PM Workbench: Now handles Long Strings in Document Replacement for MS Office 2010.

Service Channel: improved support of message handling in New Call.

Work Order:

Closing Wizards: The Work Order Closing Call Script and Service Recommendation functions have been reinstated, correcting a problem in earlier versions of 7.3.

Validate Inventory tab vs. Inventory History: When the Save button is clicked, the system now compares the total cost and quantity of unquoted lines entered directly on the Inventory tab with the total cost and quantity posted to inventory history. If it matches, the Work Order is saved. If not, a TabHistoryMismatch alert box appears instead. The tab mismatch information is also written to the error log if the appropriate sys-alert-tabmismatchhistory registry is present. Contact support if this alert persists.

Invoicing Tab: This release corrects a spurious ‘Client is not a Template’ error that occurred when the user attempted to clear the Override Client field.

7.3.498.088

IVR: Logging Pane now updates and Success messages are returned.

7.3.498.087

Service Billing: This release allows zero dollar invoices with only costs (and no revenues/COD entries) to be billed to a template Client. In addition, the Service Worksheet processing no longer brings up the list of each WO/Job combination; this is reserved for Service Invoicing only.

PM Workbench: This enhancement allows Crystal Reports to pick up the specific Job ID that is currently active in PM Workbench. Crystal Report Functions added to the Reports tab of the PM Workbench do not require the user to enter in the Job ID if the report is job based. See user note 7.3.1 for details.

7.3.498.086

TechAnywhere: The security from the Work Order is correctly applied to Labor Journal, Purchase Order, Sales Journal, and new Site Equipment records during the TechAnywhere Post UNLESS the record is defined as global via registry.

Recurring AP Journal: Validation prevents the entry of negative amounts in the following fields: Recurring Amount, Quantity, Quantity Billable, Unit Cost, Amount, Revenue Rate, and Amount Revenue.

Job: This release corrects a display issue on the JC Summary tab: moving the mouse within this tab no longer results in buttons from the Main or Invoicing tabs showing through.

Windows Menu: Previously, SAM Pro’s Windows menu did not list the TechFinder window. In this release, a TechFinder entry is added to the Windows menu when a TechFinder window is opened, and removed when the window is closed.

7.3.498.085

Service Channel: this release ensures that the data from multiple ServiceChannel tracking #'s is separated into individual files for proper processing.

Service Billing: New validation ensures that template-type clients are only billed when the net invoice amount is exactly ZERO DOLLARS. The Service Worksheet SERVICEWORKSHEETv73b032.rpt dated 11/22/2011must be imported to support this functionality. See user note 5.9.2 for details.

Dispatch Board: This release extends the Unavailable Technician functionality to the Classic Board when the Change Orientation button is clicked. Unavailable Techs will now have their row header displayed with a red background.

Tech Anywhere: This release corrects a Tech Anywhere and Scheduled Event Manager Posting Conflict.

Physical Counting: This release corrects a problem in the List Physical Count report: the List Missing Items option and the First / Last Uncounted fields, now work properly.

Asset viewer: This release corrects a spurious ‘Job is a Template record’ message that previously occurred when the user attempted to clear the Default Overhead Job fields from the Costing tab.

Quote Master Wizard: The sys-viewer-vqte option ApprovalWizardDefaultTechStatus is used to set the default status in the Approval Wizard's Technician pane. In recent 7.3 releases, this option worked correctly UNLESS the technician was a subcontractor. In this release, the software has been corrected so that the ApprovalWizardDefaultTechStatus is also used for subcontractor technicians.

PM Workbench: The Progress tab now displays the Job Progress information correctly; in previous releases it was not displayed.

7.3.498.083

Email: This release adds a 'Date:' header line to email messages to support email servers that require it. An updated version of the XmlToPdf.jar file is included in the zip file for this release that also supports the Date header line for emails with .PDF attachments sent from SAM Pro.

Job Journal: This release corrects a sporadic error that resulted in the Job Journal posting incorrect reversals to GL history.

New Help Menu Option - SQL History: There may be times when your support representative needs to see the SQL generated by certain actions: the SQL History option has been added to the Help menu to enable this. See user note 1.2.12 for details.

SubAnywhere: In this release, you may disable collateral entered in SubAnywhere from attaching to the Work Order equipment by implementing the option detailed in user note 2.35.

7.3.498.082

Printer Selection: Previously, an error was generated when the user tried to print to certain unusable printers on SAM Pro’s printer list. In this release, unusable printers no longer appear on the list.

Start Create EOM Unvouchered AP GL Entries: In previous releases, this function skipped GEN lines from Credit PO’s but picked up Inventory lines. In this release, applicable Inventory and Gen lines on Credit PO’s lines will be processed.

Quote Master: In this release, the approval wizard sums the Subcontractor lines so that only one line for each Subcontractor will be written to the work order’s Tech tab, and the quote will post successfully.

Location viewer: this record now displays correctly if one or more inventory items on the Location Items tab have a quantity-on-hand of 100,000 or more.

Tech Unavailability: The following enhancements are enabled if the registry option IdentifyUnavailableTechs in sys-viewer-vdsptchbrd is set to true and time off has been entered on the Technician record’s Unavailable tab.

NewCall
If the Technician and Date scheduled are both entered, a Warning will appear saying the Tech is Unavailable when the New Call is saved.

TechFinder

Workorder Technician Tab
