Service Channel:

To prevent naming conflicts the Archive and Reject folders are included in the naming conflict resolution.

Better handling of bad data occasionally sent to us from ServiceChannel.

This release allows our ServiceChannel FMMS bridge to support multiple companies (ServiceChannel PIN's). See user note 13.2 for details.

7.3.498.078

Important Installation Note: The zip file for this release includes a file containing all bitmap definitions in the image (master~pushbuttons.obj) and an executable image (v.exe) stripped of all bitmaps. The bitmaps will be loaded at runtime from the master~pushbuttons.obj file and the SKIN1 directory (if bitmap skinning is in effect). Running this release requires the presence of the change.log, recover.log and master~pushbuttons.obj files in the same directory as the image (v.exe) file. This configuration should allow XP users to run without ‘non-continuable protection fault errors’.

Important Note on Colors: In order to fully support Bitmap Skinning, users’ computer display settings must be set to 24 or 32 bit color. If the Color Quality is set to 16 bit (Medium in XP, or High Color in Windows 7), the new bitmaps will appear with their standard, pale gray background, but the registry settable background and mouse over color changes will not appear. Setting the Color Quality to 24 or 32 bit should provide the full bitmap skinning functionality.

VM Memory: SAM Pro’s Smalltalk virtual memory has been expanded to 250MB from 150MB. This should better support the running of extremely long reports and the unfiltered display of large record viewers without encountering out of memory errors.

Viewers (General):

In this release, History record viewers will start at the Range screen to avoid the unnecessary load time need to display the entire list of entries. In previous releases, the registry entry sys-startscreen-filter was required to implement this functionality.

This release eliminates a sporadic problem where the Change Record message displayed twice when leaving a record without saving your changes.

This release corrects a problem where the wrong sidebar appeared when the Refresh button was clicked in the Client Site Equipment and Job Billing Item viewers

The error ‘Not enough storage is available to process this command. ( OS error 16r8 )’ may occur if the user’s systems do not support the bitmap cloning associated with the new skins. In this release, bitmap cloning is disabled when the 'sys-gui' registry not available, a Skin Id is not specified, and when logging in as the support user. Note that the User’s Registry Tab may be used to turn skinning off or on by user.

In previous releases, the mouse over box drawn around bitmaps was not always removed when the mouse was quickly run over a series of buttons. This problem has been corrected so that these “leftover” boxes no longer appear when the mouse has moved off of the button.

This release extends the ability to successfully create a named range to history viewers opened at the filter screen.

New / Enhanced Reports:

Asset Profitability (RASSTPRFTBLY.rpt): This report compares Earned Revenue with Overhead Costs for the time period the user selects to calculate the Asset Profitability and Asset Cost/Hour for each Asset on the report, as well as a report total profitability. See user note 1.1.21 for details.

Asset Usage (RASSTUSGE.rpt): This report provides Overhead and Distributed usage for the time period the user selects. See user note 1.1.22 for details.

Report Customer Statement: This report now supports auto-emailing in the Customer Statements report (RCUSTSTMNT.rpt) dated 8/30/2011 or later. See user note 1.1.23 for details on the registry settings needed to implement this enhancement.

AP Journal: In previous releases, the system erred when you added an entry with a single quote ' in the EFT/Credit Trx Id: field, but allowed the entry to be saved (but could not be deleted). In this release, the user is no longer allowed to enter the single quote in this field.

AR Sales Journal: Validation has been added to prevent the user from changing the Entry Type on an existing entry. By default, the Entry Type may only be changed in the Sale Journal is in ‘add’ mode. A registry entry (NOT recommended) overrides the above validation; see user note 2.13.

Client Site viewer – Sagequest: This release handles an error that occurred when the Sage Quest interface was on and the user loaded a client site record with the Site Latitude field is blank, and Work/Ship Street Address includes the @ character.

CRMAnywhere – Appointment Confirmation: This enhancement allows your customers to log on as a guest and confirm or reject an appointment work order for a service call. See user note 17.5 for details.

Inventory:

Inventory Item Stock Status viewer: This function now excludes non-inventory items. This release also corrects a display issue with the On Hand and Available quantities – these fields now correctly display.

Inventory Item Viewer: The Equipment Type Id has been added as a Range Field to the Filter Screen.

Physical Count Processing: Corrects ‘Batch Number Mis-Match’ error when importing entries from a previously exported .csv file.

Notes: If a user (not a notes administrator) accessed a private note created by someone else, and attempted to change it, the message “you cannot change the record because the change button is disabled” would appear and the user would be unable to exit SAM Pro correctly. In this release, the message appears, but the user is allowed to close the notes viewer.

Purchase Order: Previously, users could change existing PO’s from type Purchase to Credit (and vice versa). Validation has been added so that the PO Type may only be changed in Add mode. A registry entry (NOT recommended) is available to ignore this validation; see user note 2.33.

Quotes: Validation currently disallows changes to all scope lines (and the detail lines associated with the scope) unless the status is set to Open, forcing the user to first change the status to Open to make changes. A registry setting allows changes to Accepted options; see user note 2.3.4 for details.

Start Job Cost Allocation: Corrects the Start Job Cost Allocation ‘Key is missing’ error that occurred when attempting to enter the Start Date.

Work Order:

This release corrects a performance issue launching the Scheduled Event viewer from Work Order viewer’s Scheduled Event button.

If you double click on one of the lines on the Escalation parent tab, the applicable Scheduled Event record is now opened.

7.3.498.074

Graphical User Interface

Bitmap ‘Skinning’: this release supports a new and brighter look for SAM Pro via bitmap ‘skinning’ of the top and side button bars. See user note 1.2.10 for an example of the ‘skins’, and user note 2.32 for details on configuring your system to run with these new skins.

Lists: In previous versions, the highlight color for lists (including new call and the dispatch board) was a bright blue. In Version 7.3, the highlight was changed to a dark gray for better readability. In response to user comments, this highlight color has been changed back to blue.

Record Viewers:

Additional validations have been added to alert a user when they are in danger of exiting a record without saving it their changes. See user note 1.2.8 for details.

More efficient/quicker right-click open of viewers implemented.

When typing in a multiple line text box with only one line showing, pressing Enter once again adds a carriage return instead of moving the cursor to the next field.

Report Preview: This release corrects a spurious error in recent releases that occurred when moving the mouse over a report preview screen.

Revised Reports:

Report Quote Form (RQTEFRM.rpt): The following functionality has been added to the standard Quote Form dated 8/29/2011:

The Estimated Tax for Fixed Price Scopes will be displayed when the Print Estimated Tax box is flagged.

Supports the ability to expand the printing of Scope Of Services by adding Notes attached to the Quote record via the sidebar Notes button. To enable, the Notes Summary field must contain the Option Code. Up to 60 lines of 80 characters each are supported; text is automatically wrapped to the next line if needed.

Service Invoice (SERVICEINVOICEv73b032.rpt): The version of this report dated 8.29.2011 supports expanded Material, Other and Sub quantity fields of up to 99.999.99; previously, quantities were limited to 9,999.99.

AR Sales Journal: Corrects a sporadic problem using the Create Credit Memo Button for a COP posting where the line amounts did not total correctly.

CRMAnywhere: See user note 17.4 for a new registry entry to allow sorting of open work orders and service request lists if multiple sites are involved.

CSR Anywhere:

The Quote's Status and Status Category are now updated as needed when options are added.

The Quote’s Status and Status Category are now displayed on the Open/Manage Leads Page.

A Registry Option to Restrict Inactive Quotes from this page is detailed in user note 2.31.

Corrects error -141 that occurred when a technician user attempted to run reports from the CSR Reports menu.

Client Order: An Order may now be cancelled if a Pick Ticket has not yet been printed for any of its Items. Cancelling an order automatically reverses its backorders/allocations. See user note 15.2.2 for details.

Email (SMTP): The system now correctly handles the case of a message containing a line consisting solely of a period.

Job Costing

Prevailing Wages: When using the Prevailing Wage logic on a job, the job cost calculated for overtime was incorrect. This has been corrected in this release so that the job cost is no longer inflated.

Job Cost Code and Billing Item: The Job Id is now a required field in the Job Cost Code and Job Billing Item viewers.

PM Billing

See user note 2.8.11 for a global registry entry to provide default Income and Accrual GL Accounts if the corresponding fields on the Site PM Billing tab are blank or not specified in Master Contract.

Client Site PM Billing Tab Changed Field - GLJ Trx Id:
If multiple amortizations for the same accounting period have been made for the same job, only the most recent GLJ Transaction will be listed. If this is the case, the GLJ Transaction will be followed by an asterisk, indicating that multiple transactions exist.

Client Site PM Billing Tab Detail View: Changed Field Labels:
GL Income (was GL Credit Id): GL Accrual (was GL Debit Id):
These labels have been changed to better define their function.

Service Management

Material Requisition Wizard: Corrects a problem where the last line on the Work Order Required Resource tab was generated to a different po from the other lines - even though they were tagged for the same vendor and location.

Service Evaluation Wizard: The user will only be required to answer all unanswered questions when it is invoked on invoicing the work order. When the wizard pops up based on the registry setting or on closing, the answers are not required.

Dispatch Board: In recent releases, if the Classic board was resized, clicking in it would maximize it. The Classic board now retains the window size that you select.

Purchase Order New Field - Job Tax Status: This display-only field has been added to the Main tab. The value is derived from the Job / Work Order entered in the PO header.

Startme.exe: This release includes a new startme.exe file. When the first user (of a particular OS) accesses a version, the underscore version of the v.exe runtime will be generated with the user’s OS designation. If you have XP and Windows 7 users, you would expect to see two runtime images:

V_2011_9_16_12_13__18_[Microsoft_Windows_XP].exe and

V_2011_9_16_12_13__18_[Microsoft_Windows_7_Professional].exe

XP users will be directed to the XP runtime, and Windows 7 Professional users will be access the Windows 7 runtime.

7.3.498.069

Report Service PM Agreement Summary Report (RPMAGRMNT.rpt)  
New Option: Use Job Open Date? The revision dated 8/22/2011 includes this new option. Checking this box will restrict the report to only include history that is greater than or equal to the Job’s Date Open. Default is unchecked (the original way the report ran); all history would be included.

Service Invoicing: Corrects a problem when the Max Tax per Invoice protocol was implemented (SalesTaxMaxPerInvoice=true in sys-ffv-global-settings) where sales tax was assessed on Use Tax jobs.

IM History: This release corrects a system primitive error that only occurred if sys-startscreen-filter was set for IM History and he/she attempted to create or select a named range.

Work Order Service Evaluation: A new enhancement allows the inclusion of general questions in Service Evaluations. Only unanswered questions (where the answer is set to unknown) will appear on the Wizard. See section 11.18 for details on these enhancements and changes to default behavior.

New Call: When you use New Call to create a Work Order from a Web Log, the Web Log's change entry is now updated with the Date, Time, and User Id and the description WOFromNewCall .

Quote Registry Option – Flat Rate Import Tax Rules: By default, the Flat Rate Import code forces each line's Tax Type Id to 'n/a' instead of applying normal SAMPRO tax rules. The registry setting detailed in user note 2.3.3 may be used to use the Job’s tax rules when setting the Tax Type.

Client Collection Notes: This release corrects a problem where Collection Notes were not deleted properly if the user exited from SAM Pro immediately after deleting this type of note.

Registry Entry for Job Costing Fringe Burden: This new option brings the Job History computation in line with the computation used in the GL History. This is important if your firm is not using Data-Basics Payroll module, but still desires to job cost estimated fringes and also accrue these to the general ledger. See user note 2.8.10 for details.

Start Purge Message Table

Important Note: The correct registry Id for this function is sys-start-sprgemssge (was previously documented as sys-start- sprgemssgetble).

This release: adds a commit at the end of processing; corrects a Sybase (-157 error); and implements a progress meter.

PM Workbench:

A new registry option may be used to hide employee labor cost on the Cost Sources Tab. See the Registry section of user note 7.2 for details.

A new field, Document Description, has been added to the input windows that appear when you click the New RFI, New Transmittal, New Submittal and New RFQ buttons. The contents of this field is written to the corresponding field in the Document record created for your RFI, Transmittal, Submittal or RFQ file.

A new field, Document Description, has been added to the quick edit windows that appear when you right-click an item listed on the RFI, Transmittal, Submittal and RFQ tabs. This field will be used to update the corresponding field in the Document record created for your RFI, Transmittal, Submittal or RFQ file.

Document Viewer: The user is no longer permitted to edit the Document Category for RFI, Transmittal, Submittal and RFQ documents. The Document Description may be edited if needed.

TechAnywhere:

The sys-ffv-global-settings registry includes an option, BranchSequence = nextwo, that enables a branch prefix to be prepended to the Work Order Id. TechAnywhere now checks to see if it should use a branch prefix and use it when posting NewWOs message.

Previously, if the sys-techanywhere registry option AutoPostCOD was set to false, the system created a one-sided GL History entry. This has been corrected, and an invoice master record (with the status set to New) is no longer generated if this registry option is implemented.

In previous releases, all TechAnywhere attachments came in with the Web Viewable CRM, Web Viewable CSR, and Web Viewable Tech flags checked. For signatures captured in TechAnywhere, all 3 are now cleared.

T5018 Forms: The prompt to print the summary page of this form has been eliminated: it is the end-user’s responsibility to transfer the necessary values to the summary form manually.

Purchase Controls: New fields added to the Vendor, Insurance, Purchase Order, and User records allows dollar limits to be placed on release purchase orders created by specific users, a PO Limit per Work Order, and the ability to block the release of PO for Vendors with expired Insurance. See User note 3.10 for details.

Vendor Viewer: Two new tabs, Defaults and User Fields, have been added to the parent select of the Vendor viewer. Several existing fields from the Main and Contacts tabs have been moved the Defaults tab for better organization.

CSRAnywhere: The Description field on the Manage Open Leads/Quotes Options page has been repositioned as the last data-entry field on the page. This will prevent its being overwritten when the user enters the Unit Cost or Other Rate Id when tabbing through the fields.

Viewers:

Corrects a problem in previous releases where the Add record button was not grayed out when a new record was added.

This release corrects a spurious invalid id error that occurred when an Id of the maximum field size is typed in and the user presses the Enter key to advance to the next field.

The Delete button no longer appears on sidebar of simple record forms (e.g., Account Manager) that have no child tabs. Like other forms, the user is now forced to delete records from the menu.

This release corrects a Field Size error that only occurred if the user saved a record while a push button on one of the child lines in the record was in mouse over mode.

7.3.498.065

Custom Index: The Custom Index Id field has been expanded to 50 characters.

Client Site Equipment Id: An additional 10 Client Site Equipment User fields have been added to the User Fields tab, for a total of 20.

Database Conversion: corrects error encountered when logging out after a database conversion.

Graphical User Interface:

In previous releases, if the user clicked on the extreme right-hand side of some buttons with short names (e.g., Go), the system did not recognize the click. In the release, clicking on any section of a button indicated with a mouse-over will ‘push’ the button.

Updated buttons that are easier to read on high-resolution monitors have been added to the following screens:

AP Journal: Main Tab

AR Cash Receipts Journal:

AR Sales Journal:

Clock: Increment/Decrement Minutes/Hours -

Calendar: Previous/Next Month -

Document:

Client Collection:

Client Collection Notes:

Job: Main Tab

Inventory Item: Pricing/Cost Tab

Inventory Physical Count

Inventory Restock

Quote: Main Tab

Work Order: Gross Margin Tab

Inventory Receipts Journal: If a Work Order is specified in the PO, the system now sets the client site equipment when creating IRJ general item entries.

Reports: This release corrects a System Primitive Failure error that occurred with saving some reports as .CSV files.

Service Channel: New Registry Entries for Multi-Company Use – see user notes 2.29 and 2.30.

Tech Finder: This release corrects an error that occurred when accessing TechFinder when the selected Work Order’s Service Zone had no Techs assigned to it.

7.3.497.060

General Fixes and Enhancements:

Screen Fonts: This release corrects a display issue that occurred if Windows Clear Text is enabled: field labels would display bolder when the screen was repainted after selecting an Id. In this version, SAM Pro handles Clear Text so that labels will be displayed correctly.

End Key: The End Key now positions the cursor correctly (at the end for the text) in Id-type fields when the Id Search/Lookup buttons are turned on. In multi-line textbox fields with word wrap, Ctrl-End now also works correctly if the text includes an embedded blank line, positioning the cursor at the end of all the lines of text.

Id Search Buttons: This functionality has been expanded to support disabled fields. If a field is disabled, the grayed out version of the Id Search button will be displayed, and the user will not be able to access the field by clicking on the button.

Virtual Memory Size in Help/About: In this image, the current virtual memory in megabytes (VM) is displayed in the About this Product window.

Invoicing:

Start Job Invoice Reverse: When reversing a service invoice, the user is now prompted with: "You are reversing and invoice related to Work Order <wrkordr_id). Would you like to set the Work Order Status to Invoice Ready?" If the user clicks yes, the system now changes any work order technician lines currently set to Billed to Invoice Ready and recalculates the Escalation Status (setting it to Invoice Ready unless other Tech lines override this setting). If the user clicks no, the system reverses the invoice but doesn't change the WO Escalation status / tech lines.

Service Invoicing: Corrects ‘Key is missing error’ when invoicing zero dollar COD invoices.

Purchasing/Inventory:

Purchase Order: Unless disabled by registry, the first Equipment Id from the referenced Work Order defaults in when you enter PO detail lines. Previously, this resulted in the first Equipment Id from the Work Order being reloaded if the user changed the Job Cost Code or Billing Item AFTER specifying a different Equipment Id. This has been corrected: the existing Equipment Id will not be changed when selecting a different Billing Item or Job Cost Code.

Start Inventory Item Cost Update: Corrects a problem where this function was not updating the Item’s Average Cost field (use for third-party reports) with the ‘calculated’ average cost that is displayed in the Inventory Item Viewer.

Inventory Receipts Journal: Corrects a problem with un-receiving items; see user note 8.6.1 for details.

Reports:

Report Quote Form (RQTEFRM.rpt): The quantity fields which show on the quote have been changed to only display 2 decimal places to be consistent with the labor detail lines (report dated 6/20/2011).

Drill-Down Client Profitability Report (DCPRTR.rpt and CCPRTR1.rpt): The Service Account Manager from the Client Site has been added to the Drilldown Client Profitability report as a range field. Both the DCPRTR.rpt (dated 6/10/2011) and the CCPRTR1.rpt (dated 6/13/2011) must be installed to support this functionality.

Service Management:

Dispatch Board: In this latest Power Board enhancement for Technician Unavailability (as specified on the Technician record Unavailable tab), the status line now displays the unavailable date range when the curse is positioned over the Tech’s summary line in the upper portion of the Power Board.

Dispatch Board: Minor cosmetic changes to the positioning of the top toolbar buttons.

Dispatch Classic Board: The Priority has been added as an editable field to the Work Order edit form that is accessible in the lower pane of the Classic board. 

Work Order Viewer

Main Tab: The WO Printer and Event buttons have been moved to the side button bar. The Ok To Invoice and Preview buttons have been moved to the Invoicing Tab.

Work Order Invoicing Tab: This release includes updated buttons for Ok to Invoice, Build Description, Print Worksheet, Print Invoice, Compute Taxes and Reset Tax Type. The existing Preview (Camera) button has been added to this screen.

IVR: Corrects problem where IVR System was posting incorrect 'date logged' to wrkordrlg table when status changes were posted.

Web Log Escalation: This enhancement allows escalation management to sense and trigger events based on web log changes (e.g, to Canceled or Duplicate), allowing the user to define escalation profile rules to send email notifications automatically. A new field, Previous Status, has been added to the Web Log to support this functionality.

7.3.497.058

General Viewer Fixes and Enhancements:

Top Button Bar: Some buttons have been re-arranged so that the Exit button is always the right-most button. The Alarm Board button has been moved the second row of the top button bar.

Side Button Bar: The Delete Record button no longer appears on the Side Button bar. To delete a record, the user may 1) Access the menu bar to select Record>>Delete Record or 2) Use the keyboard equivalent Ctrl+d to delete the record.

Id Search Buttons: This enhancement enables the addition of the Id Search Lookup button to the right-hand side of Id fields. This enhancement lets the user easily see which fields are Id fields, and also select the field AND bring up the list in a single click of the button. See user note 2.8.9 for details on enabling this option.

The Magnify button (used to zoom in on the Single/Detail view of lines) has been updated to help users distinguish between zooming in on a particular line, and searching for an Id (in the case of Id Search. In addition, the user need only single-click on the Magnify button instead of having to double-click it.

Child Tab Single View Enhancements: This release adds graphical buttons to the Single (detail) View of child tab lines that are accessed via the Magnify button. The following buttons enable the user to scroll though the lines in this child tab:

First – Previous – Next – Last line in the tab

Add, Insert and Delete lines buttons enable this functionality in the Single (detail) view line screens.

Clicking the Lines View button will return the tab to its initial, multiple line view.

StatusPane: This release includes updates to the text that is displayed in the status pane at the very bottom of the SAM Pro window when the user places the mouse cursor over a button. A registry entry is available to adjust the status line’s height, foreground color, background color and font. You may use the security option of this entry to help remind multiple security users how they are logged in. See user note 2.27 for details.

Menu Bar: A new pulldown menu labeled ‘Windows’ has been implemented.  It can be used as an additional tool to navigate within SAMPRO to currently open SAM Pro windows (for records, starter functions, and reports) by simply selecting an entry on the Windows list.

Zoom: This release corrects a display problem that occurred if you use Ctrl+Z (or the View menu option) to Zoom while in Single View, and then clicked the Lines View button. Note that user is not permitted to access Single View (with the Magnify button) while in Zoomed mode.

Wheel Mouse: Prevents “Key is missing” errors and other undesirable results if the user scrolls their Wheel Mouse while waiting for the Service Invoice (and other reports) to display.

Reporting:

Drilldown Reports: This release corrects a recent problem with drilldown reports which used hidden fields to pass values to component reports; the hidden field information was not being passed correctly. This fix is in SAM Pro, not the Drill Down reports themselves.

Launching External Apps/Crystal Reports: The system now uses the Windows Registry to find a path to Applications by Exe Name. This will enable users running 64 bit operating systems to use the new Crystal Viewer 2. Contact your support representative for details.

Document Management:

This enhancement allows the user to specify attachments to other tables in the record when attaching or scanning a new document from the viewer (functionality that Quick Attach already provides). See user note 2.26 for the registry option to do so.

AP and Purchasing:

AP Journal: Corrects a Key is Missing error that occurred when the user attempted to delete a Material Returns line from an existing Credit Memo.

Start AP Payment Approved List PM: This function matches the Vendor AP invoices for a job with the corresponding AR invoices for a job.  However, if the AP invoice had a blank job, it was matching it with AR invoices with blank jobs. In this release, the system restricts the amount collected in AR to history where the Job is specified.

AR:

AR Cash Receipts: Validations have been added to prevent the Client Id in AR Cash Receipts entries from being changed; see user note 5.8.1 for details.

Job Related:

Job & Job Billing Item: Revenues, Invoices and Purchases are not displayed if the Job is a Template or does not reference a Client Site. In this release, the messages that appear under these conditions have been made more specific (e.g., clicking the Revenues tab of a Template Job displays the message “Revenues data not available for Template Job”).

Closed Jobs and Purchase Orders: Validation has been added so that PO generation is not allowed if the current system date (today) exceeds the Job Closed date. This validation has been added to the following records: Job Record (Create PO button), Project Manager Viewer (Create PO button), Project Manager Workbench (Create PO button), Work Order (Create PO button and Material Requisitioning), Purchase Order (PO cannot be added if the header Job’s Date Closed is before the Release date).

PM Workbench: When using the New RFQ button, a ‘key is missing’ error occurred if the vendor contact entered on the input screen did not exist for the Vendor. This has been corrected.

Job Purchase Tab: In previous releases, a PO only displayed if the Job Id was completed in the header AND the PO had items. The following enhancements have been made to the current image:

If the PO has no items, it will display with “Purchase Not Itemized” in the Description field

PO’s will also be displayed if the header WO Id references the Job.

Payroll:

PR Check: This release adds support for the option to suppress PTO section on MICR printers when the Registry Id is GL Bank Account specific.

Quote Master:

Corrects an issue in recent releases where Notes attached to the Site were displayed when you clicked the Quote viewer’s Notes button: Notes attached to the Quote are now displayed.

This fix corrects a problem in recent 7.3 releases where blank lines in the Quote were not being deleted. Note that additional validation has been added so that the user is not allowed to blank the Option Code; a message is displayed advising the user to use the Delete Line button instead.

Revised Report Quote (RQTEFRM.rpt): The revision dated 3/29/2011 includes a new checkbox, Omit Declined Options that may be flagged to omit Declined scope options from the printed Quote and Quote total. See user note for a registry option to flag the Omit Declined Options box (default is for the box to be clear to preserve current behavior).

Revised Report Quote (RQTEFRM.rpt) and Quote Recap (RQTERCP.rpt): The revisions dated 4/22/2011 expand the Extended Price fields to support options of up to $9,999,999.99. Note that the Quote Total also supports this value.

Approval Wizard: The system now warns the user if the Technician line being generated is for the same date/technician combination that already exists in the Work Order. If the user chooses to continue, the existing Technician line (in the Work Order) will be replaced by the Wizard’s Tech line.

Blackberry Mirifex Post:

Corrects problem where Blackberry/Mirifex Posting was hanging due to Work Order's "open remote techs" warning message.

Service Management:

Work Order Quoted Labor Lines and Payroll: This release corrects the posting of WO-Labor to Job History when the Work Order is set to Invoice Ready so that employees are not paid for Quoted lines.

Work Order Other tab: Insert Line with Copy is once again enabled for all lines except the following: Insert-with-copy IS disabled when the line being copied references a closed Accounting Period that has the new WO-Other-to-GL option turned on.

New Call: The Client Site’s WO Other tab may be used to generate standard trip/truck charges to Work Orders created in New Call. Previously, the Sales Tax Group and Type for the Work Order Other lines generated in this fashion were derived from the Sales Tax Group on the Client Site COP tab. In this release, the system uses the Sale Tax Group in the Job record when generating the Work Order Other tab line.

Color Coding for Unavailable Techs: The Power and Classic Dispatch boards are now able to indicate that a Technician is unavailable by displaying his information in red. A registry entry is required to turn this functionality on (see user note 2.28). The Unavailable Days are set in a new tab in the Technician record (see user note 11.11.2).

Master Contract - Setup/Renew enhancements: see user note 11.14.1 for details.

Service Channel: extends the upload of Quotes to Scopes with a status of 'Printed'.

Tech Finder: Inconsistencies in the way Windows renders fonts resulted in the right and left-hand upper panes in TechFinder not always aligning perfectly. The new defaults work correctly if the user’s display is set to 100% font size; the registry options detailed in user note 2.22.1 may be used to correct the display for users running at 125% (Control Panel\All Control Panel Items\Display in Windows 7.)

Scheduled Events: In previous releases, if a user wished to manually take a scheduled event off hold, the user had the responsibility of manually replacing any tokens in the event. This release includes a new button, Fix Tokens that can be used to execute the token replacements when necessary. 

Web Log viewer: The Status field may once again be set by the user.

Start Archive Work Orders and Start Autoarchive Work Orders: These two functions are designed to allow high-volume customers to set older Work Orders to an Archived status. See user notes 11.16 and 11.17 for details.

Dispatch Power Board: The Client Site’s Shipping Street Address Line 2 has been added to the Dispatch Board. Note: the field will show up near the end of List. If you have customized your Dispatch Board columns, you must drag the field between to the desired location (e.g., between the first street address line and the city). If the column order of the Dispatch Board has not yet been customized, the new field will be positioned between the first street address line and the city.

Shop Order Pick List Entry:

Corrects reversing logic when a line is deleted so that the default date and accounting period are set correctly.

TechAnywhere:

Corrects a Droid issue with carriage returns.

In this release, the TechAnywhere event manager no longer attempts to re-post messages with the status of "PostedBy User". This allows clients to resume processing of posting other messages by restarting the TechAnywhere event manager.

TechAnywhere now supports COD payments when message payload contains multiple Workorders.

Fixes handling of Negative Values with a minus sign in first character. Also sets the price for Labor/Inventory and Other lines. The extra flag is set, the billing rate id to 'unit price'.

This release corrects the reference number written to the WO COD tab during the TechAnywhere post so that the Check Number (and not the Message Id) is displayed.

Web:

CSR Anywhere: assorted enhancements and fixes. See user notes 18.2 and 18.4 for details.

CRM Anywhere/CSRAnywhere: This enhancement may be enabled to improve the way the page headers in CRMAnywhere and CSRAnywhere are handled so that the span the entire screen. Modifications to your existing graphics will be needed to support the change. See user note 17.3 for details.

Sub Anywhere: Assorted fixes to improve client-side performance issues and correct errors.

SubAnywhere: Improves client side performance issues, quote editing, and negative number handling.

7.3.497.050

Blackberry/Mirifex: inactive equipment is not included in the list of equipment (and various info regarding the equipment) exported to the remote tech devise.

PR Check: A new registry setting will disable the display of PTO information on the PR check stubs – see user note 2.16.2 for details.

COP Invoice: When COP orders are invoiced, extraneous pricing lines (with only a GL Entity and a Revenue Type) are no longer written to the AR Sales Journal.

Work Order: In this build, the message “WARNING: this work order has open assignments to remote technicians” has been temporarily removed.

Required Resources Wizard: When this Wizard is invoked, the system now defaults the Location from the Work Order header.  This Location can be overridden by the user, but can never be blank.

PM Billing Changes:

Client Site PM Billing Tab: Validation now prevents the entry of both positive and negative contract amounts on the same line. The entry of negative amounts is denied on lines flagged as 'renewable'.

Work Order Viewer: When the Work Type is 'PM Invoice', changes (including line inserts and deletes) are not allowed on the Revenue Adjustments tab. See user note 2.4.6 for a registry entry to restore the previous behavior (to allow changes).

Reverse Job Invoice: The default behavior is now to deny PM Invoice reversal and instead generate a negative dollar invoice via Create PM Billing (see user note 7.9.1 for details). A registry option (see user note 2.24) for a registry setting to allow PM Invoices to be reversed

Scheduled Event Manager
A registry setting is now available that, when implanted, will check for Pending events which have tokens which have not been replaced; see user note 2.23 for details.

7.3.497.049

Registry: When a Registry record containing an option that is flagged as Multiple Settings (e.g., some sys-printer-W2 records) is loaded into the viewer, the option will be ‘exploded’ so that each setting now as its own Setting Key/Setting Value line. Disabled lines are excluded from this enhancement.

AP Journal List: In this enhancement, the AP Journal Entry Type (Purchase or Credit Memo) has been added as a column to all of the list options for this viewer.

Work Order: When processing Required Resource Inventory, the Import Cost Wizard now skips truck stock that has already been entered on the Work Order Inventory tab.

Quote Viewer: Corrects a problem with Field Auditing.

7.3.497.048

Revised Report PR Local Tax Report – RPRTAXL.rpt (3/4/2011): Corrects a ‘Table #lcltx not found’ error’ when run for a tax authority with no activity for the given time period. In the 3/4/2011 revision, if no activity is found, the report is displayed with the header only and no data.

Remote Time Entry: A new version of the Remote Time Entry executable (time_expense_viewer.exe), dated 2/11/2011, supports the printing of reports under newer OS such as Windows 7. Contact Support if this updated file is needed.

Purchase Order: the user is now prevented from setting the PO Date Closed prior to the PO's creation date.

Tech Finder: This enhancement enables the user to set up to 5 work order hour cut offs and associated colors for use in the Tech Finder assigned hours section; see user note 2.22 for details. .

Remote Tech: Corrects problem with Blackberry uploads including a Resolution code.

Service Channel: When the Upload to Service Channel button is pushed in the Quote Viewer, a confirming message ('This Quote has been queued for uploading to ServiceChannel') is displayed. Also corrects issue with the Proposal Upload.

CSR Anywhere: The Quote page now displays the Site’s work/shipping address instead of the obsolete mailing address.

7.3.497.047

W2 Printing: new W-2 Category fields have been added to the Tax Table and Tax Authority records: these fields supersede the use of the User 1 field for the handling of box 12 and 14 codes and titles for unemployment insurance. The User 1 field is still supported if the new fields are blank. 

Work Order Other Tab - Other Rate Filter: Implementing this registry option filters the Other Rates displayed on the list view to those referenced in the Job’s Rate Schedule; see user note 2.4.5.

Client Site PM Billing Tab: a new field, Work Order Id, has been added to the detail view (accessed with the Magnify button) of these lines. If a PM Invoice Work Order was generated to bill this line, its Id will be displayed in this field.

Service Channel: internal fixes to databridge, corrects client site equipment auto-loading issue in New Call impacting ServiceChannel.

Fill Back Orders: corrects sporadic problem handling negative quantities.

Quote Master: If the Job Id is selected manually, the system now defaults in the Report Id, Quote Notes and Small Print from Job's Site, and the Branch Id will be set from the Job (if completed in the Job record) or from the Job’s Site (if the Branch is blank in the Job but completed in the Site).

Child Tab Detail / Single View Enhancements: this enhancement allows the user to move from line to line without accessing the line view, and to Add, Insert and Delete lines; see user note 1.2.1 for details.

Child Lines – Odd / Even Color: Child tab lines are now displayed using the Odd / Even color scheme selected by the user with the Set Color button. The selected line will be displayed in the Background color selected by the user with the Set Color button.

Compute PR (Canadian PR Issues): This release corrects the application of CPP, EI and PPIP credits; eliminate excessive use of rounding, and implements use of standard tax credit.

7.3.497.046

Revised Report AR Aging (DARAGE.rpt): This drill-down report has been revised as of 3/9/2011 to better handle unapplied cash receipts.

Inventory Restock: In previous releases, the system deleted closed Inventory Restock transactions. This resulted in a lack of an appropriate audit trial. The default in this release is to not delete restock records when they are closed; see user note 8.7 for details and a registry entry to restore the previous behavior.

Tech Anywhere: If the previous payroll period was still flagged as the default, and payroll had already been run for it, TechAnywhere had an issue posting labor for the current payroll period. This has been corrected.

Tech Material Pickup (Start Workorder Material Pickup): The ‘To’ location is now a required field.

7.3.497.045

Create PM WOs: A new Job Id Range Filter has been added to Start Create PM WOs function. This enables the user to limit this functions to a specific Job or Jobs. This filtering impacts lines entered directly on the Client Site Equipment PM Schedule tab, as well as lines that will be generated from Master Contract.

Create PM Billings: A new Job Id Range Filter has been added to enable the user to limit this function to a specific Job or Jobs. This filtering impacts lines entered directly on the Client Site PM Billing tab as well as lines that will be generated from Master Contract.

Recurring GL Journal: Recurring GL Journal entries are inactivated by setting the Last Effective Date to earlier than today. This enhancement adds a Last Effective Date range filter to the viewer list. This filter is preset to exclude entries with a Last Effective Date less than the current system date (today) from the active list.

PM Work Orders: A new registry option will disable the posting of job history of budget cost and budget revenue for Preventive Maintenance work orders where the work order lines are marked QU. See user note 2.4.4 for details.

Service Channel: The Quote upload was only uploading Scopes with a status of 'Open': this has extended to include Scopes with a status of 'Printed'.

Inventory Item: Corrects the Inventory Serial Tab 'openLabTestResults' Not Understood error when double-clicking on a line. The Serial/Lot Master is now correctly displayed.

Dispatch Board: The Client Site’s Shipping Street Address Line 2 has been added to the Dispatch Board. This field will show up near the end of the list if you have customized your Dispatch Board columns. You must drag the field to the desired location. If the column order of the Dispatch Board has not yet been customized, the new field will be positioned between the first street address line and the city.

Labor Journal: The Labor Journal now supports prevailing wage calculations on lines that are work order based. Previously, only Job-based lines were supported.

Location Viewer: The calculation used to display the Locations Items tab no longer includes the quantity bought to a Job in the On Hand column.

Work Order Other Tab: Corrects “Runtime error: Key is missing” when changing the Cost Code.

Mirifex: internal changes to support posting logic.

W2 Magnetic Media: The revised Report W2 Electronic File (RWEF.rpt), dated 3/1/2011, supports the new Box 12 functionality for Third Party Sick Pay. The Third Party Sick Pay flag in type RW records will be set if any PR History is found with a W2 Category of 12:J.

Revised Report: Drilldown AP Aging by Vendor (DAPVAGEv73b033.rpt): This release / report enhancement adds new temp table logic to resolve out of memory errors that some users experienced with large databases. This version of the report (dated 2/28/2011) should only be used with 7.3.493.033 and up.

7.3.497.044

Client Site: A new field, Invoice Description Extended, has been added to the Detail view of PM Billing tab to allow for a more detailed Invoice Description.  If completed, this field is written to the Invoice Description of Work Performed during the creation of PM Invoice-type work orders. Note that the older Invoice Description on the PM line is still written to the Revenue Adjustment line as in previous releases.

W2 Magnetic Media – Box 12 Support: This enhancement supports the inclusion the W2 Category fields in Deductions & Earnings records in the Report W2 Electronic File functionality. Previously, only 401k deductions were supported.

Revised Report: RW2EF.rpt: The revised Report W2 Electronic File, dated February 17, 2011, must be imported to support the new Box 12 functionality. This report is suitable for version 7.2 and up.

AP Journal: the registry option AttachCostsToARInvoiceForWO allows the user to attach vendor costs to AR Invoices when vouchering. In this release, attachment (whether manual or automatic) is no longer made to reversed AR Invoices.

SAMPRO: Previously, if an error occurred during startup of a Sampro service, the image was left running in the background using up RAM. The image is now successfully closed preventing this memory leak.

Service Channel: If the parts quantity is greater than one, the extended price is correctly included in the invoice total of the emailed invoice spreadsheet.

Dispatch Board: Corrects a problem that resulted in the Technician Id on the Classic Board’s WO Summary (the lower half of the board) being case sensitive.

Edit Daily WOs: When launched from the Dispatch Board, this function once again uses the statuses selected on that Dispatch Board.

PR Check: This release corrects a PR Check PTO Summary issue in recent images. Holiday hours (for example) were being incorrectly included in the PTO summary as negative hours.

Notes Viewer: This enhancement Implements a global registry setting that prevents non-administrator users from changing or deleting Notes records. See use note 2.8.8 for details.

Technician Viewer Remote Access Tab: Two new options of the Remote Device Type, Windows and Android, replace the old XP option. See user note 11.11.1 for details.

7.3.497.043

Client Site Equipment: A new field, Deny TA Access, has been added to the Main tab. An RAQ may be implemented to deny TechAnywhere users access to this equipment if the Deny TA Access box is checked. Note that a new v.cus is required in order to see the new field.

7.3.496.042

CPP Time Import: The CPP import now supports enhanced duplicate handling.  When processing the import file a message will come up at the end with ‘Import completed’ with errors and it will open a work area that will list the errors.  This work area can be saved or printed.  Once the errors have been corrected the user can re-run the import file.

CRM Anywhere: The sidebar graphic now correctly appears on the Print Quote page. The Quote now also supports the CRMReportType registry option of pdf; if this option is implemented, the Quote itself will be displayed in pdf format.

Quote Master Wizard: If the Client is on Credit Hold when a new work order is generated, the Tech Tab child lines are set as they should be for the type of technician they are assigned to, and the Work Order’s Escalation Status is set to Credit Hold and Credit Hold box is flagged. A Credit Manager must clear the Credit Hold box on the Work Order before it will appear on the Dispatch Board, or be released to a technician.

PR Miscellaneous Deduction Checks: Fixes to accommodate mixed Remittance Types of Deduction, Employee and Vendor.

Job Cloning: Previously, if the CloneJobEquipmentExistingSite registry was enabled, cloning the job resulted the existing site having its PM Billing lines changed to the newest job. In this release, the Site’s PM Billing Schedule is not changed as a result of the clone.

Client Site PM Billings: several enhancements, including the ability to enter negative bill/accrue amounts to correct errors. See user note 4.2.2 for details.

GL Journal: several enhancements to the GL Journal screen; see user note 6.3 for details.

Service Channel: The SAM Pro data is now always updated when an Invoice has been uploaded to Service Channel. The Invoice Date uploaded to Service Channel now includes the time using the format 'mm/dd/yyyy hh:mm' where the hh:mm represents the current time.

7.3.496.041

Quote Master: Selecting a Flat Rate has been wizardized. Additional forms have been added to the old Flat Rate import screen for Labor, Material and Inventory (based on the Flat Rate Category child tables) to allow the user to edit hours and quantities before the lines are imported into the Quote. These additional screens are accessed by clicking the Next button on the Flat Rate Wizard.

If the user simply wishes to import the flat rate without adjusting the hours or quantities, the Finish button may be clicked. Note that the Flat Rate’s Pretax Price (if specified) will be used to set the Fixed Price on the Quote Scope.

Canadian PR (Pay Type): The PTO Accrual Method field has been added to the Pay Type viewer to allow for specification of the PTO Accrual Method.  The Employee viewer has code that validates the use of the PTO amounts (hours or percent) relative to the Pay Type's Accrual Method. See user note 9.14.2 for details.

Start Generate Recurring Labor Journal: This release corrects an hours calculation error that occurred if the Cycle range was completed.

Sage Quest: When Work Orders were uploaded to SageQuest, they were previously sent using an hours format like “estimatedHours=2.5”. At SageQuest’s request, we now convert estimated hours from hours to seconds before we send it up to them.

Service Channel: The ServiceChannel invoice upload is now successfully gets the User Id and Password from the registry

Edit Daily Work Orders: If this function was not allowed in the User Groups and Functions table, a user could still access it via the Edit Daily WOs button on the Dispatch Board. This loophole has been closed.

W2s – Box 12: This release increases the size of Box 12 Code Fields from 1 to 2 characters. These codes are specified in the W-2 Category fields of the Deduction and Earning viewers. This enhancement was specifically added to support the after tax contributions to Roth retirement plans which requires codes AA or BB.

7.3.495.040

Shop Order: Corrects a sporadic problem where Fill Back Orders was posting to wrong Item. The Transfer Qty BO'd has been added to the BOM full screen view of the Shop Order. 

Shop Order (Transfer Ticket) Pick List Entry: Entering a non-zero value in the Qty Transferred field now forces the Transfer Done field to True: this field must be flagged for correct processing.

Registry: Corrects a problem where the registry option DisabledField for a child tab failed if the tab name (e.g., childPTO in the employee viewer) is capitalized.

Quotemaster: Previously, if an Accounting Period was not flagged as Default, the posting of PO's from the Quotemaster Wizard failed. The following enhancement (when generated PO’s):

1. Uses the default Accounting Period (if it exists),
2. If no default exists, it uses the 'first' active accounting period with today's date in the date range. 
3. If both of the above fail, the Wizard warns the user, and the PO post fails as in previous releases.

Deductions Viewer – Support for Third Party Sick Pay: this enhancement supports coding for third-party sick pay. If the W-2 Category field is set to 12:J, anytime an amount is found for Box 12 Code J, the system will mark the Box 13 check box labeled Third-party Sick Pay on the W2.

WO List Report: When the Print Notes option is selected, Secure Notes (generated by the Audit Changes registry option) are now excluded from the report.

Recurring AP Journal: Corrects problem where user could not enter the GL Account on the Recurring Lines if the Payment Type was set to Check.

Viewers (general):

This release corrects the horizontal placement of bitmaps in the top button bar.

The user will now be notified if an attempt to create a duplicate entry fails. For example, a technician cannot be scheduled on the same date and work order more than once. Previously, the duplicate line would not be added, but the user was not notified.

SQL Server Database Conversion: implements incremental commits when creating Foreign Keys and Indexes during conversion.

Printer List: Users with a very large number of printers may have found some missing from SAM Pro’s list of printers because the allowable number of characters for all the printers’ names was exceeded. The allowable number of characters has been expanded from 6000 to 10,000 characters to correct this problem.

7.3.495.039

Registries to Set Parent and Child Tab Fonts: this enhancement enables the user to adjust the Fonts used for the Parent and Child tab labels in SAM Pro viewers. In particular, a ‘skinnier’ or smaller font may be specified to enable users with lower screen resolutions to see all the tabs on the Work Order and other viewers with MANY tabs. See user notes 2.18 and 2.19

Registry to Set Title Font: Previously, the registry used to specify the font for labeling titles and lists was restricted to a 10 point fixed width font. This restriction is no longer required; see user note 2.20.

Purchase Order: Credit PO's (both vouchered and not yet vouchered) can now be un-received (previously, only vouchered Credit PO’s could be un-received).

AP Journal: when attempting to delete a journal entry, the system now checks the status of the Accounting Period earlier in the process. This prevents inappropriate changes to the Check records of manual checks and credit card transactions associated with AP Journal entries for inactive accounting periods.

Box 14 - W2s: In previous releases, users could implement SDI (Box 14 on form W-2) by setting the User 1 field in the applicable Tax Authority to SDI.

In this release, the system now uses the Tax Table to handle unemployment insurance, disability, etc. more generically. The Tax Table User1 fields now may be used to specify the titles for unemployment, insurance, disability, etc. Only the Box 14 description should be entered, i.e. FLI,TDI or SUI in the User1 field.

Quote Master Flat Rate Wizard: Selecting a Flat Rate has been wizardized. Additional forms have been added to the Flat Rate import for Labor, Material and Inventory to allow the user to edit hours and quantities before the lines are imported into the Quote. See user note 10.3 for details.

Quote Master Approval Wizard: this release corrects a problem that occurred if the user immediately logged out of SAM Pro after the Approval Wizard was run: a new Work Order was created, and nothing else (no PO, no update to the Quote).  Also in this release, new Work Orders generated by Quote Master will have their Description field set to 'Quote: #####'.

Magnify Button: In some instances, the switch from the lines view to the detail view generated an error that appeared to be data related but was really a timing problem. This has been corrected.

7.3.495.038

Create PDF button: supports use with archived documents tagged as ‘Read Only’.

AR Sales Journal: now denies changes to the Invoice Id for previously posted AR Sales entries. 

Dispatch Board: corrects display issue on the Dispatch Board's top toolbar

Fill Backorders: Corrects problem with partially filled shop backorders.

Recurring Labor Journal: Corrects problem where Labor Journal Entries were not generated by the Start Generate Recurring Labor Entries function.

Work Order Labor Tab (customizations with Start / End Times):

If user enters the Hours first, and then sets the Start End times (resulting in the Hours changing), the Revenue Amount is now updated correctly.

The Start/End times from the Labor Journal (if included in the customization) are now used to update the Work Order Labor tab when labor is imported to the Work Order via Import Costs.

Document Management: Corrects obscure issue when emailing file attachment as part of a Scheduled Event.

Quote Master: If the Job Id is specified in the Quote header, the Job’s Material Price Level is now used for default pricing on the inventory tab, overriding the Client Site Material Price previous used by default. If the Job Id is not completed, the system will continue to use the Site’s Material Price Level.

7.3.495.037

Notification Category: A new field, Obsolete, has been added to this record. See user note 11.9 for details on using this field.

Escalation Profile: A new field, Obsolete, has been added to this record. See user note 11.8 for details on using this field.

Worker’s Comp State – New Field: WC Gross from Prevailing Wages: Exclude Fringes
Workers comp 'wages' typically should not include any amounts related to prevailing wage fringes (entered in the Fringe Rate field of the Job’s Prevailing Wages tab).  This new behavior is activated by flagging the Exclude Fringes field in the appropriate Workers Comp State records.

Physical Count Processing: enhancement added to handle commas inserted in ‘blank’ line of .cvs file by Excel when importing a spreadsheet.

Invoice Master, Cost Code and Billing Item viewers: PM (Project Manager) filtering has been applied to these viewers. Note that in Start Reverse Job Invoice, only Invoices corresponding to the user’s PM Filter may be selected.

Quote Master Approval Wizard: If you cleared the flag from an Option Code in the QM Wizard, details pertaining to the unflagged options persisted in some of the following screens. This has been corrected.

7.3.494.036a

AR Sales Journal: Corrects problem that did not allow Job / Client fields to be entered directly for manual entries.

AR Sales Journal: Enhanced validation to deny changes to the Invoice Id for previously posted AR Sales entries and to insure that the specified Invoice Id must be appropriate for users’ security settings.

Revised Reports: Several reports should be updated for 2011 US Payroll Tax reporting. See user note ** for these import updates. See user note 1.1.15 for details on this important update.

Percentage of Wages Vacation Accrual: This enhancement implements vacations accruals with a 'percent of wages' option for Canadian Payroll scenarios and possibly for certain US setups. See user note 9.14 for details.

Printing and Emailing from Report Preview: This registry option may be implemented to ensure that reports that display the “Did this report print successfully” confirmation are, in fact, printed before they are allowed to be emailed. See user note 2.6.4 for details.

Compute Payroll: When implemented, a new registry option results in the employee's gross wages being reduced by the amount of any Section 125 deductions before applying the 401k deduction percentage. See user note 2.17 for details.

Client Site: In previous releases, the Client Site User 1 and 2 fields appeared on both the COP and User Field tabs. They are now only on the User Field tab as they should be.

7.3.495.035

Revised Reports:

Client Profitability Report (12/15/2010) – Version 7.0 and Up

This report (DCPFTR.rpt) now skips entries with Client Rn = 0. Note that its component reports (CCPFTR1.rpt, CCPFTR2.rpt & CCPFTR3.rpt) should be updated for Version 7.0 (these reports are dated 10/8/2009) or an error may occur with certain settings.

Unvouchered AP Summary Report (12/3/2010) – Version 7.0 and Up

This version of the Unvouchered AP Summary Report (RUNVCHRDAP3.rpt) corrects a typo in the GL Entity field.

Start Report Import: assorted enhancements; see user note 1.14.

Work Order: corrects display issue on TechAnywhere tab.

Job Journal: expenses posted to GL History now have the source journal correctly identified as Job Expense, not Job Labor.

Inventory Receipts Journal: The user is now required to specify an accounting period before changing any of the detail lines.

Dispatch Board: Corrects error that occurred in the Classic Board if you clicked the cell one past the last column and that row had a valid WO in the last column.

Start Client Site Import: This new function allows a user to import a pre-defined, comma separated ASCII file containing information needed to create new records and relationships between Clients, Sites, Site Equipment, Jobs, Cost Codes and Billing Items in the database. See user note 4.3 for details

7.3.493.034

AR Sales Journal: This release closes a loophole that allowed users to overwrite an existing Invoice Master record when crediting a Credit Memo without using the Credit Memo button.

Work Order Invoicing Tab – New Override Terms and Client Id fields: This enhancement allows the Client and/or the AR Terms code in the Work Order Header Job to be overridden when a ‘COD’ job has overages or receivables that must be billed an assigned to a Client. See user note 11.1.10 for details.

7.3.493.033

AP Journal: If a manual checked is entered, and then deleted, and the user elects to reuse check#, the system will now allow the number to be reused.

PR Check Printing: This release extends MICR check printing to handle multiple bank accounts / entities: see user note 2.16 for details.

7.3.493.032

Canadian T4 Forms: Box 24 will now be blank if it is the same as Box 14.
Box 26 will now be forced to blank.

Inventory Average Cost: A registry entry is now available to limit the average cost calculation to only those cases where inventory is actually on-hand at the location being queried. If there is no stock on-hand for the specified location / serial number, the cost will be zero. See user note 2.8.6 for details.

Physical Count Export / Import: This enhancement adds the Pick Sequence to the last field/column of the .csv file created when exporting the Physical Count List; this field is ignored on the import.

Work Order: If multiple inventory receipt journal entries are made for the same PO, the WO Purchases tab now displays the Job Quantity and Quantity Vouchered correctly.

Start AP Payment Approved PM List: when the new View Invoices button is clicked, all Vendor Invoices (typically scanned into the AP Journal or Quick Attached) on this list will be displayed..

Viewers (general): This release corrects sporadic problems where the screen would erroneously autoscroll when you clicked into a field (e.g., in the AP Journal, the upper pane would auto-scroll when you tabbed into the Account Period field under some screen resolutions).

Accounting Period: In version 7.3, we implemented the optional interface of WO Other to GL which is controlled by a check box in the Accounting Period record. The following registry detailed in user note 2.15 is designed to help manage the setting of this new field.

AR Cash Receipts Journal: Previously, changes were not allowed to entries referencing an inactive accounting period. In this release, changes (and applicable reversing entries) to receipts in inactive accounting periods will be written to the open accounting period and effective date that the user selects. Changes are not allowed if the receipt has been entered in the Bank Deposit Journal.

7.3.492.031

Logon History: internal updates.

7.3.492.030

Inventory Adjustment Journal: A new field, Transaction Type, implements validation logic that ensures that the data entry for Transfers is consistent with the selected Type.  See user note 8.1.

Work Order Import Costs Wizard: Corrects a sporadic timing problem.

7.3.490.029

Work Order Other to GL (including the expensing of Assets): Previously, the GL was never impacted from Work Order Other tab. In this release, the Work Order Other tab will write to GL if specified in the Accounting Period. See user note 19.6 for information on implementing this functionality.

Quote: Quote User fields 3-10 added to the Notes tab.

7.3.490.028

Job Prevailing Wages Tab: a new Fringe Rate field enables you to separate Fringes from the Base Rate for prevailing wages. See user note 7.1.2 for details.

Report PR Certified Payroll Report: this updated report references the new Certified PR Report Label field on the Job Prevailing Wages tab. See user note 1.1.12 for details.

Database Conversion: performance enhancement to SQL Server conversions where only a few table changes are needed.

Quote: This release adds enhanced validation so that the Quote's Client Site CANNOT be changed if any Scope or Equipment Tab lines have the Equipment Id completed. The software supports the ability to ‘clone’ an existing quote – see user note 10.1.5 for details

Start Work Order Entry: Validation now requires that only an active payroll period may be selected.

Inventory Item: The Purchases Tab was not displaying On Hand values correctly if a receipt was made on the base purchase order, the purchase order was made a change order, and then the remainder was received. This problem has been corrected.

Client Site: The Call Script Id field on the Main tab has been relabeled to reflect its function: WO Closing Call Script id.

Quote: The Inventory Item Id is now a required field on the Inventory Tab.

Custom Index: This enhancement enables DBAs or system administrators to store custom indexes within their data. The next time the database conversion is triggered (when updating to a new version), the SAM Pro software will automatically install all active Custom Indexes; see user note 1.11.

7.3.490.027

Specify Annual Standard Hours: the system now allows the default value of 2080 for the annual standard hours (for salaried employees) to be overridden by employee (see user note 9.12.1) or by registry (see user note 2.8.7).

Viewers: When the Refresh button was clicked, certain fields (such as the Work Order’s AR Term Code on the COD tab) were not reloaded from current data. All fields are now reloaded when Refresh is clicked.

Service Billing Worksheet (SERVICEWORKSTEET.rpt): This release corrects a problem with auto-saving service worksheets. The registry entry sys-report-serviceworksheet must include the registry option AutoSaveWhenPrinted. See user note 1.1.2 for details.

Start Message Table Purge/Archive: this new function allows the system to clean up the Message table (used by TechAnywhere, SaqeQuest, FMMS, etc.) and improve the performance of the Work Order TechAnywhere tab. See user note 1.12 for details.

Document Management: The Archive File Location and Type fields in the Document Record are now successfully completed during the scanning process.

ADP Payroll Import: This enhancement allows the import of files where the GL Entity field is blank.

AP Journal: A new field, Date Received may be used to record the date the Vendor Invoice was received by your company. See user note 3.7.1 for details.

7.3.489.026

AP & AR Sales Journals: In version 7.2.476.098, validations were added to the AR Sales Journal to prohibit the entry of AP Control accounts on Prices lines, and to the AP Journal to prohibit the entry of AR Control, AP Control & Bank accounts on GEN lines. Some users find that these validations conflict with their procedures: see user notes 2.12 and 2.13 for registry entries to disable these validations.

View Documents as PDF: When the showDocument button is pressed in view documents it now handles multiple pdf children and image children and displays as one large PDF.

Tech Anywhere: If the amount of data entered into the recommendation field by the tech surpasses the 1024 character limit, SAM Pro truncates the data so it will fit into a weblog and post the message.

Create PM WO: As of version 7.2.476.071, if the Work Code Id is different on two lines of the Client Site Equipment PM Schedule for the same day and technician, the system forces a separate work order to be created. Since some users prefer to have PM lines with multiple work codes appear on the same work order, a registry entry (see user note 2.11.3) now allows you to do so.

Preview Reports: This release corrects problems that occurred if the user clicked on the Preview Report option of the report range viewer and selected HTML or Text. A registry entry may be required for the HTML option to work properly; see use note 2.8.5 for details.

Labor Journal: Corrects the Hours tab so the Job Id field no longer overlaps the Job Cost Code.

Work Order Import Costs Wizard: A new field, Actual Used, has been added to the Inventory screen of the Wizard. See user note 11.1.7 for details on this field and how it should be used.

Quote Master: When entering a flat rate to a quote scope line, the scope of services in the quote scope line now always defaults from the corresponding field in the flat range category.

Create PDF Button: This release corrects a sporadic File Creation error when using the Create PDF button in the Documents viewer or the View Files button in Start AP Payment Approved List. A registry entry may be used to increase the maximum wait time; see user note 2.8.4.

Project Managers Workbench: Credit Memos now show in the AP Summary TAB and are eligible for double-click functionality (to display the Vendor Invoice) and right click (to PM approve for processing). Clicking the Pay Balance button correctly sets the PM Amount Approved to a negative value.
